Chapter 1175: Chapter 1174: The Thing in the Ice Box

"Huo Huashen from our sect leads more than twenty experts at the Nascent Soul Stage who are stationed in Muxue City. He might know the whereabouts of the Carefree Guest," said Mu Baiyi.

...

As the year drew to a close, the Martial Arts Hall announced a holiday break. Before the holiday, Old Lu and two other teachers decided to hold a parent-teacher meeting.

Firstly, it was to summarize the teaching achievements since they had become teachers.

Secondly, it was to have the parents encourage the students to not neglect their Fist skills during the holiday and to remember to practice.

Mr. Murong gladly agreed with the teachers’ ideas and even volunteered to decorate the Martial Arts Hall. The inside and outside of the hall were festively adorned with lights and decorations, creating a very festive atmosphere.

"Parents of Liu Yu, please come in, please come in."

The three teachers stood at the door, warmly welcoming the parents.

"This must be Old Lu. Our little Yu often mentions you, saying how much he likes your Fist teaching style."

"Zhige rarely praises anyone, but when he talks about you, he has nothing but compliments."

"Old Lu, Teacher Meng, Teacher Xue, please take extra care with these two children."

"Certainly, certainly, by the way, where is Zhige?" Lu Yang inquired. Zhige should be living at Liu Yu’s place, so why didn’t he come along?

Liu’s father sighed, "Zhige went out with Su Yuan. He said he would make it back in time for the parent meeting. The kids are grown now, and we can’t control them anymore."

Zhige and Su Yuan?

A flicker of doubt passed through Lu Yang’s mind. The two of them together probably meant it wasn’t as simple as just hanging out.

"Gong Che’s parents, please come inside."

Gong’s father enthusiastically shook Lu Yang’s hand.

"Old Lu, thank you so much. Little Che’s illness has finally healed. We are really grateful to you..."

Mid-sentence, Gong Che’s parents burst into tears, surprised that Gong Che’s coldness had truly vanished without a trace and that he had gained such a robust body.

"It’s nothing, just what I should do," Lu Yang tried to pull his hand free. He wasn’t very good at dealing with overly enthusiastic people.

Gong Che’s parents then turned to thank the gatekeeper, Mr. Huo.

"Just before the meeting, Little Che told us that he had encountered human traffickers, and it was you who scared the traffickers away. Thank you, thank you."

Huo Huashen remained solemn and stood up straight, "These are what I should do!"

Lu Yang continued to greet the parents: "Shi Yi... you have a large family, don’t you?"

Lu Yang saw that behind Shi Yi followed a large group of relatives, including Shi Yi’s parents, Shi Liehu, and Bing Wu, along with people from the Ice Flood Dragon Clan.

It was a massive procession, like sweeping through the streets.

The leader of the Ice Flood Dragon Clan came forward, grabbing Lu Yang’s hand, and burst into tears, "Old Lu, thank you for nurturing Shi Yi."

"I am Shi Yi’s god-grandfather. To be honest, we had high hopes for this child but didn’t know how to nurture him properly. Thanks to Old Lu for your expert guidance."

"I believe Shi Yi will definitely live up to Old Lu’s efforts and will quickly grow with the resources our clan provides!"

The Clan Leader of the Ice Flood Dragon Clan wanted to say more but was pushed aside by Bing Wu, who was in line to express her gratitude.

"Old Lu, thank you for helping our family reunite. You act low-key, Old Lu, and do not want others to know about your presence. Rest assured, I have not told anyone about your identity."

Shi Yi’s large family entered the Martial Arts Hall, and other children and parents gradually arrived, thanking the three teachers for their nurturing. Their children were now strong enough to kill a cow with one punch.

Inside the Martial Arts Hall, parents exchanged words, endlessly praising the three teachers while Mr. Murong, standing aside, couldn’t stop smiling.

"The parent-teacher meeting is about to start. Why haven’t Zhige and Su Yuan arrived yet?" Lu Yang muttered, wondering if the two boys might have run into trouble.

Just then, he saw Zhige and Su Yuan sprinting towards them.

To be precise, Zhige was carrying something unknown on his back and dragging Su Yuan along at an alarming speed.

Fearing that he would miss the parent-teacher meeting, Zhige didn’t bother to hide his true Cultivation Level.

"Hurry up and get in, we’re just waiting on you."

Lu Yang followed the two into the Martial Arts Hall, softly closing the big door, leaving Huo Huashen outside.

Lu Yang smiled warmly at the students and parents, cleared his throat, and spoke in a very gentle tone:

"Hello, everyone! First of all, please allow me to represent all the teachers of our class and express our sincerest gratitude to the parents who took time out of their busy schedules to attend today’s parent-teacher meeting."

"I have the privilege to teach this class by coincidence and by fate, and I believe Teacher Xue and Teacher Meng share the same sentiment."

"In the past period, students have made significant progress in all aspects. This could not have been achieved without each student’s hard work and the support and cooperation of all the parents."

"...With the New Year approaching, I hope students will not just indulge in eating, drinking, and playing, neglecting their martial arts."

"Then, see you all next year."

Lu Yang had the manner of a teacher and spoke methodically, bringing the meeting to a close amidst enthusiastic applause, with some students even being moved to tears.

Once the parent-teacher meeting disbanded, the three teachers gathered together. Meng Jingzhou laughed and punched Lu Yang lightly.

"That sounded quite convincing."

"You’re not wrong, staying in the Extreme Northern Lands is quite comfortable; it’s a great place for renouncing worldly desires."

Meng Jingzhou felt he had managed to calm Old Lu.

You see, before I arrived, look at what kind of life Old Lu was living, fighting the Four Great Demon Kings and battling the beast tide.

Since I arrived in the Extreme Northern Lands almost six months ago, there were no occasions for Old Lu to take action. He would teach during the day and retire peacefully at night.

Once the parent-teacher meeting ended and they officially broke for the holidays, both students and teachers had a holiday of two whole months.

"What do you think, how about we find a place to have some fun after the holiday?"

"That sounds good," Lu Yang and Xue Shilou had no objections.

While the three were speaking, Fang Zhige and Su Yuan came to Lu Yang, holding an ice box.

"Teacher Lu, can you open this ice box?"

Lu Yang was startled. The ice box was carved quite anciently, obviously no ordinary object.

"Where did you find this?"

Su Yuan, with his head lowered, dared not face Teacher Lu. "We picked it up."

"...Tell the truth to your teacher."

"We picked it up from beneath the Killing Heart Secret Realm under Soul Cliff."

Lu Yang tapped them both: "Soul Cliff is not a place you should be going to. What would you have done if something had happened? Even I couldn’t have saved you in time!"

Su Yuan muttered softly, "That voice said it was safe..."

"Listen to it or listen to me?"

"We’ll listen to you, Teacher."

Lu Yang’s expression relaxed slightly as he carefully examined the ice box. His cultivation had reached the Divinity Transformation Stage, yet he couldn’t see through the ice box.

Meng Jingzhou and Xue Shilou shook their heads; they had never seen such an ice box.

"Fairy, you..."

"This looks like Leng Ningxiang’s ice box."

"Who is Leng Ningxiang?"

"Oh, she’s an assassin, always cold-faced and never smiles. She’s quite attractive, ranking at the bottom of the top ten beauties of Ancient Times. Her cultivation technique is the ’Killing Heart Scripture,’ which emphasizes harboring a murderous intent while maintaining a heart as calm as an ancient well. However, she never fully mastered her technique."

Being at the bottom of the top ten beauties of Ancient Times would still mean she was extraordinarily beautiful.

"Why hasn’t her technique been mastered? Is it because she lacks talent?"

"Not really. It’s because the Killing Heart Scripture requires detachment from personal feelings and compassion. However, during one assassination mission, she fell for Yang Kongdong. Although she always denied liking Yang Kongdong, the progress of her cultivation didn’t lie—she liked him."

"Yang Kongdong is the one with the Harem Golden Core?"

"That’s right."

The Immortal Fairy used her Immortal Sense to penetrate the ice box’s layered seals: "Let’s see what’s inside this box... Is that an arm?"

Chapter 1176: Chapter 1175: My Things Were Originally Taken by Your Two Schools

"A severed arm?" Lu Yang’s expression gradually became more vivid.

If I remember correctly, Fairy Eternity once mentioned that Yang Kongdong had numerous concubines. In the end, a fire in the harem led to him being dismembered by them.

If Leng Ningxiang was one of the concubines, wouldn’t stealing an arm seem not too difficult?

"This ice box is somewhat peculiar. It’s not safe in your hands. How about I temporarily keep it for safekeeping?" Lu Yang said gently.

The voice inside Su Yuan’s body sneered, already suspecting that this man surnamed Lu was no good—he must have realized it was a treasure and was merely fabricating excuses to claim it.

Su Yuan was really naive. It was obvious the ice box was extraordinary, and he should have hidden it, yet he just brought it out, practically waiting for it to be stolen.

Su Yuan and Fang Zhige didn’t think much about it and simply agreed.

"Then goodbye to Teacher Lu, Teacher Xue, and Teacher Meng. See you next year."

The pair bid farewell, and following the students and parents, they left the martial arts hall, which was now only occupied by the three teachers and Elder Murong.

"What a handsome ice box." Although Xue Shilou didn’t know what was inside the ice box, that didn’t stop him from finding it impressive.

The gorgeous patterns on the ice box seemed to tell an ancient legend, both simple and majestic.

Xue Shilou then took out his own ice box for comparison. His also had intricate patterns, but compared to the one brought by Fang Zhige, it was somewhat lacking.

...

In a secret room, a pair of eyes slowly opened, flashing an unusual light.

"I didn’t expect that before I could find the arm, it would appear on its own in Muxue City?"

"Is this what they call fate?"

A tall figure stood up, revealing a thought-provoking smile.

...

After the parent-teacher meeting, Huo Huashen, who had been tense, yawned and relaxed.

Large snowflakes fell on his head, which he brushed away.

He looked up at the gray sky, "It’s snowing again."

No, no, can’t doze off. Standing outside, he represented the face of the martial arts hall; he needed to maintain his essence, qi, and spirit.

Thinking this, Huo Huashen perked up and stood at attention.

"Little Huo."

Hearing someone calling him, Huo Huashen instantly shivered; the voice sounded a bit familiar.

Then, he saw three people approaching at the street corner.

It was his own Sect Leader, Chi Sect Leader of the Yaoyang Sect, and Grand Elder Liu Zhen.

Why had three esteemed transcendence tribulation figures from two sects all come here?

"Greetings, Sect Leader!" Excited, Huo Huashen was about to kneel but was gently supported by a mana force from Mu Baiyi.

"That’s enough, there are too many prying eyes here; no need for such formalities."

"Yes!"

Twenty Nascent Soul Stage juniors also noticed the commotion and hurried over, not just to let Sect Leader Mu recognize them, but getting familiarized was also beneficial.

Having the Sect Leader personally inspect their work, following their elder brother to the Extreme Northern Lands really had its perks.

Mu Baiyi waved his hand to make the Nascent Soul disciples step back.

"It seems you have been doing well here. I heard that it was you who found the lead on the Ruthless Sect."

"Sect Leader flatters me; it was merely a coincidence."

"Even coincidence is part of fortune. Since you have been in Muxue City this whole time, do you perhaps know the whereabouts of the Carefree Guest?"

"The Carefree Guest?"

Huo Huashen was somewhat puzzled and didn’t know why the Sect Leader would suddenly bring up the Carefree Guest, although the Carefree Guest was the strongest among those in the Divinity Transformation Stage in the Extreme Northern Lands, it hardly seemed worth the personal inquiry of three people from the Transcendance Tribulation Stage.

He bowed his head and told the truth.

"Sect Leader, a few days ago, the Carefree Guest indeed appeared in the Extreme Northern Lands and even angered Vice City Lord Ma of Muxue City. However, the Carefree Guest truly has skills. Vice City Lord Ma locked down the city for ten days and dug three feet into the ground, but still couldn’t find the whereabouts of the Carefree Guest."

"The Carefree Guest had once declared that he would seek revenge on Vice City Lord Ma, but so much time has passed and the Carefree Guest hasn’t made a move for revenge. It seems likely that he simply spouted momentary bravado and did not dare to provoke Vice City Lord Ma any further, having already left Muxue City."

"Has he already left?" Mu Baiyi pondered.

This was troublesome. Now, they had this single clue about the Ruthless Sect Leader, and it was cut off.

The two sects had already offended the Ruthless Sect, so they must eradicate it completely, offending them to the death.

They couldn’t rest until the Ruthless Sect Leader was dealt with.

The Jiuyou Sect’s Grand Elder Liu Zhen snorted coldly, "Humph, all for naught, a wasted trip."

Suddenly, Mu Baiyi shuddered, feeling someone release a murderous intent, and looked sharply in that direction before shouting loudly.

"Who is it!"

Through the falling heavy snow, a slender figure approached, a smile of unclear intent hanging on his lips—uncertain whether it was a sneer or a scoff.

"Unexpected, really unexpected, my things ended up in the hands of you two sects."

A chill glinted in the eyes of the slender figure.

His arm was part of him, and as long as the arm came within his sense range, even with it sealed in the treasure box, he could still vaguely sense its location.

Following his perception all the way here, he sensed that his arm was right inside this Tiger Roar Martial Arts Hall.

And both Sect Leader Mu, Chi Sect Leader, and Grand Elder Liu Zhen were all here.

How could there be such a coincidence in the world!

Surely, these two sects found his arm and used it as bait to lure him in.

Laughable to the extreme, truly ignorant of the heavens and the earth, to actually dare plot against him.

"City Lord?" Huo Huashen was astonished the moment he saw the slender figure.

The visitor was actually the City Lord of Muxue City!

"City Lord? No, he’s just taken on the appearance of the City Lord of Muxue City."

Mu Baiyi and the other two Transcendance Tribulation Stage individuals walked slowly towards the slender figure, expressions solemn.

"The City Lord of Muxue City is said to be a powerhouse of the Extreme Northern Lands, but he’s only at Integration Peak, and it’s impossible for him to approach us undetected, am I right, Sect Leader Yang?"

"Sect Leader Yang? The Ruthless Sect’s Sect Leader Yang?" Huo Huashen was shocked, so the City Lord of Muxue City was the Ruthless Sect’s Sect Leader Yang?!

"Mu Baiyi, interesting. Among the three sect leaders, I admire Eternity Sect the most, followed by your Jiuyou Sect. After Qin Haoran died, Jiuyou Sect didn’t fall apart under your management but thrived instead."

Sect Leader Yang chuckled lightly, his tone casual as if conversing with a long-lost friend.

Then his voice cooled, the air filling with murderous intent.

"But that’s no reason for you to scheme against me."

"Really thought that because Great Xia put all four sects side by side, you have the status to stand equal with me."

"Arrogant!" Liu Zhen couldn’t hold himself back, taking the initiative to attack first. Of the three Transcendance Tribulation Stage members from both sects, only he was a veteran at Middle Tribulation Stage.

"Great Sun Crossing the Sky!"

A burning sun ignited atop Liu Zhen’s head, the temperature sudden spiked, instantly melting the heavy falling snow.

"Wait, don’t attack, take it to the sky. Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou are still inside!" Mu Baiyi didn’t expect Liu Zhen to be so impatient to fight.

Both Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were inside the martial arts hall, and if either of them were harmed, they would have to face the relentless pursuit of the Seek Dao Sect and the Meng Family!

However, it was too late for Mu Baiyi’s words as the Great Sun was already taking shape.

"Plucking Plum Immortal Palm."

Sect Leader Yang’s figure blurred, appearing in front of Liu Zhen in an instant and striking his abdomen with a palm, dispersing the Great Sun.

Chapter 1177: Chapter 1176: Demonic Sect Civil War

"Tell me where the item was found, and I might spare your lives," Sect Leader Yang said slowly. He had gone through great pains to obtain information that someone near Muxue City had gained an inheritance suspected to be Leng Ningxiang’s, and his own left arm was definitely among Leng Ningxiang’s buried items.

As long as he knew where Leng Ningxiang was buried, he would be able to find his own left arm.

But he hadn’t found it.

The Jiuyou Sect and Yaoyang Sect had only arrived in the Extreme Northern Lands for a short time when they found his left arm. They must know where Leng Ningxiang’s inheritance was.

"What item?" Mu Baiyi and Chi Sect Leader, about to make their move, were confused.

"You’re acting quite convincingly. It seems neither of you wants to live!"

Sect Leader Yang’s face turned cold, truly a case of not shedding tears until one sees the coffin.

Mu Baiyi thought the Yangs were simply madmen. Of course, everyone in the Ruthless Sect was a madman, and Sect Leader Yang, as the head of the Ruthless Sect, spouting madness was nothing out of the ordinary.

He suppressed the urge to curse loudly and struck alongside Chi Sect Leader.

"Let’s attack together!"

"Gold Crow True Flame!" Chi Sect Leader’s eyes shot out countless gold crows made of Gold Crow True Flame, as if the gold crows were reincarnated, lifelike.

The gold crows, fast as lightning, flew towards Sect Leader Yang, who had an incomplete soul and a missing arm, unwilling to face such an extremely yang entity and leapt into the air.

"Abyss Hell—Big Grinding Plate!"

A huge iceberg appeared out of nowhere above Muxue City, causing an uproar among the citizens. What was happening? Why had an iceberg suddenly appeared?!

Countless bronze chains, heated to scalding by flames, emerged from the iceberg, rattling towards Sect Leader Yang as he leapt into the air.

Sect Leader Yang was entangled by the scalding bronze chains and dragged towards the iceberg above Muxue City.

The Big Grinding Plate of Abyss Hell contained the concept of one yin and one yang, the iceberg represented the ultimate yin, and the chains the ultimate yang. When a sinner’s soul was bound by the ultimate yang chains on the ultimate yin iceberg, it was like being crushed by a millstone, only stopping when reduced to dust and bone.

"Golden Cicada shedding skin."

Lu Yang was pondering whether to ask Immortal Fairy to open the ice box.

Before he made up his mind, a thunderous noise came from outside.

Looking out the window after pushing it open, he saw Mu Baiyi and Chi Sect Leader fighting with someone he didn’t recognize.

"Wow, how did they start fighting?"

Meng Jingzhou regretted slapping his thigh; he should never have come to the Extreme Northern Lands.

He hadn’t encountered the four Great Demon Kings, but this time, directly came across four Transcendence Tribulation Stage figures.

Who else’s mundane life has experienced fighting among four Transcendence Tribulation Stage figures above their heads?

In the backyard, Old Ma looked up at the sky, occasionally lowered his head to eat some grass, then continued gazing at the sky.

He had come to the Extreme Northern Lands this time not as a Protector but as an onlooker.

Finally, there was some excitement to watch.

"Why is Mu Baiyi calling him Sect Leader Yang? Could it be that he is Yang Kongdong, the Sect Leader of the Ruthless Sect?" Lu Yang only remembered that the Sect Leader of the Ruthless Sect bore the surname Yang, his real name unknown. According to the testimonies of the two captured Vice Sect Hierarchs, even they weren’t sure if their leader truly bore the surname Yang.

"So it really is Yang Kongdong, huh? I didn’t expect this guy to still be alive, his life really is tough," Immortal Fairy’s voice echoed in Lu Yang’s ears.

"Who would have thought that he didn’t die when he was dismembered back then, but survived the ordeal through a secret technique or perhaps his concubines didn’t actually want to kill him back when they parted his body. Maybe they just wanted a part of his body to stay with them forever?" Immortal Fairy speculated.

"But no matter what, his method is still not as good as my Playing Dead Technique," Immortal Fairy boasted proudly, explaining that practitioners could be dismembered during the Playing Dead Technique but could resurrect exactly as before once the technique was lifted.

Which was unlike Yang Kongdong, who still lacked a piece of his soul—the left arm.

"Does that mean the Sect Leader Yang of the Ruthless Sect is indeed Yang Kongdong?" Lu Yang realized, seeing the deep roots of the Ruthless Sect.

At Su Yuan’s home.

Su Yuan nervously looked at the sky, not expecting that a fight would break out towards the Martial Arts Hall just as he had returned home.

He hoped Lu Yang and the others were safe.

In Su Yuan’s spiritual space, a white figure sealing its own power saw the battle of the three sects through Su Yuan’s eyes. The moment it saw Yang Kongdong, cold sweat broke out and its body trembled continuously as lost memories surged forth, piecing together past experiences.

"I... I remember now; I am the true City Lord of Muxue City!"

It suddenly looked up, anger filling the sky, and roared at Yang Kongdong, "It was you, you killed me and took my place!"

Shi Family.

The Clan Leader of the Ice Flood Dragon Clan, who was reminiscing, stared dumbfoundedly at the sky.

"By the Ancient Ancestor above, how did four Transcendance Tribulation Stage suddenly appear?"

Wasn’t it said that Muxue City didn’t have even one Transcendance Tribulation Stage?

He had just come to attend a parent-teacher meeting, to get acquainted in front of Lu Yang, and afterwards, there was such an exciting show?

In the sky, attacks continuously fell. If any landed within the city, countless would die or be injured. The high officials of Muxue City acted together to block these attacks.

They never thought that their city lord was no longer the same as before.

Muxue City had a City Protection Array, but only the city lord knew how to activate the Array Method, and naturally, Yang Kongdong wouldn’t care about the death of Muxue City’s citizens.

"Not good, two attacks are coming at me at the same time!" Vice City Lord Ma cursed inwardly, unable to withstand two attacks.

Suddenly, a small wooden sword flew by, blocking one of the attacks.

"Elder!" Vice City Lord Ma was very excited and looked for the owner of the small wooden sword, only to find that the greatly respected master of Swordsmanship had always been in Muxue City.

"He’s really troublesome." Yang Kongdong was getting impatient, as he was slightly winning despite being one against three.

But securing a quick victory wasn’t easy.

"Get the arm, complete the soul, and all problems can be solved easily."

Yang Kongdong fought as he moved towards the Martial Arts Hall.

"Not good, stop him!" Mu Baiyi became anxious. Both Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were in the Martial Arts Hall; these two definitely couldn’t be allowed to come to harm!

And he also faintly felt that a great disaster was imminent. If Sect Leader Yang got close to the Martial Arts Hall, there would no longer be any chance of winning.

Seeing Mu Baiyi’s reaction, Yang Kongdong was certain that Mu Baiyi had found his arm.

"Scorch the heavens, boil the oceans!" Chi Sect Leader and Liu Zhen acted together, flames hot enough to evaporate lakes appearing in their palms with just a wisp.

"Abyss Hell–Avici Blade!"

Mu Baiyi held the Abyss Avici Blade, its blade pitch-black with ghastly figures entwined around it. After it was nurtured for decades in Fengdu, it became his Life-Bound Magical Treasure after he advanced to the Transcendance Tribulation Stage.

"Plucking Plum Immortal Palm."

Yang Kongdong refused to withstand these attacks directly, repeating his old trick by striking Chi Sect Leader’s abdomen with a palm.

Like a kite with its strings cut, Chi Sect Leader crashed through the ceiling of the Martial Arts Hall and fell in front of Older Teacher Lu, writhing in pain on the ground.

Yang Kongdong’s gaze fell on two ice boxes placed on the podium.

Xue Shilou noticed Yang Kongdong’s gaze and hurriedly guarded his own ice box.

"Found it!"

Yang Kongdong, seeing Xue Shilou’s unusual reaction, reached out with an invisible giant hand and forcibly took the ice box.

"My ice box!" Xue Shilou shouted, but it was to no avail.

Yang Kongdong couldn’t help but touch the ice box, feeling that after so long, his body was finally complete.

The beauties did not kill him after dismembering him back then; instead, each obtained a part of him and buried his body with their dead, unwilling to just be buried like that, he slept using secret techniques, and during the Great Xia period, a junior cultivator awakened his head.

He continuously tempted the junior cultivator to find other parts of his body, aiding his return to his prime.

"Not good, don’t let him get the ice box!" Mu Baiyi shouted, realizing that the ice box contained the "thing" Yang Kongdong mentioned.

"Too late!"

Yang Kongdong crushed the ice box without hesitation, taking out a column of ice shaped like an ice sword.

The fight suddenly stopped, and the three Transcendance Tribulation Stage from both sects looked at Yang Kongdong skeptically. Is this ice sword such a precious thing?

"Where is my arm!"

Chapter 1178: Chapter 1177: The Origins of Yang Kongdong’s Various Moves

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou bowed their heads to look at the ice box lying undisturbed on the podium, then simultaneously turned their heads to look at Xue Shilou, who was distressed nearby.

If it weren’t for Xue Shilou protecting his ice box in time, Yang Kongdong wouldn’t have mistaken it for something else.
