With a splat—

Lu Yang couldn’t dodge this palm strike; it pierced through his abdomen, blood flowed ceaselessly, and his breath grew weak.

"Old Lu!" Meng Jingzhou shouted excitedly upon seeing this scene.

"Teacher Lu!"

The students of the Martial Arts Hall cried inconsolably upon witnessing this scene, unable to bear watching any longer.

Yang Kongdong, from his superior position, looked down at Lu Yang, "If that’s all the ability you have, you might as well die."

The gap in their realms was too great; no technique could bridge it.

"Don’t worry, everyone in this city will be buried with you."

Suddenly, Lu Yang looked up, his mouth bloody, and gazed at Yang Kongdong, his eyes full of mockery.

"Senior Yang Kongdong, I heard you like to borrow strength using the Harem Golden Core. Coincidentally, I also like to borrow strength. Do you know from whom it is best to borrow strength?"

"What?" Yang Kongdong was stunned for a moment, not understanding the meaning behind Lu Yang’s words.

Suddenly, his complexion changed, witnessing a scene he could never comprehend in his lifetime.

Lu Yang’s Realm kept soaring, from Early Integration Stage, Mid Integration Stage, Integration Late Stage, Early Tribulation Stage, Middle Tribulation Stage, Late Tribulation Stage... to Pass Tribulation Peak!

What’s happening? Did the Void Refinement Stage just coincidentally fluctuate to the Pass Tribulation Peak?

How could such a coincidence happen!

In an instant, Lu Yang’s injuries healed, and his aura surged to an unbelievably high level.

Lu Yang stepped closer to Yang Kongdong, who felt as if he was not facing Lu Yang but an unreachable Immortal Mountain!

"The answer is that it’s easiest to borrow power from oneself!"

Tofu Venerable Celestial Form, borrowing the power of the Buddha Country Immortal Body.

Chapter 1182: Chapter 1181: The More You Know, the Faster You Die

"Who can tell me what’s happening, why does Talent Lu’s momentum seem even stronger than it was at the beginning?"

The common people of Muxue City could hardly discern Lu Yang’s exact realm; their vague feelings were based on the atmosphere at the scene.

The city’s defensive commander had a grave expression, and his voice trembled as he spoke, "Hundreds of years ago, I once saw a great demon emperor from afar, swallowing a whole city in one bite. Only later did I learn that it was a Middle Tribulation Stage great demon emperor, yet the sense of danger that Lu Yang gives me far exceeds that of the great demon emperor."

"Could it be that he’s now in the Late Tribulation Stage... or even the peak?!"

"Yes, that’s it, his realm must have fluctuated to the Pass Tribulation Peak!"

Meng Jingzhou, watching from below, gritted his teeth in frustration. "Bullshit about realm fluctuation to Pass Tribulation Peak. Just now, Old Lu rushed toward Yang Kongdong for a bloody battle and took the opportunity to use Imitation Fist, borrowing strength."

Lu Yang twisted his shoulders and, holding the Green Peak Sword, stepped closer to Yang Kongdong.

"Senior Yang, you hit me quite hard just now, it’s only fair that it’s my turn!"

Lu Yang transformed into a rainbow, a dazzling light blooming as he next materialized behind Yang Kongdong, sheathing his sword, and a spray of blood blossomed on Yang Kongdong’s chest.

Disbelief contorted Yang Kongdong’s face as he twisted his head to look at Lu Yang behind him; a single stroke had pierced his chest—what an incomparable swordsmanship!

Even Liu Ningxuan, who had created the Silent Destruction Sword Technique, was no better back in his day!

"Carefree Steps!"

Yang Kongdong vanished on the spot. After entering the Heartless Realm, his Killing Heart Scripture and Carefree Steps had both improved. There was no way Lu Yang could keep up with his speed.

Mu Baiyi and his two companions turned pale upon witnessing this. None of them had seen how Yang Kongdong disappeared; if they were in his place, they were certain to die without a doubt!

Yang Kongdong, now an unparalleled assassin, hid his presence and appeared above Lu Yang, icy dagger in hand, aiming a lethal strike at the crown of his head!

Yet unexpectedly, Lu Yang looked up, locking eyes with Yang Kongdong as if he had known he would be there, thrusting his sword once more. The blade shattered the icy dagger and pierced through Yang Kongdong’s right hand!

Yang Kongdong quickly retreated, activating the Snow Lotus Secret Method from Heavenly Mountain Sacred Land to rapidly heal his injury, then vanished once again using the Carefree Steps.

A coincidence?

Yang Kongdong refused to believe in such luck, continually circling around Lu Yang, looking for an opportunity to strike. Unexpectedly, Lu Yang raised his hand and unleashed a Sword Qi. Yang Kongdong abruptly stopped to dodge the attack but then a second Sword Qi followed, slashing a deep, bone-exposing wound across his back.

The Carefree Steps he was so proud of were ineffective in front of Lu Yang!

Lu Yang’s Spiritual Sense was incredibly strong, allowing him clear sight of Yang Kongdong’s every move. Although he wasn’t adept at footwork and couldn’t keep pace with Yang Kongdong’s steps, his Sword Qi was astonishingly fast!

Since Carefree Steps didn’t work, Yang Kongdong immediately changed his strategy, grasping an ice-cold spear. The spear thrust forward like a dragon, employing the Shaohao Spear Technique.

Clang, clang, clang, clang—

Spear clashed with sword, and Yang Kongdong once again felt an oppressive force emanating from Lu Yang.

The sense of oppression that came with Lu Yang’s recent ascension was not an illusion but intuition!

Setting aside the Dao Fruit Embryo, Yang Kongdong himself was a Transcendance Tribulation Peak elite powerhouse. Not to mention, he harnessed a multitude of abilities reflecting the strengths of various schools, thoroughly mastering numerous prestigious techniques from Ancient Times.

But now to feel pressure from a junior who was also at the Pass Tribulation Peak was simply inconceivable.

No, that wasn’t right. This feeling of being crushed by someone of the same realm, he had experienced it in Ancient Times, among those invincible at the Pass Tribulation Stage who successfully became immortals!

What a joke. Even if one’s realm climbed, they needed corresponding combat experience to match. Merely improving one’s realm without practical application of skills was like a child holding a knife; the advantage in realm could not be played to even half its effect.

But what was up with this junior Lu Yang? It was as if he had long been familiar with the methods of combat in the Transcendance Tribulation Stage. Facing Lu Yang was like facing an experienced, veteran Pass Tribulation Cultivator; his moves were controlled and precise, his magic skills and swordsmanship were seamlessly interwoven.

Even if someone fluctuated to the Pass Tribulation Stage occasionally during the Void Refinement Stage, taking that opportunity to boost their combat experience, this kind of result should not be possible.

Where did such rich combat experience come from?!

Yang Kongdong, who had been through the brilliant power struggles of the Great Era of Ancient Times and was even one of its main characters, thought he had seen all sorts of situations, yet Lu Yang’s case still far exceeded his understanding!

The people of Muxue City did not understand why Lu Yang had suddenly grown stronger, but even they could see that Yang Kongdong was on the losing end in battle after Lu Yang’s transformation. The number of injuries on Yang Kongdong kept increasing, and the healing pace of the Snow Lotus Secret Method couldn’t keep up with the rate at which he was getting injured.

Resurrected from a hopeless situation, Muxue City erupted in cheers, shouting Lu Yang’s name.

Xue Shilou eyed Lu Yang’s swordsmanship with a burning gaze, every strike captivating him beyond his understanding.

"This is what it means to be a Sword Cultivator..."

The Rake Skill and Shovel Skill that he had dedicated time to comprehend gradually surfaced in his mind, inspiring Xue Shilou with newfound mental agility.

"You junior might have had some fortuitous encounters to gain experience in Pass Tribulation combat, but the gap between the Pass Tribulation Stage and the Dao Fruit Outline is not something you can imagine!" Yang Kongdong had assumed that Lu Yang had just managed to fluctuate to the Pass Tribulation Peak and thought that dragging out the fight would see his realm fall back down.

At this rate, if the fight continued, he would be the one to die!

Semi-Immortals had an absolute advantage over Pass Tribulation Cultivators. Yang Kongdong had never cared about Pass Tribulation Cultivators; even both Vice Sect Hierarchs of the Ruthless Sect were Pass Tribulation Cultivators, and their capture by Great Xia had not caused the slightest ripple in his heart. They were disposable, less important than finding his left arm in the Extreme Northern Lands.

"Alas."

Yang Kongdong activated the Seven Emotions Dao Fruit Embryo, and an aura of sorrow spread quickly. Cries arose from beneath Muxue City, overwhelming mortals and cultivators alike, reducing them to tears and stripping them of their will to fight, now merely lambs for the slaughter.

In contrast, Lu Yang’s eyes shone brightly as if harboring twin swords, completely unaffected by the Seven Emotions Dao Fruit Embryo!

Of course, Lu Yang was unaffected. The power he borrowed was from his own Buddha Country Immortal Body; he was practically an immortal clone now. Unless Yang Kongdong used an actual Seven Emotions Dao Fruit, he could not affect him.

"How is this possible!"

Seeing this, Yang Kongdong was so surprised he almost lost his Merciless State of Mind. Unlike the direct attacks of the Embryonic Spatial Dao Fruit and Vajra Dao Fruit Embryo, the Seven Emotions Dao Fruit Embryo was cunning and difficult to defend against; it had been tested many times during conflicts in Ancient Times, even catching Semi-Immortals in its snare.

He had even made Semi-Immortals fall for him.

"No, there’s someone inside your body!"

Though Yang Kongdong couldn’t control Lu Yang’s emotions, he could sense them.

And in his perception, at this moment Lu Yang had dual emotions, the most likely explanation being that there was someone else inside Lu Yang’s body!

Lu Yang looked at Yang Kongdong with some surprise, never underestimating the Seven Emotions Dao Fruit Embryo.

His lips curled into a cruel smile, "Senior Yang seems to know a lot. That means you cannot be allowed to live."

Chapter 1183: Chapter 1182: Death of the Ruthless Sect Master

Seeing the smile tugging at Lu Yang’s lips, Yang Kongdong was suddenly seized by a chill.

That smile looked nothing like one belonging to a good person!

Wasn’t the Seek Dao Sect claimed to be the leader of the Five Great Immortal Sects of Great Xia, the foremost of the Righteous Path? Could this really be a prodigy nurtured by the Seek Dao Sect?!

Lu Yang approached Yang Kongdong with a sinister smile, and before Yang Kongdong knew what magic skill had been used, his vision suddenly blacked out, and he could see nothing at all.

The citizens of Muxue City could see clearly. All at once, a pair of hands larger than Muxue City itself had appeared, crossing and enveloping Yang Kongdong.

Yang Kongdong realized something was amiss and tried to escape, firing ten Cold Ice Breaking Arrows in rapid succession, hoping to tear open an exit. However, these enormous hands contained the power of space itself; any attack or sword skill was redirected to another dimension.

"Damn, it’s Universe in Palm!" Yang Kongdong recognized this ancient and formidable Divine Ability, but it was already too late.

As Lu Yang’s hands crossed and clasped together, the gigantic hands enveloping Yang Kongdong also came together,

and as the two giant hands vanished, a golden cicada’s shell about the size of a person emerged, now shattered and releasing an injured and battered Yang Kongdong.

Although he had avoided most of the attack using the Golden Cicada Shedding Skill, he was still seriously injured.

The Golden Cicada Shedding Skill could only be used three times in quick succession, and he had already used it twice.

Previously, in the hundreds of exchanges between Lu Yang and Yang Kongdong, Yang Kongdong’s spiritual essence had gradually shown symptoms of depletion, and the Snow Lotus Secret Method was insufficient to completely heal his injuries.

In contrast, Lu Yang seemed to possess an unending surge of spiritual essence.

Indeed, Lu Yang’s spiritual essence was inexhaustible. Although Tofu Venerable Celestial Form could not transform him into an Immortal Body, the Buddha Country Immortal Body could constantly provide him with spiritual essence, exhausting Yang Kongdong to death.

The commotion of the battle was so great that even city lords from a thousand miles away were drawn to the scene. The sight of the two clashing made their scalps go numb, knowing that appearing on the battlefield would not allow them to survive even three moments.

Old Ma was lying in the stable, munching on the frozen hay while attentively observing and learning.

It has to be said, setting out with Lu Yang indeed enriched one’s combat experience.

He had seen many battles between Pass Tribulation Cultivators, but those so-called battles were merely sparring sessions, with both sides holding back, so the experience gained from watching them was limited.

But setting out with Lu Yang was different; they encountered bloodbaths among Pass Tribulation and Semi-Immortal cultivators, full disclosure of their trump cards, battles fought to the death. Observing such fights, one’s combat experience would soar rapidly, with unmatched efficacy.

Over the years, he had accompanied Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou on their journeys, and not only had his realm improved, but his perspective and combat experience had also increased significantly.

He and Meng Jingzhou’s father, Meng Potian, along with the housekeeper of Meng Residence, were sworn brothers. Among them, Meng Potian was the strongest, the eldest brother, and now Old Ma reckoned that even Meng Potian himself might not be his match.

Xue Shilou, who was also observing the battle, found it quite enlightening; his eyes glazed over as he mumbled to himself, gradually developing his unique set of sword skills.

Pu—

Yang Kongdong’s abdomen was pierced by a sword, suffering a wound so severe that it could no longer be healed.

His eyes bloodshot, he snapped out of his Heartless State, furious to the extreme. The Heartless State had allowed him to make calm judgments, while the Angry State enabled him to perform beyond his usual limits and take his strength to the next level.

"Youngster, you forced my hand!"

He made a series of hand seals, exceedingly complicated. Mu Baiyi and the other two felt a chill run down their spines; this was the same Kongtong Seal that had heavily injured them!

This was Yang Kongdong’s most prized move, the essence of all his learned skills refined and condensed into the unique Kongtong Seal.

The citizens of Muxue City, as well as the nearby city lords who had come to watch, felt an overwhelming suffocation. This was merely the aura leaking from the Kongtong Seal; they couldn’t even imagine what it must be like to face it head-on.

No living being could survive beneath the Kongtong Seal!

"I have my own self-created moves as well," Lu Yang’s sword moved with his will, Essence, Qi, and Spirit unified, reaching the realm of Sword Heart Clarity. His Sword Qi was concealed, not leaking even the slightest bit. To an onlooker, it would be hard to tell that the Green Peak Sword was imbued with Sword Qi at all.

He focused all his power into his right arm, muscles bulging visibly as small blood vessels burst, leaving his arm bloody.

"Immortal Sword Technique!"

Boom—

The seal and the sword technique collided, turning the world black and white, and for a moment, everyone lost their sight and hearing. All was chaos; whether a moment or the time it took to drink a cup of tea passed before they regained their senses, no one could say.

"Who won?"

At the center of the battle, Lu Yang’s right arm had vanished. Rubbing their eyes for a clearer look, they saw his arm reappear without a scratch on his body, only his clothes extensively damaged.

In contrast, Yang Kongdong was left with only the upper half of his body. His lower half had been completely shredded by the Immortal Sword Technique, not even bits of flesh remaining. It was hard to believe that a Pass Tribulation Cultivator could execute such a terrifying move.

In Ancient Times, it was rare for a duel between cultivators at the Pass Tribulation Peak to end in death, unless there was a great disparity in strength.

The cultivators from Muxue City, at Body Integration Realm and Pass Tribulation Stage, stood dumbfounded, feeling as if their prior cultivation beliefs had collapsed. A Pass Tribulation Cultivator had actually defeated a Semi-Immortal!

Yang Kongdong, weak and on the verge of death, glared at Lu Yang with a look of deep resentment, as if to etch Lu Yang’s image into his mind before crushing a token.

"You young fool, you forced my hand!"

He had an agreement with the Great Qian Dynasty; in exchange for helping them find the Four Ancient Immortals’ clues, the Great Qian Dynasty would assist at a crucial moment.

He hadn’t wanted to resort to this measure, but Lu Yang had pushed him to a dead end. Without using it, death was certain!

Luckily, he had one use left of his ’Golden Cicada shedding skin’. Yang Kongdong made up his mind to use it to recover from his injuries and then watch how the Great Qian Dynasty would kill this junior!

"Golden Cicada..."

"Yang Lang, wouldn’t it be nice to always be with me?"

Leng Ningxiang appeared from his left arm, hooked around Yang Kongdong’s neck, and tenderly kissed him.

Feeling Leng Ningxiang’s warmth, Yang Kongdong’s pupils contracted abruptly. Leng Ningxiang’s obsession hadn’t completely disappeared; she had been waiting for this moment all along!

Leng Ningxiang was still a master of using poison!

"Get away from me, you maniac!" Yang Kongdong desperately pushed Leng Ningxiang away, but she held on too tightly, and he couldn’t break free.

"Yang Lang, we will be together forever!"

They embraced and fell from the sky, landing in the backyard of the Martial Arts Hall. Yang Kongdong’s eyes widened as he stared blankly at the sky, breathless, while snow from the branches outside Lu Yang’s room fell, burying him.

Lu Yang had no extra concern to watch Yang Kongdong’s end. Yang Kongdong had created a huge problem for him; the token he’d crushed formed a spatial vortex from which a terrifying aura emanated.

A youth dressed in ancient ceremonial attire appeared, holding a Bone Staff adorned with ornaments, symbolizing the supreme authority of the Great Qian Dynasty.

The youth glanced at the dead Yang Kongdong and shook his head slightly—bringing the dead back to life was beyond him.

Then his gaze settled on Lu Yang.

"Yang Kongdong mentioned you have a clue to the Four Ancient Immortals?"

In fear of the Great Yu Dynasty breaking their promise, Yang Kongdong mentioned as he crushed the token that Lu Yang had a lead on the Four Ancient Immortals.

Lu Yang recognized the youth’s identity—Great Qian Dynasty, The Controller.

Chapter 1184: Chapter 1183: Snow Emperor

"Lord Controller is joking, how could a junior like me have any clues about the Four Ancient Immortals?" Lu Yang slowly backed away, calculating ways to escape.

The gap between those at the Transcendance Tribulation Stage and Immortals was insurmountable by any means, he could crush Yang Kongdong, and so could Lord Controller crush him.

"Oh, you know me?" Lord Controller looked at Lu Yang with interest. Whether it was the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord or he himself, they were all figures from three hundred thousand years ago, their images long gone in the river of history; modern Cultivators shouldn’t recognize him.

That’s not right, since the Demon-Subduing God Lord and the Demon-Removing God Lord fell at the Laurel Fairy Palace, the higher-ups of Great Xia had become aware of his and the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord’s appearances.

"You are Lu Yang? It seems your status in Great Xia is higher than I imagined."

Lord Controller smiled, this junior either knew the news of the Four Ancient Immortals or not, once captured, all would become clear.

He poked the skull of the Bone Staff, and from one side of the staff a bony hand emerged, fingers clenching and then loosening, as if just awakening from sleep.

Lu Yang struck with his sword, leaving only a white mark on the palm of the bone hand, unable to slow its attack.

"Little Yang, let Immortal try instead."

Fairy Eternity directly seized control of Lu Yang’s body.

Fairy Eternity, controlling Lu Yang’s body, lightly tapped her toes in mid-air, deftly avoiding the grasp of the bony hand.

"Oh, indeed there’s some skill here," Lord Controller raised an eyebrow. Logically speaking, Lu Yang should not have been able to dodge that hit, or rather, no Cultivator at the Transcendance Tribulation Stage should have been able to evade it.

Was it just a coincidence?

No matter.

A mere Transcendance Tribulation Cultivator was not worth his concern. Who was he? The one presiding over sacrifices for the Great Qian Dynasty, the Divine Monarch who condensed the Outline of the Dao Fruit with the Power of Faith. He had created so many Semi-Immortals, one could say a word from him could decide the life and death of a Pass Tribulation Cultivator.

Lord Controller threw out the Bone Staff, and as it caught the wind, it turned into a skeleton: "Go and capture him."

Following Lord Controller’s command, the skeleton’s eye sockets blazed with two green ghostly flames. This was his Lifebound Magical Artifact, forged from his own bones, akin to his clone, proficient in many Divine Abilities and magic skills.

The skeleton split into two hundred and six pieces of bone, separating and floating in mid-air.

Then, the bones rearranged themselves in another pattern, forming a cage and trapping Lu Yang.

Fairy Eternity didn’t know how to use a sword and wielded the Green Peak Sword like a hammer, smashing it hard against the cage, numbing her arms with the vibration.

Lord Controller crooked a finger, calling the cage back to him.

This was his Life-bound Magical Treasure, and it was impossible for a Transcendance Tribulation Cultivator to escape.

Then he saw a huge explosion within the cage, and after it cleared, Lu Yang appeared outside the cage.

Lord Controller frowned, Lu Yang’s actions had once again caught him off guard.

"Techniques like the Sky Demon Disintegration Technique, destroying oneself and then reconvening in another space."

"Quite interesting, I do want to see how many times you can use such a technique."

Then the cage trapped Lu Yang, he self-detonated to escape, the cage trapped Lu Yang, he self-detonated to escape, the cage trapped Lu Yang, he self-detonated to escape...

Lord Controller’s eyelids twitched, his face struggling to maintain composure.

Could the Sky Demon Disintegration Technique really be used consecutively?

Had he guessed wrong, and this wasn’t a magic skill but a Dao Fruit Outline?

No, that couldn’t be right. If it was a Dao Fruit Outline, at most it would self-detonate part of the body, how could it be a continuous full-body explosion?

If it was indeed a Dao Fruit, that would be even more absurd. The junior was just at the peak of the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, having temporarily reached this realm, how could he possess a Dao Fruit?

"Little Yang, you see, not only is self-detonation good for attacking, but it’s also very useful for escaping," Fairy Eternity still had the leisure to depict the blueprint of the Immortal Lineage with Lu Yang.

Lord Controller made an "X" gesture with his index finger, and two of the skeleton’s ribs flew from either side towards Lu Yang, stabbing into him. They carried the power of space, like two nails, fastening Lu Yang firmly within this space!

The hearts of the citizens of Muxue City were in their throats, having thought that resolving the Yang Kongdong matter would be the end of it. Little did they expect an even more terrifying existence to descend!

The various City Lords who had flown in to watch the battle were filled with regret. From Lord Controller’s leisurely stroll, it was clear that his cultivation level absolutely crushed that of Yang Kongdong and Lu Yang.

In other words, this was an Immortal!

If the Immortal took things seriously, a mere flick of his finger could reduce thousands of miles to flat ground. Although they were lofty Integration Period Cultivators, in front of an Immortal, they were no different from ordinary people!

...

At Tiger Roar Martial Arts Hall, Xue Shilou sat meditating with closed eyes, the scenes of his past flickering through his mind: learning swordsmanship from a young age, practicing his stance in the snow, gaining a bit of fame, the fusion of personalities, awakening of his bloodline, shining brightly in the Extreme Northern Lands, and receiving pointers from Daoist Lu on the Rake Skill and Shovel Skill.

Every part of his past had a reason, his experiences must contain some kind of meaning.

Daoist Lu deftly used a shovel to bury bodies, clearly, this was something he had done often.

Does this mean that as a Sword Cultivator, one must act in secrecy and kill imperceptibly?

Furthermore, it’s about being selfless in your swordsmanship, with one strike to the throat!

The mystery of the Rake Skill contained the unity of One Sword Becomes Ten Thousand and Ten Thousand Swords Returning to Origin.

Yes, indeed, a rake is also a type of sword.

Xue Shilou tossed his sword to the side and grabbed a rake. In that moment, the nine teeth of the rake were no longer just nine teeth—they were nine swords!

Meng Jingzhou frequently looked up at Lu Yang above him, then turned to glance at the mumbling Xue Shilou beside him, feeling like his eyes were not enough.

Xue Shilou, as if in communion with the rake, saw many Illusory Shadows appear around him, each shadow holding a sword and demonstrating different swordsmanship. Then the shadowy figures merged one after another into the rake, becoming a Swordsmanship unique to Xue Shilou.

"This is the swordsmanship I created... Rake Swordsmanship!"

"Rake Swordsmanship is not easily revealed. Once it appears in this world, it must end with death!"

Xue Shilou didn’t need to verify the strength of the swordsmanship he had created. The moment that the swordsmanship was born, the third trial of the Snow Emperor Bloodline automatically qualified him!

This was the best proof!

"I want to make my wish come true!" Xue Shilou stated, having completed the three trials of the Snow Emperor Bloodline, which would allow the Snow Emperor to grant any wish.

This was the only way to save Daoist Lu!

Space twisted and a white-robed, white-bearded elder walked out.

With his every breath, the entire Extreme Northern Lands seemed to breathe with him, his thoughts influencing the will of the Extreme Northern Lands.

He was the Snow Emperor, an existence only from the legends of the Extreme Northern Lands, someone no one had ever seen!

The white-bearded elder had a solemn expression and an inherent dignity. Following his appearance, except for Xue Shilou, no one knew who this white-bearded elder was, but they held their breath, not even daring to breathe heavily.

It was as if the presence of this white-bearded elder made legends something that offended the majesty of the heavens!

"Is it you who completed the three trials?" The Snow Emperor said while exhaling a chill, the air itself seemed to freeze.

"Junior Xue Shilou pays his respects to the Snow Emperor!" Xue Shilou knelt on the ground and bowed.

"What, he is the Snow Emperor!" Murong Grandpa was a cultivator born and bred in the Extreme Northern Lands and had, of course, heard tales of the Snow Emperor. He had not expected that this supremely powerful figure who suddenly appeared was the Snow Emperor!

Could it be that the Snow Emperor truly exists?

"Indeed, there has not been a qualified person for eighty thousand years." The Snow Emperor’s expression did not change, but one could hear the esteem he held for Xue Shilou in his tone.

"From now on, you shall be the new Snow Emperor. You have passed the three trials, and as per the rules, I can fulfill one wish for you. What is your wish?"

Upon hearing these words, Xue Shilou, excited, pointed to Lu Yang in the sky who was impaled by ribs.

"I want to save him!"

The Snow Emperor looked up, his cold gaze fixing on the young man dressed in ancient ceremonial garb. His expression tightened and his eyes deepened, as if he were an omniscient being that could see through all things.

He spoke slowly, with a certainty that could not be questioned.

"I can’t defeat an Immortal."

Chapter 1185: Chapter 1184: Stepping on the Tai Chi Diagram

"Ah?" Xue Shilou thought he must have heard wrong. freёnovelkiss.com

"What did you just say?" Xue Shilou cautiously repeated.

He had competed against the clock to invent new magic skills, all to ask the Snow Emperor to save Lu Yang.

"I’m only a Semi-Immortal, not strong enough to defeat an Immortal," the Snow Emperor seriously said, not feeling there was anything wrong with that statement. Rather, it would be peculiar if he could defeat an Immortal.

The Extreme Northern Lands were already sparsely populated, with far fewer people than the Central Continent, Buddha Country, Demon Territory, and East Sea, and it was difficult for even one Semi-Immortal to appear in a hundred thousand years, let alone an Immortal.

"Choose another wish, and I can make you a Semi-Immortal, grant you countless wealth, and teach you all the cultivation techniques and magic skills from the past to the present."

Grinding his teeth and persistently kowtowing, Xue Shilou said, "Saving Daoist Lu is my only wish!"

The Snow Emperor found himself in a difficult position; this was the first time his expression changed, as tradition dictated that he must satisfy one wish of the trialist.

But the problem was he truly couldn’t defeat an Immortal.

"If you really want to save someone, there is, in fact, a way."

Xue Shilou looked up in surprise; the Snow Emperor did have a method.

"It is customary for the Snow Emperor to fulfill one wish of the trialist, and if you have no objections, I can relinquish the position of Snow Emperor to you right now for you to fulfill your own wish."

Xue Shilou: "..."

Seeing Xue Shilou’s disappointment, the Snow Emperor said with heartfelt emotion, "Our Snow Emperor Lineage is destined to become Semi-Immortals with a lifespan of a hundred thousand years. In that time, we will make countless friends and witness many old friends pass on; your friend’s fall is but the inescapable destiny of friends of the Snow Emperor Lineage, and you must learn to accept it."

In his heart, the Snow Emperor added one more thought: unless the Ancient Immortal who bestowed upon him the Dao Fruit Outline intervenes.

With that in mind, he unconsciously touched the wordless white jade token on his chest.

But that was impossible.

Loud sounds of Self-Detonation once again echoed across the sky, attracting the Snow Emperor’s attention.

Pierced by ribs and nailed in this space, Lu Yang had once again escaped through Self-Detonation, stunning even The Controller, who could no longer sit still.

For a junior to use the same method to escape repeatedly right under his watch was one thing, but what was key was that this junior, after leaving the cage, just stood there beside it, without any intention to flee far!

It was a blatant disregard for him!

"Ghost Kings Invasion."

Thick smoke rose from the Bone Staff, each wisp manifesting as an incarnation of the King of Ghosts. Ten thousand ghosts swept across the sky, obscuring the sun, devouring every trace of Spiritual Energy in their path.

The Great Qian Dynasty practiced human sacrifice, offering humans to the divine, the nation, and the heavens. The great Qian Cultivators were never short of ghosts and other wicked beings; if there were none, they would simply create them.

The Snow Emperor shook his head, pitying the junior. It would not be just the junior who might die or be injured if he went up but even himself.

The wordless white jade token on his chest shook, inquiring the Snow Emperor about the events occurring outside.

The Snow Emperor relayed without missing a word what he had witnessed to the supreme being residing within the white jade token.

To his surprise, the supreme being’s reaction was incredibly intense.

"Immortal, those are Immortal moves; what is that youth’s relationship with Immortality!"

"This is a once-in-a-millennium opportunity, that youth must be related to Immortality; we cannot let anything happen to him here!"

"But once we leave this place, it will bring calamity..."

"Scared of bloody what!"

Before the Snow Emperor could even respond, a beam of Immortal light shot out from the white jade token toward the sky, leaving the flabbergasted Snow Emperor behind.

"How is this possible, he has never made a move for three hundred thousand years!"

An Immortal suddenly appeared in front of Lu Yang, with a speed so fast it was almost instantaneous.

Facing the ferocious approach of tens of thousands of ghastly Ghost Kings, the Immortal stood upon the Tai Chi Diagram, the Power of the Supreme Yang surging forth, burning away everything in the world, rendering the Sun dull and colorless in this moment.

"Get lost, all of you!"

No matter what the cultivation level of the King of Ghosts had been in life, or the type of devouring intent The Controller overlaid upon them, before the Power of the Supreme Yang, they all ignited in self-detonation and in the blink of an eye, were reduced to ash and smoke!

The Immortal, dressed in coarse cloth, unkempt and looking like a savage who had walked out of a cave from ancient times, was filled with wildness.

The moment The Controller saw the Immortal, he braced himself as if facing a great enemy, slowly pronouncing the other’s title.

"Immortal Jiuchong!"

Upon hearing The Controller announce the name of Immortal Jiuchong, the area below Muxue City was thrown into an uproar.

"Immortal Jiuchong?! Is it the legendary first Immortal Jiuchong who became immortal?"

"Who else would dare to carry that title!"

"Good heavens, even the Immortal Jiuchong has appeared!"

Immortal Jiuchong turned his head and glanced at The Controller, "The Controller of Great Qian? You can get lost too! I’m not in the mood to deal with you!"

"Boy, where did you learn this self-detonation trick, and what is your relationship with Immortal Fairy Eternity!"

"Jiuchong?" Immortal Fairy Eternity didn’t expect Immortal Jiuchong to suddenly appear here.

Immortal Jiuchong was stunned, looking at Immortal Fairy Eternity in shock, "That tone... it’s you, Immortal Fairy Eternity! How did you come back to life?"

"Not now, it’s not the time to talk about this. I can’t stay in the outside world for too long, Silent Extermination Immortal will be looking for me..."

"You’re talking about Silent Extermination Immortal? She’s already dead."

"What?" First Immortal Fairy Eternity’s revival, then Silent Extermination Immortal’s demise, one piece of good news after another left Immortal Jiuchong unable to react at once.

"God Demon Seven Killings!" The Controller launched seven tokens, a Soul Stabilization Technique which could immobilize the opponent’s three souls and seven spirits, rendering them unable to move and at the mercy of others.

"Hey, you’re really annoying. Immortal Fairy Eternity, wait for me to deal with him, then we can talk!"

Immortal Jiuchong turned away impatiently, focusing his attention on The Controller.

With a flip of his hands, he held a small sun in his left hand, symbolizing the Supreme Yang, and a blood-stained full moon in his right, emitting Yin Energy. He clutched the sun and moon, and smashed them directly towards The Controller!

The Controller didn’t react in time at first, and only when he realized what Immortal Jiuchong was doing did he raise his Bone Staff to block the sun and moon.

The ancient records did not describe Immortal Jiuchong’s combat as close-quarter brawling.

Snow Emperor watched Immortal Jiuchong battle in the sky, and other than shock, no other expression could be seen in his pupils.

"This is impossible!"

"May I ask what’s the matter?" asked Xue Shilou, puzzled.

Only then did Snow Emperor remember that Xue Shilou was still here.

"Since you’ve passed through the three rounds of trials, there’s no harm in telling you these matters."

"Our Snow Emperor Lineage has seen a total of six Snow Emperors, and you will be the seventh."

"Although the Extreme Northern Lands regard the Snow Emperor as their faith, in reality, the Snow Emperor’s true identity is that of an Envoy for Immortal Jiuchong."

"The Envoy for Immortal Jiuchong?"

"Yes, this was the agreement made between Immortal Jiuchong and the first-generation Snow Emperor. Immortal Jiuchong resides within this wordless white jade token, while the Snow Emperor wears the token and roams about the Extreme Northern Lands collecting information from the outside world."

"And Immortal Jiuchong grants the inheritors of each generation of Snow Emperors the outline of the Yin-Yang Dao Fruit, helping them become Semi-Immortals. I am no exception."

"According to the descriptions by past Snow Emperors, in the past 300,000 years, Immortal Jiuchong has never once left the white jade token. Today, for some unknown reason, he has actually left the token and come to the outside world!"

Snow Emperor thought Xue Shilou’s wish to save Lu Yang was already outrageous, but never would he have expected Immortal Jiuchong to actually go and save Lu Yang!

"Fairy, what are you thinking about?" Lu Yang regained control of his body and noticed that the Fairy was deeply pondering something.

"Immortal Jiuchong wasn’t this kind of personality before; his manner of fighting wasn’t this unrestrained."

Chapter 1186: Chapter 1185: Extreme Northern Lands Abundant in Schizophrenia

"I never expected the Nine-layered Immortal Venerable to really take action."

The Yin Yang Qi covered the sky like a dark curtain, and the Snow Emperor sighed softly. After all, Xue Shilou would sooner or later become the next Snow Emperor; some things could be told to him now without harm.

"Actually, there are two reasons why the Nine-layered Immortal Venerable has never left the wordless white jade token."

Upon hearing this, Meng Jingzhou couldn’t bother to pay attention to the fight in the sky anymore and hurried over to listen, dragging a small stool to the doorway.

The Snow Emperor gave Meng Jingzhou a cold glance. Following the direction indicated by the Snow Emperor, Meng Jingzhou saw no one behind him.

"There’s no one behind me, Your Excellency. It’s just us here," said Meng Jingzhou, his face reading "I am an honest child."

"I’m looking at you!" the Snow Emperor shouted, irate. You’re an outsider, why would you come over to eavesdrop on matters concerning the Snow Emperor lineage?

Ah? Was I not supposed to listen?

Seeing the Snow Emperor angered, those like Murong Grandpa and Huo Huashen, who’d also come over with a door plank, sulkily left.

"I am really one of our own." Meng Jingzhou took a book titled "Chaotic Qi, Yin and Yang, Three Talents, Four Symbols, Five Elements, Six Harmonies, Seven Luminaries, Eight Desolates, Nine Earths, Ten Heavens, Only I Am Venerated Immortal Technique" from his Identity Jade. This was the Nine-layered Immortal’s cultivation method, also known as the "Digital Immortal Skill."

His self-created Only I Am Venerated Fist was based on the Digital Immortal Skill. Technically, the Nine-layered Immortal could be considered his mentor.

"The Nine-layered Immortal Venerable’s Immortal Technique?"

The Snow Emperor was surprised; this truly was one of their own.

"Lord Snow Emperor, Fellow Daoist Meng is truly trustworthy; he would never speak a word of this to others," Xue Shilou said.

Resigned, the Snow Emperor sighed, "One reason the Venerable Immortal does not leave the white jade token is that he is avoiding an unspeakable and unknowable entity. The Immortal Venerable has always been secretive about this entity, and I, too, know nothing of it."

"The second reason is that the Immortal Venerable suffered an accident in Ancient Times, resulting in the emergence of a second personality."

"This second personality is extremely belligerent and prone to losing rationality. The Immortal Venerable fears that if his second personality takes control, it would lead to catastrophe, so he dares not leave the white jade token."

"So, it was a second personality," Lu Yang, who flew back just in time, overheard the Snow Emperor and resolved Fairy Eternity’s doubts.

Thinking about it, the Extreme Northern Lands seemed to make it easy for those he knew to have dual personalities. Xue Shilou before, Su Yuan after, and now there emerged another Nine-layered Immortal.

The Snow Emperor looked at Lu Yang, who had arrived, with a complex expression. He did not fuss over the eavesdropped conversation. If it were him facing The Controller, he would have been caught by now. Whereas Lu Yang managed to hold his own against The Controller with ease.

"The Venerable Immortal has always wanted to resolve his dual personalities issue. Hence, actually, having a dual personality is one of the conditions to become the Snow Emperor. It requires one to have had a dual personality once and then only one left, in hoping for us, generation after generation of Snow Emperors, to learn from the experience."

"...You people of the Snow Emperor lineage really do have your quirks."

In the entire Muxue City, only the Tiger Roar Martial Arts Hall had a relaxed atmosphere. The people of Muxue City were anxious about the battle between the two Immortals; a fight of this level was beyond their comprehension, impossible for them to understand.

The city lords who had come to watch knew even more, and thus, felt even more fear. Immortal beings meant mastery over certain rules; Fairies existed on a plane entirely separate from mortals, each gesture capable of altering the heavens.

They wanted to turn and run, but then they thought they would never witness another Immortal Battle in their lifetimes, so they couldn’t bring themselves to flee.

"Immortal Jiuchong, one of the Four Ancient Immortals, really has made an appearance," The Controller fought off his enemies with a Bone Staff, growing more and more excited as he fought.

Initially, when Yang Kongdong had sent him a message about Lu Yang carrying clues of the Four Ancient Immortals, he had been skeptical, suspecting that Yang Kongdong was simply fearful that The Controller would not come without such a lure, and Lu Yang’s steadfast denial made him doubtful.

Now, there was no need for doubt—Lu Yang indeed had a lead to the Four Ancient Immortals!

No, this could no longer be called just a clue. The Four Ancient Immortals they had been searching for so ardently had truly manifested!

Nowadays, day and night were one, with the day embodied by the Sun and night by the Moon; people of the world had never witnessed such a spectacle where both coexist. But there, Immortal Jiuchong stood, holding the Sun and Moon, his feet set upon the Tai Chi Diagram. In his presence, day and night, Yin and Yang, merged in stark harmony.

Upon seeing this scene, Chi Sect Leader and Elder Liu Zhen of the Yaoyang Sect couldn’t help but tremble and knelt to worship Immortal Jiuchong in the void; their sect had always esteemed the Sun as the most magnificent entity in the world.

Be it their previous ritual of sending people to the Sun or their current dedication to researching solar energy to propagate the grandeur of the Sun, it was all in honor of this belief.

And yet, the power of the Sun was but one aspect of Immortal Jiuchong’s Yin-Yang Dao Fruit.

If he proclaimed that what he held now was the true Sun, then it was indeed the true Sun!

The sky split into two at the will of Immortal Jiuchong—one side extreme Yang, and the other extreme Yin—a realm of both ice and fire.

Ancient legends spoke of the awe of the world at the event of Ten Suns hanging in the sky, but those ten suns were but ten Golden Crows—unworthy of comparison with the Sun manifested by Immortal Jiuchong.

"Go!" freēwēbηovel.c૦m

Immortal Jiuchong hurled a fireball, which illuminated brilliantly. The Controller, single-handedly forming a spell, executed an Immortal Method which existed only during the Great Qian Period and was not recorded by later generations.

"Heavenly Gang Shield!"

Thirty-six Heavenly Gangs transformed into thirty-six layers of Vajra Cover in front of The Controller. However, faced with the Sun, these shields were like rice paper—easily torn apart, and the intense flames surged directly toward The Controller.

The Controller vigorously wielded his Bone Staff to deflect the fireball, which, upon falling a thousand miles away, exploded, creating an unfathomably deep pit. A long while later the gust of the explosion roared in, followed by the sound of its impact.

Direct contact with the fireball had singed and melted the skull atop the Bone Staff, but in the next moment, the skull miraculously restored itself.

The Bone Staff, refined from his own bones after The Controller became an Immortal, was his Life-bound Magical Treasure, made of Immortal Bone, possessed of tremendous self-healing powers.

However, what The Controller had not anticipated was that Immortal Jiuchong lay behind the fireball, and after it had been deflected, what followed was a sneering Jiuchong.

Immortal Jiuchong split his body in two—one half Yang and the other Yin—each representing the most extreme forces in the world. As he struck out with both fists, it signified the meeting of Yin and Yang, resulting in a terrifying spatial collapse.

The Controller conjured mist to blur Immortal Jiuchong’s vision and seized the moment to escape, transforming his Bone Staff into armor.

The skull of the Bone Staff affixed itself onto The Controller’s head as a helmet, the spinal column extended to clasp onto his back as a backplate, and the rib sections locked onto his chest as a breastplate; in an instant, The Controller was fully armed, ready for close combat with Immortal Jiuchong.

But he knew this alone was not enough—he needed to either capture or kill Immortal Jiuchong to free up the position held by the Yin-Yang Dao Fruit.

He couldn’t accomplish this alone, so he quietly crushed the Emperor’s Token to summon the help of Mid-heaven Emperor Lord in battle.

As the Emperor’s Token shattered, a spatial vortex emerged, and Mid-heaven Emperor Lord stepped out, only to hastily retract as if he had discovered something, causing the spatial vortex to vanish without a trace, leaving both Immortal Jiuchong and The Controller confused.

At the peak of the highest snow mountain outside Muxue City, a graceful figure leaned back in the Emperor’s Chair, watching the Immortal Battle within the city. At the moment the spatial vortex disappeared, she let out a soft sigh,

"Was it because I allowed some emotional Fluctuation when I saw Mid-heaven Emperor Lord, and he sensed my presence?"

Chapter 1187: Chapter 1186: The Controller’s Dao Fruit

"Ha ha, calling for help is useless!" Although he did not know why the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord had disappeared with just one step, Immortal Jiuchong did not care too much, taking advantage of The Controller’s moment of distraction to attack first.

The Controller was still wondering why the Emperor hadn’t come over when a scorching hot fist hit him in the face, followed by an extremely cold one. The alternating hot and cold punches forced The Controller to keep retreating, blood dripping from the corners of his mouth.

Although The Controller was bleeding, his Bone Armor deflected most of the attack, and he hadn’t sustained serious injuries.

In the Great Qian Dynasty, The Controller was a civil servant, but he didn’t become The Controller just because he was eloquent. He simply did not want to bother with state affairs; otherwise, it would not have been easy for the Mid-heaven Emperor to ascend to the throne.

The Controller’s prowess in punching was unmatched, and his Immortal Blood was boiling. He vibrated both arms simultaneously, striking horizontally at Immortal Jiuchong.

Immortal Jiuchong embodied the ultimate power of yin and yang. During the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, one touch could either char someone to ash or freeze them into a crystal. However, wearing the Bone Armor on his hands, The Controller was unintimidated by trading blows with Immortal Jiuchong.

The bone spikes grew from the Bone Armor, and The Controller struck as if holding brass knuckles, causing wounds with each hit on Immortal Jiuchong’s body.

Both were supremely confident in their strength, roaring at the same time with an air of supremacy, aiming to vanquish the opponent. A terrifying aura spread broadly, and the sound of cracking bones echoed within them. However, the bones mended themselves immediately after breaking, and they continued to fight without feeling pain or fatigue.

To the unaware, it seemed both were practicing the Eternity Dao Fruit.

Immortal Jiuchong spotted a weak point in The Controller’s armor, which was also the thinner part, and decisively struck with the Yin-Yang Fruit.

However, unexpectedly, at the moment of his punch, the armor shifted bones from other parts to block the punch, rendering it ineffective.

"That’s quite interesting."

Boom—

After separating from the combat, both caught their breath, enduring pain while observing any signs of agony in their opponent’s expression.

To no avail.

Immortal Jiuchong snapped his fingers, and clusters of Immortal Fire appeared. To any cultivator with a Fire Spirit Root, it would be a great fortune. For him, it was just a matter of thought.

Then, spheres of Profound Ice followed, comparable in quality to ten million-year-old Mysterious Ice.

The cultivators of both Great Qian and Great Yu who had been in slumber till now were losing lifespan, whether it had been a few hundred or over a thousand years due to any secret technique used. However, if frozen in this Profound Ice, they would achieve an almost eternal sleep, maintaining the same lifespan even if awakened a million years later.

A sphere of Profound Ice flew towards The Controller, who deflected it with his hand, but countless clusters of Immortal Fire and Profound Ice followed, overpowering even if The Controller had three heads and six arms.

A cluster of Immortal Fire breached The Controller’s defense, but then suddenly changed direction and collided with the Profound Ice, annihilating each other.

Immortal Jiuchong’s expression tensed as that cluster of Immortal Fire had escaped his control.

Immortal Methods were not sufficient to contest with Dao Fruit. Was this the ability of The Controller’s Dao Fruit?

"Fairy, is The Controller’s Dao Fruit related to controlling objects?" Lu Yang asked, now having gained some insight into Dao Fruits to make some deductions.

In all of Muxue City, only Lu Yang could discern such intricacies. Others struggled even to keep up with the pace of the battle, let alone analyze it.

"Not quite," Fairy Eternity said with a giggle, pointing out what Lu Yang had missed.

"Look! During their close combat, when Immortal Jiuchong seized the opportunity to land a punch on The Controller, the Bone Armor blocked it, right?"

"If it were a controlling type of Dao Fruit, The Controller wouldn’t have had time to react, and neither should the armor, but that wasn’t the case."

"If I’m not wrong," the immortal Fairy continued, "The Controller possesses a Dao Fruit of Enlightenment and Spirit Awakening type, which can bestow life onto objects, command them, and the objects even have the capacity for autonomous combat."

"So that’s it."

"A controlling type of Dao Fruit?" Immortal Jiuchong reached the same conclusion as Lu Yang.

Hearing Immortal Jiuchong’s analysis, The Controller smiled subtly and began blatantly using his Dao Fruit skills. In an instant, all the Immortal Fire and Profound Ice flying towards him were spiritually awakened and turned against Immortal Jiuchong.

"Using my own moves against me?"

Immortal Jiuchong had a thought flash through his mind, conjuring the same number of Immortal Fire and Profound Ice to collide with those controlled by The Controller, causing the earth and mountains to shake within a ten-thousand-mile radius.

"Managed to block it? Not bad," The Controller said breezily, now holding the upper hand.

Immortal Jiuchong could control Immortal Fire and even manifest the Sun, but whether it was Immortal Fire or the Sun, they were tangible, and anything tangible was within The Controller’s control. How could Immortal Jiuchong make a move?

Suddenly, Immortal Jiuchong was struck by an unknown attack. The strike was powerful, sending him flying, crashing through over a dozen mountains before coming to a halt.

Where did that attack come from?!

Immortal Jiuchong quickly realized that Spiritual Energy also fell under The Controller’s control—it was an attack from the Spiritual Energy!

With that thought, Immortal Jiuchong took a deep breath, drawing the Spiritual Energy from within a thousand miles and refining it inside his body.

Immortal Jiuchong guessed that The Controller could only control non-living things; if he could control living things, he would have controlled Jiuchong’s body long ago, not just the Immortal Fire and Spiritual Energy.

So, by absorbing and refining all the Spiritual Energy, making it a part of his body, The Controller could no longer control it!

The Controller raised an eyebrow, surprised that Immortal Jiuchong, though he didn’t figure out the correct Dao Fruit, had made the right choice.

"How will you handle this now!"

With a thought from The Controller’s Immortal Sense, he enlightened the mountains surrounding Muxue City, which awoke like a giant sleeping on the ground.

The Snow Mountain Giant rose, towering ten thousand feet tall.

Immediately after, the earth swelled, forming layers of cages trapping Immortal Jiuchong.

The earth had also been enlightened by The Controller, used at his command!

Everything under heaven and earth was within The Controller’s scope of control!

The battlefield shifted outside the city, and those daring cultivators in the city left Muxue City en masse to follow and watch the battle.

They watched in awe as one snow mountain after another, under The Controller’s summons, stood like people upon the earth.

Yun Zhi, looking down at the quaking, awakening snow mountains beneath her feet, shook her head helplessly, packed up the Emperor’s Chair, and jumped down from the mountain to find a spot unaffected by the tumult to watch the battle.

"Earth Snow Mountains? Merely mundane objects daring to trap an immortal!" Immortal Jiuchong bellowed, his body shuddering as he broke free like a dragon escaping its chains, shattering the earthly shackles and knocking over a Snow Mountain Giant with a punch.

The Snow Mountain Giant, headless, fell to the ground, causing it to shake.

"Mundane objects, you say? Then take a look at these!"

As Immortal Jiuchong smashed the head of a Snow Mountain Giant, a metallic, lustrous humanoid figure flew out from within, slamming Jiuchong into the ground!

Boom—

The heavens shattered, the earth exploded, and a large blast erupted underground. The humanoid figure was sent flying by a punch from Immortal Jiuchong, who then burst forth from the soil.

Yet, after taking a heavy punch from Immortal Jiuchong, the humanoid figure remained intact, only bearing a fist imprint.

"Immortal Gold?" Immortal Jiuchong frowned.

This was not a magic artifact crafted from Immortal Gold; The Controller didn’t have the assets of a Yingtian Immortal; it was merely raw Immortal Gold. However, this piece of Immortal Gold, enlightened by The Controller, could be referred to as a living Immortal Gold entity, terribly hard.

"Always able to surprise me with something unexpected," Immortal Jiuchong sneered.

"But you surely don’t think my Yin-Yang Dao Fruit can only control Immortal Fire and Profound Ice, do you?"

Chapter 1188: Chapter 1178: The True Abilities of the Yin-Yang Dao Fruit

"Blustering!"

The Controller remained steadfast, unshaken by the verbal provocation of his opponent. Countless Snow Mountain Giants rose from the ground, kneeling before him in submission, and then the earth gave birth to numerous agile stone pillars, as flexible as the tentacles of an octopus.

Immortal Jiuchong’s fist knocked down a Snow Mountain Giant, but immediately afterward, a being made of Immortal Gold, hiding inside the giant’s head, launched a sneak attack on Immortal Jiuchong.

The Snow Mountain Giants were merely a distraction, the real trick lay in the beings made of Immortal Gold hidden inside!

These pieces of Immortal Gold were unrefined and lacked the might of Immortal Artifacts, but Immortal Gold itself is renowned for its strength. The Yingtian Immortal even used Immortal Gold to forge his body, demonstrating how terrifyingly hard Immortal Gold could be.

Immortal Jiuchong’s fist left an imprint on the face of the Immortal Gold being, yet it caused no substantial damage!

Immortal Jiuchong intended to leap into the air, but from the ground, a segment of a tree branch, acting like a tentacle, sprung up and entwined around his ankle. This was a heavenly tree from countless Suiyues ago, frozen within the permafrost, now brought to life by the command of The Controller.

Beneath the lands of the Extreme Northern Lands lay buried countless corpses, all within the range of The Controller’s animating powers.

Though Immortal Jiuchong immediately broke free from the grasp of the tree branch tentacle, it provided an opportunity for the beings of Immortal Gold.

Three to five Immortal Gold beings swarmed forward, pinning down Immortal Jiuchong’s limbs, with one sitting atop Jiuchong and punching his face repeatedly, each blow strong enough to smash a Pass Tribulation Cultivator to death.

Immortal Jiuchong instantly transformed into a being of flame, corporeal yet intangible, passing through the beings of Immortal Gold.

"Refine!"

Immortal Jiuchong bellowed, and his Immortal Fire enveloped the Immortal Gold beings. His Immortal Fire was most suited for refining Immortal Gold; in the Ancient Times, even the Yingtian Immortal borrowed his fire to forge Immortal Artifacts.

In an instant, the Immortal Gold beings were melted into a liquid mass.

Whoosh—

A blob of liquid flew out from the flames toward Immortal Jiuchong.

Even when transformed into liquid, the Immortal Gold beings remained under The Controller’s animation, still obeying his commands to attack Immortal Jiuchong by all means necessary.

Immortal Jiuchong rapidly retreated, knowing that if the liquid Immortal Gold beings surrounded and then solidified around him, he would be trapped in an impenetrable cage of Immortal Gold, which would be quite troublesome.

Simultaneously, he extinguished his own Immortal Fire used for refining the Immortal Gold beings before The Controller could commandeer it.

The Controller clicked his tongue. Indeed, as an Ancient True Immortal, Jiuchong’s reaction was impressively swift.

The Immortal Gold beings, now liquid, took on various shapes, extending indefinitely and forming an exceedingly thin layer that adhered to the bodiless Snow Mountain Giants.

The Immortal Gold solidified into a layer of armor for the Snow Mountain Giants, granting them the strength to battle Immortal Jiuchong.

One by one, the Snow Mountain Giants pounded their chests, resembling headless great apes.

The Controller then procured Mystic Ice, which Immortal Jiuchong had manifested during their earlier confrontation but had not yet been fully consumed.

The Mystic Ice, too, was alive, and at The Controller’s bidding, it morphed into ice spears, becoming weapons for the Snow Mountain Giants.

Now armed with armor and weapons, the Snow Mountain Giants surged forward, attacking Immortal Jiuchong, their Mystic Ice Spears posing a real threat to Jiuchong in his fiery form.

A Mystic Ice Spear pierced Immortal Jiuchong’s body, momentarily giving him a corporeal form, and seizing the opportunity, countless Snow Mountain Giants pinned him down and hammered him into the ground, where a vortex appeared, swallowing Immortal Jiuchong whole.

Then, the earth heaved and cracked, fissures emanating light, followed by a surge of fire that blasted apart the numerous Snow Mountain Giants, akin to a volcanic eruption—a doomsday scene never to be witnessed in the Extreme Northern Lands.

Faced with the wrath of Immortal Jiuchong, The Controller remained undeterred, continuing to order the Snow Mountain Giants to assault.

Immortal Jiuchong hovered in the air, consumed by towering anger.

Suddenly, an illusory chessboard appeared on the ground, immensely vast, with each Snow Mountain Giant positioned within a square.

What is this about!

The Controller became alert, for there was no mention in the ancient texts of Immortal Jiuchong possessing such a technique!

"All things in this world can be divided into black and white."

"The Snow Mountain belongs to the Yin Attribute."

Immortal Jiuchong’s voice boomed, as if speaking to himself. Aside from Fairy Eternity and Eldest Senior Sister, no one understood what he meant.

As Immortal Jiuchong’s words echoed, a very inconspicuous black chess piece appeared above the heads of the Snow Mountain Giants.

Immortal Jiuchong’s index finger and middle finger were stacked together, pinching a white chess piece.

The white piece fell, overlapping with the black piece above the head of the Snow Mountain Giant, where black and white collided, mutually dissolving each other.

The bi-colored chess pieces disappeared, and astonishingly, the Snow Mountain Giant also vanished into thin air.

"In this world where there is Yin, there must be Yang. Yin and Yang generate each other, and they also conquer each other."

The Controller stumbled backward, finally understanding what Immortal Jiuchong had done.

Yin and Yang generate and overcome each other. The Snow Mountain Giant was a creature of Yin attributes. When it came into contact with an equal amount of Yang attributes, Yin and Yang collided, and both would be annihilated!

"No, the Snow Mountain Giant is a creature of the Five Elements. How could it be divided by Yin and Yang?" The Controller still had some confusion.

Immortal Jiuchong burst into laughter, taking steps closer to The Controller.

"The Dao Fruit represents the rules. Before the emergence of the Yin-Yang Dao Fruit, it wasn’t clear whether the things in this world were categorized according to the Five Elements or Yin and Yang."

"But now that my Yin-Yang Dao Fruit has appeared, everything in this world is classified by Yin and Yang. The division by the Five Elements is merely a more detailed classification based on the division of Yin and Yang!"

In other words, these are the rules set by the Yin-Yang Dao Fruit!

Immortal Jiuchong realized that The Controller did not control the Dao Fruit of authority; he couldn’t possibly manipulate so many Snow Mountain Giants for precise attacks. Instead, he possessed Dao Fruits related to imparting life or awakening spirits.

But in his presence, it didn’t matter.

The Controller’s face turned pale. Originally, he could animate all things, even Immortal Fire and Profound Ice. He thought he could restrain Immortal Jiuchong,

However, the reality was starkly different. Immortal Jiuchong prescribed the rules for Yin and Yang, allowing annihilation of Yin and Yang, which was actually what suppressed The Controller!

"I want to see how much you can annihilate!"

The Controller activated the Dao Fruit of awakening spirits. The earth shook, people of Muxue City stumbled left and right, thinking it was an earthquake.

Those high-level cultivators turned pale; this was definitely not as simple as an earthquake!

The entire Extreme Northern Lands were in turmoil, with the first change appearing around The Controller.

Beneath his feet, the ground rose, not becoming giants or such, but transformed into an earthen sphere covered with snow and ice.

Muxue City was also on this earthen sphere!

The sphere was incredibly large; standing upon it, one could not even feel its curvature!

The people of Muxue City did not understand the meaning of this earthen sphere, and even the high-level cultivators had a vague concept of it. Lu Yang, however, couldn’t be clearer.

Nowadays, all six continents were forged from star planets. The Controller made the earth come alive, reverting it to its original, primitive planetary form!

The Controller could use these star planets to strike at Immortal Jiuchong at any time.

"So what if they are star planets!" scoffed Immortal Jiuchong. In the Ancient Times, battles would easily shatter stars; what threat could these few planets pose?

He could even use Yin and Yang to counter each other and make these planets disappear.

"No, there are people on the planets!" Immortal Jiuchong’s true personality cried out. The Controller was threatening to use the lives of the Extreme Northern Lands.

"So what!" the other personality of Immortal Jiuchong was unmoved, which was exactly what his true personality feared.

"Let me control the body!" The true personality of Immortal Jiuchong wrestled for control of the body.

The Controller sneered, eager to see what else Immortal Jiuchong could do.

Immortal Jiuchong took a couple of deep breaths; it had been a long time since he had used this move.

"Extreme Yin Cold!"

Immortal Jiuchong opened his Yin Domain. The already cold temperatures of the Extreme Northern Lands fell further and further, dropping to a point that had never been seen before in history.

Absolute Zero!

It was as if the world froze in that moment. All living beings in the Extreme Northern Lands were immobilized, the land itself no longer transforming into a planet, the entire realm of the Extreme Northern Lands was enveloped by absolute zero. Under absolute zero, no object could move, resulting in an effect akin to a halt in time!

"See what I mean, what did I tell you? Controlling Immortal Fire and such, these are merely superficial abilities of the Yin-Yang Dao Fruit. These are the true powers."

Chapter 1189: Chapter 1188: Hush Money

Immortal Jiuchong’s technique wasn’t a true halting of time, he could only cause an area to enter Absolute Zero, where time in the Extreme Northern Lands comes to a stop while the rest of the continent continues as normal.

The range of the Time Immortal’s time stop encompassed the whole world.

Seeing the situation take a turn for the worse, The Controller turned and ran.

All his methods had been countered by Immortal Jiuchong, the battle was going poorly, and if not now, then when?

"Not good, he’s trying to escape!" Lu Yang shouted. A battle between Immortals, even if one could determine the victor, it was hard to seal one’s fate; if one wanted to flee, the other could hardly stop them.

However, Lu Yang quickly relaxed, although Eldest Senior Sister had not made a move, she must have arrived by now.

With Eldest Senior Sister here, Immortal Jiuchong was sure not to escape.

"Why call that Miss Yun for help? We, the Five Ancient Immortals, are enough to catch someone." Fairy Eternity would rather ask the Four Ancient Immortals for help than seek Miss Yun’s assistance.

"Fairy, are you sure Immortal Jiuchong can catch someone?"

"Of course, Immortal Jiuchong alone can’t manage it, but I can call for help."

"Little Yang, go out and shout ’Yingtian Immortal is petty’ a couple of times, and Yingtian Immortal will come over."

"Yingtian Immortal has always been like this; he could sense anyone who cursed him, but then Ashy Bean was around, Yingtian Immortal didn’t dare to tune in, but now that Ashy Bean’s gone, his senses have restored."

"...Fairy, wouldn’t it still be better to ask Eldest Senior Sister to help catch the person?" After some deliberation, Lu Yang felt that catching a Daqian Immortal wasn’t worth risking his own small life.

"Oh, what are you afraid of, with me protecting you, nothing will go wrong!" Fairy Eternity held her small chin up and gave her chest a confident pat.

A subject must obey when the emperor commands his death; without any other choice, Lu Yang left the spiritual world and whispered a sentence.

"Yingtian Immortal is petty..."

Crack—

Absolute silence reigned in the Absolute Zero domain of the Extreme Northern Lands, the sudden sound of thunder was terribly conspicuous.

Thunder tore through the void, and Yingtian Immortal, constructed of lightning, appeared in front of Lu Yang, his expression somewhat unfriendly.

"Kid, was it you who called me petty?"

"This..." Lu Yang’s forehead broke out in sweat, stammering. Yingtian Immortal had arrived too quickly; wasn’t this very pettiness?

Fairy Eternity stepped forward to back up Lu Yang, protecting him as though she were shielding a small chick: "It was I who cursed, what of it?"

Yingtian Immortal’s expression shifted then settled into a smile, he chuckled sheepishly: "I was wondering who was reminding me to be careful, and it turns out to be you, Fairy Eternity."

It was only now that Yingtian Immortal noticed something amiss, this was the domain of Absolute Zero, also detecting the chase high in the sky, he noticed the dueling sides.

"Immortal Jiuchong and The Controller?"

At the same time, he looked at Lu Yang in astonishment; how come you’re at the scene again, kid?

"You first help Immortal Jiuchong." Fairy Eternity urged.

Yingtian Immortal nodded and flew towards the sky.

"Ying Tian?"

Immortal Jiuchong wasn’t surprised by the arrival of Yingtian Immortal; that thunderclap made it obvious someone had cursed Yingtian Immortal, announcing the arrival of his Thunder Clone.

"Another one?!" The Controller couldn’t help but glance back while frantically escaping, almost cursing out loud.

Those Four Ancient Immortals they couldn’t find no matter how hard they looked before, how come two have suddenly turned up in such a short span?

Was what Yang Kongdong said true, that this place had clues to the Four Ancient Immortals? But these clues were just too many.

"Let’s join forces and catch him."

"Alright!"

The two had known each other since Ancient Times, and although both had suspected each other of being body-snatched by some mastermind behind the scenes, with no contact for three hundred thousand years, they set aside their past grievances in the face of a common enemy and joined forces to capture the foe.

Ying Tian Immortal’s Thunder Clone was unbelievably fast, intercepting The Controller in the blink of an eye.

The Controller tried to escape in a different direction but was intercepted by Immortal Jiuchong.

"Thunder Tribulation..." Ying Tian Immortal was about to habitually summon the Thunder Tribulation to deal with The Controller when Immortal Jiuchong stopped him.

"Don’t use Thunder Tribulation, his Dao Fruit ability is Enlightenment!"

Ying Tian Immortal decisively abandoned the summoning of Thunder Tribulation, and the two tacitly used their physical bodies to fight.

The Controller had managed to fight Immortal Jiuchong to a standstill only because of the added strength from his bone armor, but now with Ying Tian Immortal joining in, there was no chance for resistance.

Before long, Immortal Jiuchong and Ying Tian Immortal were dragging The Controller back to Muxue City, his many ornaments having fallen off during the fight, lost somewhere, now resembling a plucked rooster.

The Controller did not understand why the two were taking him back to Muxue City.

"Done!"

The two threw The Controller to the ground, and Immortal Fairy emerged from Lu Yang’s body, boasting triumphantly.

"How about that, now you know how formidable we Five Ancient Immortals are, right?"

Then she bragged to Lu Yang, "See, what did I tell you? We didn’t even need Miss Yun to lift a finger to deal with this ’Death Life’ or whatever!"

"It’s The Controller," Lu Yang corrected her.

The Controller stared in alarm at Immortal Fairy, not understanding what she meant by the "Five Ancient Immortals."

Wasn’t it the Four Ancient Immortals?

"So that’s it, I didn’t realize the Tribulation Dao Fruit could be used like this." A familiar voice came from behind Ying Tian Immortal, frightening Ying Tian Immortal so much that he almost dissipated his Thunder Clone.

"Eldest Senior Sister!"

"You did well," said Yun Zhi, nodding.

No one knew that what Yun Zhi truly appreciated wasn’t the capturing of The Controller but Lu Yang’s ability to solve Yang Kongdong on his own.

From initially needing her help when facing a Transcendance Tribulation Stage enemy, to now being able to stand on his own, resolving a Semi-Immortal by himself, was indeed remarkable progress.

The Controller looked at Yun Zhi in disbelief, finally understanding why the Emperor had stepped forward only to retreat immediately.

So this terrifying existence that could even chill the Emperor’s spine was also in the Extreme Northern Lands.

"Let’s get this clear, I am the one who caught this person!" Immortal Fairy quickly spoke up as Yun Zhi seemed about to take The Controller away.

"... Fairy, can this capture really be counted as yours?" Lu Yang couldn’t help but tease.

Immortal Fairy declared righteously, "Whoever is caught through my connections is considered a capture by me."

"What exactly do you want, Senior Fairy? Do you want to become Sect Leader?" Yun Zhi was curious too, not understanding why Immortal Fairy put so much emphasis on this.

Capturing an Immortal to tally Contribution Points, then exchanging them for a Sect Leader voucher, would probably be a process calculated in tens of thousands of years.

Immortal Fairy waved her hand dismissively, "I don’t want to be any Sect Leader. This is hush money."

Immortal Fairy’s words left everyone present scratching their heads.

"Hush money?"

Yun Zhi repeated the words and chuckled inside, guessing Immortal Fairy’s intention—she probably didn’t want people to know she could restore her Immortal strength at any time.

Or perhaps, was it a thank-you gift for not telling Junior Brother about this? Was Senior Fairy too embarrassed to say it out loud?

Imagining Senior Fairy’s internal struggling and reluctance brought an unusual smile to Yun Zhi’s face. She shook her head with a laugh, "Then I’ll accept this hush money."

"No laughing allowed!" Immortal Fairy became furious and stomped her foot in annoyance.

Immortal Jiuchong, Ying Tian Immortal, Yun Zhi’s Junior Brother, the Immortal Lineage’s Second Boss, a High Minister and the Emperor’s Master of the Great Bean Dynasty, Young Sect Master of the Heavenly Court Sect, Speechless Daoist’s disciple, and a peerless Sword Cultivator all exchanged looks, utterly confused by the situation.

Chapter 1190: Chapter 189 The Second Battle between Immortal Jiuchong and The Controller

"Jiuchong, what are your plans? Are you still planning to stay inside this white jade token?"

After successfully sending The Controller away as hush money, Immortal Fairy Eternity was in high spirits.

"Has Jiuchong been staying in the wordless white jade token all these years?"

At this moment, the Extreme Northern Lands were still in the Absolute Zero Domain, and everyone was frozen like ice sculptures, motionless, even the Snow Emperor was no exception, frozen solid. Yingtian Immortal curiously observed the white jade token hanging on the Snow Emperor’s chest, feeling as if their fates were somewhat similar.

Both were forced to hide in the Small World space after the fall of the Fire Dynasty.

"Now that Silent Extermination Immortal is gone, there’s no need for Jiuchong to stay here, right?"

Even if the holder of the Seven Emotions Dao Fruit Embryo disappears, this shadow will always exist because the issue lies with ’me,’ not with the ’Seven Emotions Dao Fruit Embryo.’"

"That personality only knows battle, is extremely belligerent, and doesn’t care about the lives of others. If it weren’t for me stopping him just now, I’m afraid he might have obliterated all the stars in the Extreme Northern Lands, and the entire region would have perished."

Yingtian Immortal hissed, this indeed was a big problem. If something like this happened, I’m afraid Yun Zhi would take you down before you could defeat The Controller.

"Extremely belligerent?" Yingtian Immortal stroked his chin, thinking of a way to help his good brother, "Has that personality ever fought Silent Extermination Immortal?"

Immortal Jiuchong sighed, "He fought during the time of the Fire Dynasty. He nearly became the dominant personality, and I would have become the subordinate one. Knowing that he couldn’t defeat Silent Extermination Immortal, he voluntarily gave up control of the body to me. That’s how I have managed to suppress him for the past three hundred thousand years."

"If he loves fighting so much, could he defeat Daoist Yun Zhi?" Yingtian Immortal was curious.

As soon as Yingtian Immortal spoke, the normally amiable expressions of Immortal Jiuchong changed, becoming coarse and angry, and he looked at Yingtian Immortal with a cold sneer, "Ying Tian, after three hundred thousand years, I didn’t expect you to ask such a foolish question!"

The belligerent and angry personality once again took control of Immortal Jiuchong’s body!

Yingtian Immortal seemed to answer his own question, as if introducing an opponent to his good brother, "Although Daoist Yun Zhi hasn’t been cultivating for a long time, she holds the position of Eldest Senior Sister among the younger generation in the Sect and her master has just reached the Transcendance Tribulation Stage. She hasn’t learned much from her master, and I’ve exchanged a few moves with her myself, still manageable to fight."

"Oh? It seems this young girl really has something!" Immortal Jiuchong perked up at this, as his fight with The Controller hadn’t been satisfying, and he wanted to continue the fight.

With that said, Immortal Jiuchong immediately took up a stance, causing Yun Zhi’s brow to furrow, "Are you going to fight me here?"

This is Muxue City, where everything is in a state of Absolute Zero. If you break something, nobody can fix it. freёweɓnovel.com

Immortal Jiuchong cursed loudly, "You little brat, rambling on and nitpicking. If it’s a fight you want, just fight. Why pick the place...!"

Bang—

Yun Zhi grabbed The Controller, her launch like a cannonball, creating a sonic boom that shattered the Tiger Roar Martial Arts Hall.

Lu Yang shivered at the sight. Immortal Jiuchong’s careless words had clearly enraged Eldest Senior Sister; otherwise, she wouldn’t have caused such a major commotion.
