Immortal Jiuchong hovered mid-air, surrounded by countless flames of Immortal Fire and Profound Ice, like stars orbiting around him, protecting Immortal Jiuchong.

Not to mention the Profound Ice, but these Immortal Fires alone could melt the glaciers in the Extreme Northern Lands and turn them into a vast ocean!

"Go!"

Immortal Jiuchong, like an emperor commanding fire and ice, led the charge against Yun Zhi. The trailing Immortal Fire and Profound Ice painted a brilliant trail, reminiscent of the Flying Sky Map from Ancient Times. Wherever it passed, icebergs melted only to be frozen in that moment!

Confronted with the ferocious charge of Immortal Jiuchong, Yun Zhi glanced at her empty left hand, capable of unleashing the Cloud Falling Palm, and then at her right hand holding The Controller. She decisively charged toward Immortal Jiuchong with The Controller in tow.

Both Immortal Jiuchong and The Controller were shocked.

Originally, Yun Zhi hadn’t planned on bringing The Controller into the fight, but if she left with Immortal Jiuchong, only Junior Brother, the Fairy predecessors, and Yingtian Immortal would be left in Muxue City, making it all too easy for The Controller to escape.

Junior Brother went without saying; he wasn’t a match for The Controller yet.

The Fairy predecessor was still recovering from serious injuries. If forced to suddenly regain her strength, she would likely end up further injured and then squatting in Junior Brother’s Spiritual Space for three hundred years.

Yingtian Immortal had only sent a Thunder Clone, with half the usual power. Single-handedly, he most certainly couldn’t beat The Controller.

The Controller, bombarded by the Immortal Fire and Profound Ice, cried out in pain and then collided head-on with Immortal Jiuchong!

Even Immortal Jiuchong, courageous and battle-skilled as he was, hadn’t expected Yun Zhi’s move and was immediately dazed.

Yun Zhi didn’t care about Immortal Jiuchong’s reaction; she lifted The Controller and struck again!

Immortal Jiuchong crossed his arms in front of his chest to block but didn’t anticipate the great force and heavy momentum behind The Controller’s strike. It exceeded his ability to defend, and once again he was sent flying, piercing through countless stars in the process.

Immortal Jiuchong was fast, but Yun Zhi was faster. She appeared in his path and hit him with The Controller again, not giving him a chance to catch his breath.

Even Immortal Jiuchong, confident in his Immortal Body, couldn’t withstand such high-frequency, intense attacks. He soon swelled up with bruises.

"Huff, huff—"

Facing another attack from Yun Zhi, Immortal Jiuchong split into Yin Body and Yang Body to dodge the strike, then merged back together.

"I didn’t expect you, little girl, to know how to use The Controller as your weapon. Fighting while armed against an unarmed opponent is hardly honorable. If you’re capable, fight me bare-handed!"

If Yun Zhi had been wielding an Immortal Artifact, Immortal Jiuchong could have obliterated it with the Yin-Yang Dao Fruit. But her weapon was The Controller—an Immortal’s Body. No matter how powerful the Yin-Yang Dao Fruit was, it couldn’t annihilate an Immortal outright, so using The Controller as her weapon was quite troublesome for Immortal Jiuchong.

Yun Zhi thought Immortal Jiuchong made sense, so she switched to using her left hand to fight.

"Cloud Falling Palm."

Chapter 1191: Chapter 1190: Tiger Roar Martial Arts Hall Emerges Anew

"Heh, young people are just too young, so easily baited by provocation!"

Immortal Jiuchong laughed uproariously. Now that Yun Zhi had voluntarily given up the Controller, a weapon she was adept at using, how could she be his opponent!

"Mountains without bounds, sun and moon alternate!"

A majestic scene appeared above Immortal Jiuchong’s head, with mountains, rivers, lakes, and seas all vividly present; even the sun and moon hung high, marking the passage of time.

To the casual observer, it would appear as a piece of space cut from the Central Continent, but upon contact, one would realize it was an endless world evolved from Immortal Fire and Profound Ice by Immortal Jiuchong. Touching it would trigger the interplay of yin and yang, bursting forth with endless Primordial Qi!

This move was one of his trump cards. He had not dared to use it during the fight with the Controller, fearing the Controller might enlighten this endless world.

But fighting against an unarmed Yun Zhi, there was no need for such concerns.

Finally, as an observer, the Controller identified the impressive power of this move. Once it struck the ground, the Extreme Northern Lands would transform into a realm of both fire and ice.

How would Yun Zhi respond?

"Cloud Falling Palm."

The large, fluffy hand seemed like a cloud plucked from the sky, and that cloud hand grasped onto the world of Immortal Fire and Profound Ice.

An explosion was heard within the hand, stained with varying colors of Immortal Fire and Profound Ice, the colors changing continuously as if a dye vat had been overturned.

A tiny bit of the explosion leaked between the fingers, directly piercing through the Extreme Northern Lands, down to the world’s deepest layer.

One could only imagine the true explosive power of the world of Immortal Fire and Profound Ice.

But besides that, no more explosive force leaked out.

Seeing this, Immortal Jiuchong’s expression drastically changed. He also could not comprehend how Yun Zhi’s combat power could have increased without using the Controller as a weapon.

"Cloud Falling Palm."

"Nine Layer Ice Shield!"

Facing the second Cloud Falling Palm, Immortal Jiuchong immediately constructed an absolute defense with Profound Ice. The Nine Layer Ice Shield, his strongest defensive technique, stacked together.

A pleasing cracking sound, like a musical instrument accompanying the battle, resonated as the layers of ice shields were penetrated. The shattered ice cascaded down like a shower, and Immortal Jiuchong, along with the ice shards, became embedded in the snowy ground!

Struggling to climb out of the frozen hole, Immortal Jiuchong then saw the third palm strike bearing down on him.

"This body is returned to you!" Not daring to face Yun Zhi head-on, the belligerent personality returned control of the body to Immortal Jiuchong without a word.

"Why give it back to me at this time!" Immortal Jiuchong was panicked, relinquishing control of his own body. Just what was Yun Zhi’s background, and how exactly had the Yingtian Immortal managed to exchange blows with her!?

"Why do you care so much, just take it when I give it to you!"

"I said I don’t want it!"

The belligerent personality and Immortal Jiuchong pushed against each other, each yielding body control.

The Cloud Falling Palm descended, and peace returned to the world.

The Controller swallowed hard. No wonder the Emperor ran upon seeing Yun Zhi. If the Emperor had been a step slower earlier, they both might have been left behind by Yun Zhi.

"Cloud Falling..."

Lu Yang flew above Muxue City to observe the battle.

Other areas were shattered by Daoist Yun Zhi, the spirituality of the Heaven and Earth Treasures vibrated into dispersal, so it was impossible to tell what materials were used elsewhere.

If the doors are made from Ten-thousand-year-old Coiled Dragon Wood, wouldn’t the materials used for the rest of the building be similarly valuable?

Over the past thirty thousand years, the Snow Emperor’s rule spanned six generations, accumulating countless treasures. Immortal Jiuchong took out various precious Heaven and Earth Treasures from the Snow Emperor’s wordless white jade token and clanged away as he began construction.

Yingtian Immortal meticulously listed the construction materials: beams made of Thunder Tribulation Punishment Wood, roofing tiles fired from Soil of Rest, bricks refined from Five-colored Soil...

Soon, Tiger Roar Martial Arts Hall was fitted with the main doors and restored to its original state.

Young Master Meng didn’t find it strange at all to see Immortal Jiuchong and The Controller here after seeing Eldest Senior Sister.

What do you mean there’s no more Snow Emperor?

And the martial arts hall itself.

Chapter 1192: Chapter 1191: Elder Brother Dai, We Have Brought Back the Concerned Party (Seeking Monthly Votes)

Tiger Roar Martial Arts Hall was built by Uncle Murong himself; he was intimately familiar with every brick and tile.

Even though the Martial Arts Hall looked exactly the same as before, something just didn’t feel right.

Never mind, he thought, Uncle Murong had reached the Golden Core Stage thanks to his carefree nature—if something didn’t make sense, he wouldn’t dwell on it. There was no point in torturing oneself.

"Uncle, Old Meng and I have been talking, and we think it’s about time we left," Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou came to bid farewell to Uncle Murong.

Although they would have liked to continue teaching at the hall, too much had happened in Muxue City, and it was only proper to return to their sect to report. Moreover, only these brothers fully knew the details of the incidents.

Besides, now that the people of Muxue City were aware of the brothers’ identities, staying would only bring trouble to Uncle Murong.

"Ah, you’re leaving?" Uncle Murong said, feeling melancholy. He knew about Lu Yang and his companion’s real identities, but what left the deepest impression on him were the instructors Little Lu and Little Meng.

"We’ll come back to visit you."

Uncle Murong shook his head with a wry smile, "What’s there to visit me for? You two are busy people. It’s the thought that counts."

He could already imagine the students’ disappointed faces after the New Year when they found out their teachers were gone. He would have to find a way to console them then.

Finding a teacher on the same level would be difficult, but if no one could beat him, he could teach too.

What Uncle Murong didn’t know was that Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, and Xue Shilou had entered the students’ dreams at night, bidding farewell to each one, telling them to keep training hard, and that what their instructors had taught was enough to last them a lifetime.

The students cried in their sleep and woke up with puffy eyes, realizing it hadn’t been a dream.

The four youngsters—Gong Che, Shi Yi, Fang Zhige, and Su Yuan—were the most mature. When they learned that Mr. Lu was actually Lu Yang, they had anticipated this outcome, yet when it came to pass, they still found it difficult to accept.

"The Snow Emperor is no longer with us, but you can still be considered my successor. Will you follow me in cultivation?" The Snow Emperor asked earnestly. It had been eighty thousand years since he found someone to pass on his mantle. Now, with Xue Shilou as a promising disciple, it was time to nurture him well.

"I am willing!" Xue Shilou kowtowed three times and offered the Snow Emperor tea, bringing laughter to the venerable man.

Lu Yang remembered something and headed to the backyard. He found Old Ma standing straight, packing away dried herbs. Once they left the Extreme Northern Lands, they wouldn’t be able to find such herbs again.

It wasn’t Old Ma that Lu Yang was reminded of, but rather the tree by his room’s door.

Under the tree, he found the body of Yang Kongdong, which was being gnawed—or perhaps digested—by the tree’s roots.

Lu Yang was startled. When had the tree become so malevolent?

He had only fed it the corpses of a Foundation Establishment Stage Luo Shi and a Divinity Transformation Stage Carefree Guest.

"The lingering obsession of Leng Ningxiang must have attached to the tree after it dissipated," Fairy Eternity analyzed. "In a way, she and Yang Kongdong are together forever now."

"It might seem sinister, but there shouldn’t be any issues once Yang Kongdong’s body is consumed."

The more professional Controller also came to analyze, "This tree could be considered as having gained enlightenment, or one might say it’s a form of reincarnation, unrelated to its past life."

"When the tree truly develops spiritual wisdom, it will be a completely new being."

Lu Yang roughly understood, but he was more concerned about another issue: "Is there a danger to the Martial Arts Hall?"

The Controller shook his head, "No danger. If the hall takes good care of this tree, it can protect the hall until the tree grows legs and transforms."

"That’s good then."

"An earthquake in the Extreme Northern Lands?" Dai Bufan couldn’t make heads nor tails of the intelligence just received.

Due to its vastness with sparse population and relative isolation, he seldom paid attention to the happenings in the Extreme Northern Lands.

Even so, he knew that earthquakes had never occurred there before.

"Elder Brother Dai, we’re back!"

Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, the two heroes, triumphantly returned, having been rushed back by Old Ma, who pulled both men and a cart full of immortals frantically back to report.

Although their gains from the Extreme Northern Lands were significant, they were still disciples of the Seek Dao Sect, and Lu Yang was a junior brother under Dai Bufan. Any achievements they had made outside had to be reported back to Dai Bufan.

"You two are back from the Extreme Northern Lands?"

Dai Bufan was surprised and, seeing the joyous smiles on Lu Yang and his companion, he was reminded of how Junior Sister Gan Tian looked when she had returned from the Demon Territory, a sign that her cultivation had been fruitful and she had made a big harvest in the Demon Territory.

"It seems like you two have made quite a significant harvest in the Extreme Northern Lands?"

"Elder Brother Dai, you’re as perceptive as a deity!" Lu Yang gave a thumbs-up, genuinely impressed.

"Tell me, what did you two do in the Extreme Northern Lands?"

Listening to others’ worldly experiences could aid one’s own cultivation – a lesson Dai Bufan had learned during his Void Refinement days, and it was still applicable now.

"Elder Brother Dai, as you know, we’ve always advocated for cultivating discreetly and ’Red Dust Mortality,’ so Old Meng and I chose to teach fist techniques to students at a martial arts hall as teachers..."

"The Martial Arts Hall’s master’s cultivation level wasn’t high, just at the early stage of Golden Core. He didn’t know our identities."

"The students were all ordinary people, but of course, there were a few exceptions..."

Dai Bufan nodded frequently as he listened; it sounded credible. The Eldest Senior Sister had said that Junior Brother Lu went to the Extreme Northern Lands to temper himself, but it seems that Eldest Senior Sister could also make mistakes in her judgment – Junior Brother Lu went there to live a mortal life.

Weren’t they just talking about holding classes? How did it jump to the Ruthless Sect’s leader?

Others at the Void Refinement Stage either immersed in ’Red Dust Mortality’ or lived by ’War Feeds War,’ yet it seems you two have chosen ’Red Dust Fuels War’?

You’d better say the same when Eldest Senior Sister comes back.

Lu Yang stood silently at the doorway, pondering whether life at Captive Peak was too dull, as the prisoners had begun to talk nonsense.

The Controller had known about the existence of newspapers since his time in the Fairy Palace, but he didn’t know Guan Shanhai was the one who printed them.

The blatant arrogance of the Great Yu power was one reason why Lu Yang had asked Guan Shanhai to print newspapers.

Lu Yang nodded, gesturing for the Controller to continue.

They won’t need the broadcasting Array Method to produce sound, and after my enlightenment, the newspapers will possess a degree of spiritual wisdom. Should a commoner want to hear a specific part of the newspaper, they merely need to speak to it, and the paper will recite it automatically!"

"If commoners wish to learn to read, the enlightened newspapers can also teach them how!"

Lu Yang hissed in astonishment, seeing this as a potential idea. If feasible, the literacy rate in Great Xia, or perhaps the entire world, would dramatically increase.

Lu Yang took out a copy of the newspaper Guan Shanhai had printed and let the Controller enlighten it. Indeed, as the Controller described, it became more user-friendly.

Moreover, Enlightenment was an ability of the Controller’s Dao Fruit, which even Guan Shanhai couldn’t replicate.

In other words, to enlighten all the newspapers, the power of the Controller would be necessary.

Guan Shanhai remained silent throughout, merely looking at the Controller through the bars of the cage.

Truly, a formidable foe, the Main Priest of the Great Qian Dynasty!

Chapter 1200: Chapter 1199: Something in the Sun

However, suppressing the cultivation levels of prisoners and allowing them to move freely is a viable idea.

Take, for example, the Restraining Light Treasure Box of the Laurel Fairy Palace. Any cultivator within the box has their realm suppressed to the same level, and Fairy Eternity once possessed herself, using the Restraining Light Treasure Box to challenge the Sect Leaders of the Five Great Immortal Sects.

To suppress an Immortal, the Restraining Light Treasure Box definitely doesn’t have such power, but it shouldn’t be a problem for Yingtian Immortal to use the principle of the Restraining Light Treasure Box to refine a higher-level Immortal Artifact.

After all, he is the ancestor of refining; he cannot possibly be incapable of refining anything.

"However, in order to refine an Immortal Artifact that can suppress an Immortal’s realm, quite a bit of Immortal Gold will likely be needed," Lu Yang pondered. Although he was not the Sect Leader, as a member of the Seek Dao Sect, he had to consider the interests of the Sect.

Is the cost of transforming Captive Peak a bit too much?

"Eldest Senior Sister, do you have business at Captive Peak?"

The most notable example of the effect on Lu Yang’s side was Meng Jingzhou, whose Pure Yang Constitution nearly broke due to the surge of the Sun’s power.

To break the seal laid by the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord and liberate the power of Sun and Lunar, cultivators practicing the Yin Yang Technique welcomed a springtime of opportunity.

Of course, if the seal could not be broken, asking Immortal Jiuchong to increase the firepower of the Sun could also lead to a springtime for cultivators practicing the Yin Yang Technique.

Lu Yang performed the Tofu Venerable Celestial Form to elevate his realm to the peak of the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, where he could freely roam the universe, no longer needing Yun Zhi’s assistance.

Then Yun Zhi noticed that Lu Yang’s flight speed could not keep up with hers, so she simply formed a hand seal to drag Lu Yang along faster.

The two arrived at the Sun, and the power of the Supreme Yang hit them in the face. Lu Yang, who would once get scorched approaching the Sun, now feared not the Supreme Yang power on the surface of the Sun.

When Lu Yang wanted to get even closer, golden patterns emerged, circling the surface of the Sun, thwarting Lu Yang’s intentions.

Countless magnificent runes flickered like stars, gathered at Yun Zhi’s pale fingertips, the golden bell bracelet on her wrist jingling. Yun Zhi raised her hand, touching the golden pattern on the surface of the Sun.

Crack—

The golden pattern shattered, and the power of the Supreme Yang surged wildly, almost causing Lu Yang to tumble over.

Meanwhile, every cultivator in the Cultivation World felt the changes emanating from the Sun, with those who practiced Yin Yang Techniques experiencing the most pronounced sensations. Quite a few cultivators seized the opportunity to break through their bottlenecks.

But none of this was of concern to Yun Zhi.

"It’s time."

Yun Zhi spoke indifferently as she drew a vertical line in the air, slicing open a door on the surface of the Sun and revealing the landscape of Sun Cave Heaven.

Inside Sun Cave Heaven, majestic palaces stood tall, surrounded by an aura of immortality, glittering with gold and jade splendor as if all the marvelous treasures of the world had been used to decorate the palace. The number of Heaven and Earth Treasures within could be described as vast beyond measure, making Great Xia Palace seem insignificant by comparison.

"This is Great Qian’s Fairy Palace!"

Lu Yang suddenly realized. This was the very Fairy Palace spoken of by the cultivators of Great Qian, but they had been bound by a Restriction by the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord, unable to disclose the location of the Fairy Palace!

Turns out, the Fairy Palace had been right above their heads all along!

This wasn’t just darkness beneath the lamp; it was like hiding inside the lamp itself.

"Yes, this is Great Qian’s Fairy Palace," Yun Zhi was not surprised, as The Controller had already made everything clear.

Seeing Lu Yang on alert, Yun Zhi shook her head, signaling him to lower his guard: "The Emperor Lord left long ago. When The Controller was battling with Immortal Jiuchong, he had already sensed my presence. Knowing his character, his first reaction would have been to retreat to the Fairy Palace and lead his followers to escape. Perhaps in their haste, they failed to take the Fairy Palace with them."

"There’s no one left in the Fairy Palace now."

Upon hearing this, Lu Yang felt a sense of regret but then realized that the Fairy Palace itself was a treasure.

Worried about the lack of Immortal Gold for the renovation of Captive Peak? Well, wasn’t that problem now solved?

The brother and sister entered the Fairy Palace, which was equally grand inside. Murals depicted various bizarre events: colossal giants plowing the earth with divine oxen, sages creating paintings with a flick of their brushes, adorning the night sky with stars, divine beings descending to eliminate demons and bring peace to the world, Emperor Yu of Great Yu seated at the center of heaven and earth, upholding the Sun and Moon...

As strangers entered the Fairy Palace, divine beings and demon beasts crawled out of the murals, baring teeth and claws ready to attack the newcomers.

This was the ability of The Controller’s Enlightenment Tao Fruit. Even an Immortal would suffer severe injuries if caught off guard by a single strike from the murals.

Yun Zhi, without even a glance, snapped her fingers, and the divine beings and demon beasts dissolved like wet paintings, blurring and fading until they vanished like a receding tide.

All this was but a trivial act for Yun Zhi, and she didn’t take it to heart as she explained the origin of the Fairy Palace.

"Initially, the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord and The Controller constructed the Fairy Palace within the Sun to mitigate the influence of the Power of Faith, and since the Sun was at the center of the world, it also served to search for the Four Ancient Immortals."

"To prevent anyone from entering the Sun, the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord set up a seal."

"After Great Qian fell and Great Yu rose, Emperor Wu Yao of Yu, unaware of the purpose of the seal on the Sun, disliked the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord’s monopolization of the Sun and set his own seal, effectively trapping both the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord and The Controller within the Sun."

"In fact, the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord was not adept at Sealing Skills; his capability to set the seal relied on the accumulated Power of Faith."

"Violently breaking the seal would reveal the existence of the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord and The Controller, which was not conducive to reducing the influence of the Power of Faith."

"To escape the Sun, the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord and The Controller spent a hundred thousand years studying the seal set by Wu Yao and finally found a flaw. They could leave the Sun without breaking the seal."

Fairy Eternity understood and summarized with her hands in her sleeves: "So what you’re saying is that Emperor Yu and The Controller, these two fools, were locked inside their own home by Wu Yao, and it took them a hundred thousand years to jimmy the lock open?"

Lu Yang: "..."

The enmity between Emperor Yu and Wu Yao was not small indeed.

Chapter 1201: Chapter 1200: One Person Below the Transcendance Tribulation Stage

Transporting a fairy palace is no easy feat; even the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord didn’t bring it along when he fled, which says it all.

Moreover, the fairy palace is the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord’s magic artifact, and without his consent, it can’t even fit into a storage ring.

The dimensions of the fairy palace are measured in "li," and Lu Yang certainly can’t carry it from the Sun to an Immortal Sect, as that would be too conspicuous.

Before long, Lu Yang came up with a good idea, "Could we have The Controller use the Enlightenment Tao Fruit to enlighten the fairy palace and let it move itself to our sect?"

Yun Zhi looked at her naive junior brother with an odd tone, "You mean to have The Controller give life to the fairy palace, and then let the fairy palace fly back to our sect on its own. Then, in front of The Controller, dismantle the fairy palace and refine it into an immortal artifact, and finally use that immortal artifact on The Controller?"

Lu Yang scratched his head embarrassingly; it did sound somewhat cruel.

"Then why not just directly invite the Yingtian Immortal to come over? After all, in the end, it will be him who refines the immortal weapons."

Yun Zhi nodded, that indeed seemed like a viable solution.

Although at this moment, Lu Yang was protected by Yun Zhi and Fairy Eternity, and not afraid of the Yingtian Immortal—who would create a clone to come over as soon as someone cursed at Yingtian Immortal a couple of times—it was still not proper to call out to someone in such a manner. Being one who respected the wise and looked up to those of higher ability, Lu Yang decided it was best to personally visit the Laurel Fairy Palace to invite Yingtian Immortal.

Upon arrival at the Laurel Fairy Palace, Lu Yang saw the twins running around happily and fell into contemplation.

"Fairy, why do the cultivators of the fairy palace give birth to only girls after drinking water from the Twin River?"

"Is that so strange? It’s commonly said that ’dragons beget dragons and phoenixes beget phoenixes,’ so if men drink from the Twin River, they birth boys, and if women drink from it, they have girls."

Lu Yang had always wanted to know what would happen if a male drank water from the Twin River, but had never dared to ask.

Now the answer was revealed, and there was no need to ask.

Better to stay away from the Twin River in the future, lest its water splashes onto oneself.

Having found the Yingtian Immortal, and upon hearing that an entire fairy palace was available for refining, Yingtian Immortal became immediately interested and didn’t hesitate to head straight for the Sun.

Upon first seeing the fairy palace, even Yingtian Immortal was shocked.

"To use so many fine goods to create such a palace is a waste; such a tragic squandering of good material!"

"Look here, these two kinds of Immortal Gold have different properties, yet they have been forcefully joined together!"

"And here, the impurities have not been fully removed, and the hardness doesn’t meet the standard; what kind of mess is this?"

"Who refined this rubbish? If you can’t refine it, then don’t bother!"

"Mid-heaven Emperor Lord Mo Qingshui."

Yingtian Immortal sneered upon hearing the name, "What kind of emperor? Nothing but a nouveau riche, thinks he’s all that just because he can devour Dao Fruit."

Lu Yang understood; it was the disdain of a fellow craftsman. While the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord often embarrassingly lost face in front of the Eldest Senior Sister, at other times, he still commanded respect.

Yingtian Immortal was in the same boat.

And considering that during the Great Qian Period, the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord had been in command of the Central Continent, inspiring awe in all directions, it’s no wonder Yingtian Immortal might feel irked inside.

"Is it possible to refine an immortal artifact that suppresses realms?" asked Yun Zhi.

"With so much Immortal Gold, of course, it’s no problem!" Yingtian Immortal said confidently.

Yun Zhi nodded, albeit skeptically; she remembered when she first met Yingtian Immortal, he was also confidently claiming he could refine immortal artifacts, only to turn around and say he couldn’t do it.

Well, might as well believe him one more time.

In the eyes of Yingtian Immortal, the fairy palace was no longer a whole, but neatly arranged blocks of Immortal Gold and Spirit Gold.

He moved with a thought, summoning rolling thunder. The thunder acted like a blade, slicing through the palace; soon, chunks of Immortal Gold and Spirit Gold that Lu Yang couldn’t identify came apart, emitting a faint oppressive force that clearly was not a common object.

Ying Tian Immortal handled the Immortal Gold with ease, growing happier as he cut more of it: "Leave this matter to me."

Seeing how adept Ying Tian Immortal was, Yun Zhi temporarily set aside her doubts about his artifact-refining skills and took Lu Yang back to the Seek Dao Sect, leaving Ying Tian Immortal alone there.

"Refining something like Captive Peak, eh..." Ying Tian Immortal murmured to himself, having not crafted a space-class magic artifact for a long time, forgetting that the most important thing to refine such an artifact was missing.

"I don’t have the blueprint."

When it comes to who excels at designing blueprints, there’s none other than Zhu Tian.

Ying Tian Immortal regretted speaking so soon. If only he had known, he would have asked Lu Yang to bring Zhu Tian over before letting them leave.

"Never mind, I’ll go find Zhu Tian myself."

Before long, Zhu Tian was brought by Ying Tian Immortal to the sun, where Zhu Tian, terrified and cautious, focused solely on designing the map for the new Prison Peak.

Following that, Ying Tian Immortal recalled that refining an Immortal Artifact was best done with Immortal Fire, so he went to fetch Immortal Jiuchong.

Ying Tian Immortal and Immortal Jiuchong stood by Zhu Tian’s side, one on the left, the other on the right, both waiting for Zhu Tian’s design blueprint.

The Ancient Double Immortals stood guard like bodyguards, startling Zhu Tian significantly; fortunately, his mental fortitude was commendable, not letting tension disrupt his design thoughts.

"After all, I am the harbinger of the Great Era’s strife. Now, more and more Immortals are gathering around me," Zhu Tian thought to himself, working with even greater vigor.

...

As the latest issue of Cultivation Monthly was released, news of Lu Yang slaying a Semi-Immortal with Transcendance Tribulation Stage cultivation spread rapidly.

The common people heard it and thought nothing of it—just another challenge exceeded; Talent Lu wasn’t doing this for the first time.

But to those knowledgeable cultivators, it was entirely a different matter.

Transcendance Tribulation Stage slaying a Semi-Immortal was unheard of from ancient times to the present—a monumental event destined for the history books. Millennia from now, when future generations recount past geniuses, Lu Yang’s name will stand like an insurmountable mountain, impossible to circumvent.

The most critical point was that Lu Yang was not just any Transcendance Tribulation Stage cultivator, but one who had risen from the Void Refinement Stage fluctuations; defeating Yang Kongdong meant Lu Yang was exceedingly familiar with the power of the Transcendance Tribulation Stage.

As for whom the news brought the most mixed feelings, it was none other than Lu Baqian, Sect Leader of the Corpse Chasing Sect.

Lu Baqian put down the newspaper and heaved a deep sigh.

"Who would’ve thought Daoist Buyu’s little disciple would grow this quickly."

A disciple of the Corpse Chasing Sect, Zhao Po, had once journeyed through the Wild State with Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, an old acquaintance of Lu Yang.

He couldn’t understand why his Sect Leader felt this way.

"Sect Leader, isn’t it a good thing for Senior Brother Lu to grow so rapidly?"

"Of course, it’s a good thing, but it’s not entirely good for me."

"Why?" Zhao Po still didn’t understand.

Lu Baqian glanced at Zhao Po, whose talent for cultivation wasn’t bad but who couldn’t seem to catch on quickly, especially when compared to Lu Yang.

Although he wasn’t the brightest, he was nonetheless the next Sect Leader, so he deserved a bit more explanation.

"Many years ago, I was possessed by a Great Yu Cultivator. The Great Yu Cultivator helped me cultivate to the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, and I gained the body of that stage as a blessing in disguise, while my soul remained at the Body Integration Realm. Therefore, strictly speaking, I am a Body Integration Realm cultivator."

"That’s why I have the reputation as the supreme under the Transcendance Tribulation Stage."

"If Lu Yang one day steps into the Body Integration Realm, the title of the supreme under the Transcendance Tribulation Stage won’t hold."

Zhao Po: "..."

Isn’t the title of ’supreme under the Transcendance Tribulation Stage’ self-proclaimed?

Chapter 1202: Chapter 1201: Breakthrough to the Void Refinement Stage

Lu Yang returned to the Seek Dao Sect, and the first thing he did was to visit his good brother Meng Jingzhou.

When Lu Yang arrived at Meng Jingzhou’s abode, he saw several large pits dug at the entrance, with Old Ma standing on two legs, hooves stuck to a shovel, still digging and pouring ice cubes with swift movements, without any sign of dragging or sloppiness.

"Where’s Old Meng?"

Lu Yang noticed that one of the pits was bubbling and steaming. A red-faced Meng Jingzhou popped his head out and, with a leap, jumped into the adjacent pit of ice water.

The ice cubes in the pit were melting at a visible rate, and it looked like it was going to turn into boiling water again.

A good brother in distress, Lu Yang definitely couldn’t kick him when he was down. He kindly cheered on Meng Jingzhou, "It’s said that the greater the pressure, the greater the pressure. Old Meng, you can do it. I believe you can get through this!"

"Cultivation is something one must rely on oneself to work hard for; I won’t keep you company."

Having said that, Lu Yang ran off before Meng Jingzhou could curse.

After descending the mountain, Lu Yang noticed many unfamiliar disciples of the Seek Dao Sect pointing and discussing something. When he turned his head to look at them, the junior brothers and sisters hurriedly closed their mouths and pretended they hadn’t seen Lu Yang.

Once Lu Yang’s gaze was elsewhere, they resumed their discussion.

"That’s the legendary Elder Brother Lu Yang."

"I joined the Seek Dao Sect just to follow in the footsteps of Elder Brother Lu Yang. I finally got to see him in person today!"

"Have you heard? Elder Brother Lu Yang killed the Master of the Ruthless Sect, who was an Ancient Half-Immortal!"

"Who hasn’t heard about that? But the more outrageous part comes later. It’s said that the Master of the Ruthless Sect summoned the Controller of the Great Qian Dynasty at the cost of his life, a real Immortal. Elder Brother Lu fought several rounds with the Controller and didn’t fall behind!"

"And Elder Brother Lu never takes pride in his own achievements. Even after doing great deeds outside, he always reports dutifully to Elder Brother Dai when he returns to the sect."

"Elder Brother Lu was a Foundation Establishment spy in the Eternity Sect and even toppled it. We are also at the Foundation Establishment Stage, and when we go out, we can only carry out some minor tasks, and our opponents are at most at the Half-step Golden Core Stage, far behind Elder Brother Lu."

"When will I ever reach Elder Brother Lu’s realm?"

"You’re dreaming if you think you can compare to Elder Brother Lu."

These were all newly recruited disciples of the Seek Dao Sect. Lu Yang, who often secluded himself for cultivation or was out on missions, rarely showed his face at the bottom of the mountain.

Therefore, his appearance this time instantly prompted those disciples who hadn’t seen Lu Yang but had long heard tales about him to secretly call over friends.

However, they all lacked the courage to face Lu Yang directly, only daring to sneak peeks from behind.

Hearing the unabashed praise from the junior brothers and sisters, Lu Yang just smiled and shook his head, saying nothing.

On Sky Gate Mountain, Yun Mengmeng stood halfway up the mountain, curiously watching the second-in-command measuring the sect’s perimeter with his steps.

"Little Lotus, the second-in-command has walked around the sect several times. Why hasn’t he come up the mountain yet?"

"He might be lost," Qinghe said with certainty.

Just as Qinghe had predicted, the Seek Dao Sect was too big. It was only after the seventh time Lu Yang passed Sky Gate Mountain that he went up.

In the following days, besides accompanying Immortal Fairy Eternity to play, playing with Yun Mengmeng, participating in the New Prison Peak’s trimming ceremony, strolling down the mountain a couple of times, listening to Third Senior Sister Gan Tian talk about refining the spirit with light songs, discussing the filming techniques of Dream Mirage with Tao Yaoye, caring about the progress of Li Haoran’s cultivation, going to the barbecue restaurant with Meng Jingzhou for skewers, and writing to Man Gu, the County Magistrate, Lu Yang focused on his cultivation.

Whether it was Cultivators of the Mortal World or Hidden Cultivators, cultivation requires complete focus, and the same applied to Lu Yang, which is why he advanced so rapidly.

"Void Refinement Stage, Red Dust Mortality, War Feeds War..." fгeewёbnoѵel.cσm

In cultivation, there are no years. Lu Yang had been in seclusion in the abode for three hours, during which he had only gone out once to taste the new Spirit Food made by Yun Mengmeng.

Lu Yang meditated attentively, reflecting on everything he had experienced since ascending to the Void Refinement Stage.

"No, it’s not just about the experiences of the Void Refinement Stage; weren’t the previous experiences also a form of Red Dust Mortality and War Feeds War?"

Lu Yang was divinely inspired and vaguely touched the threshold of ascending to the Void Refinement Stage.

"Third Senior Sister Gan Tian went alone into the Demon Territory during her Void Refinement Stage to temper herself. She pitted her wits and bravery against various members of the Demon Race and made quite a name for herself."

"At that time, Third Senior Sister’s realm was not stable; she faced opponents far stronger than herself. That was her crisis, but also her opportunity."

"How is it any different for me? Every time I venture out, I encounter opponents of extremely high realms... The path of the Third Senior Sister is one I’ve already tread."

With this realization, the "path" before Lu Yang became increasingly clear, as if he could touch it by reaching out. His realm fluctuated wildly, with the changes occurring at an extreme pace.

So Lu Yang reached out.

When Lu Yang touched the "path," his wildly fluctuating realm was like a long-distance runner crossing the finish line, finally getting the chance to breathe, no longer sprinting for life. After running a few more steps, he stopped in place, gasping heavily.

"I’ve done it!" Lu Yang’s eyes shone with an unprecedented brightness, a confidence brought on by breaking through to the Void Refinement Stage.

As long as he could pass the Heavenly Tribulation, he would have successfully broken through the Void Refinement Stage!

Without leaving his abode, Lu Yang could feel the Thunder Tribulation clouds gathering above his head.

"Cultivation is so fast, huh." Immortal Fairy emerged from the Spiritual Space, clucking and applauding.

Then she remembered something she had to attend to right away.

"Well then, Little Yang, you work hard to pass the tribulation; Immortal has some matters to attend to, so I won’t accompany you."

Lu Yang felt somewhat uneasy; Fairy, what if Elder Ying Tian strikes me down mercilessly after you leave?

But he couldn’t hold the Fairy back since she had matters to attend to, so he simply replied with a "Okay."

...

Above the Seek Dao Sect, high above the Thunder Tribulation clouds, Ying Tian Immortal’s fingertips sparked with electricity as he contemplated which strength of Heavenly Tribulation to test Lu Yang with.

"Lu Yang, this boy, sure cultivates fast."

"Should I use the usual Thunder Tribulation, or one of the new types of Thunder Tribulation I’ve been researching recently?"

Just thinking about Lu Yang’s previous experience with passing the Thunder Tribulation made Ying Tian Immortal ache all over.

As Ying Tian Immortal was mulling over it, a clear stream of qi rose from below, reaching above the Thunder Tribulation clouds and manifesting as Immortal Fairy.

"Immortal Fairy, why have you come?" Ying Tian Immortal was surprised.

"Ying Tian, what kind of Heavenly Tribulation do you think Little Yang should pass this time?" Immortal Fairy inquired.

Ying Tian Immortal opened his mouth to respond, but saw another clear stream of qi ascend to the heavens, transforming into Yun Zhi.

Yun Zhi was surprised to see Immortal Fairy there as well and stated her purpose for coming.

"Elder Ying Tian Immortal, what kind of Heavenly Tribulation should my junior brother pass this time?"

"..."

Ying Tian Immortal glanced at Immortal Fairy on his left and then at Yun Zhi on his right, and thought about his own status as one of the Five Ancient Immortals, Ancestor of Refining, powerful in every respect, and remembered that his heart in seeking the Dao was unwavering, not to be swayed by external influences.

With these thoughts, he made up his mind and seriously said,

"Whatever tribulation you say he should pass, that’s the one I’ll strike down with."

Chapter 1203: Chapter 1202: Neutralize It

Outside the Abode, Yun Mengmeng held an unripe Immortal Spirit Fruit as a sandbag, tossing it at Gan Tian. Gan Tian, agile as ever, dodged, and the Immortal Spirit Fruit was caught by Qinghe standing behind. Qinghe continued to throw it at Gan Tian, who kept evading.

The three women were having a blast.

Lu Yang took a couple of deep breaths and, with a smile on his face, emerged from the Abode, looking unflustered.

Although he didn’t know what the Heavenly Tribulation would be like this time, he decided to act as if everything was under control.

"Sister Mengmeng, I’m about to break through my realm and will soon have to Pass the Tribulation; you all should go down the mountain first..."

Yun Mengmeng hadn’t expected Second-in-command to come out at this moment. Distracted, she failed to catch the Immortal Spirit Fruit that was thrown to her, which then fell to the ground.

And then, with a boom, it exploded,

drowning out Lu Yang’s voice.

Unripe Immortal Spirit Fruits were explosive.

Yun Mengmeng jumped in shock and quickly checked on Lu Yang with concern, "Second-in-command, are you all right? Did you just say you’re about to Pass the Tribulation?"

Lu Yang, covered in soot and dirt, coughed twice, no longer maintaining his unflustered poise: "Cough, I’m fine. You all hurry down the mountain."

"All right, all right."

Yun Mengmeng hastily took a bag full of unripe Immortal Spirit Fruits down the mountain, worrying that if a bolt from the Thunder Tribulation went astray and struck the fruits, it might blast Second-in-command straight into the sky.

After the three women left, only Lu Yang remained on Sky Gate Mountain. He took another deep breath, steadied his Mind State, and spread his arms wide to embrace the Heavens.

He freely unleashed his realm, ready to confront the Heavenly Tribulation. freewebnσvel.cѳm

"I’m ready. Heavenly Tribulation, bring it on!"

Lu Yang stood with his arms wide open like a crucifix, waiting for a long time, but the Heavenly Tribulation was slow to descend.

"That’s strange, where is the Heavenly Tribulation?"

"You tell me how to Pass the Tribulation, and I’ll strike that way."

Yingtian Immortal thought it over seriously and decided that it shouldn’t be up to him to determine what kind of Heavenly Tribulation would descend, as he didn’t know Lu Yang as well as Daoist Yun Zhi and Fairy Eternity.

Only those most familiar with Lu Yang could decide which type of Heavenly Tribulation should descend.

Upon hearing Yingtian Immortal’s words, Fairy Eternity was elated: "That’s perfect, just pick an easy Thunder Tribulation and give him a couple of symbolic strikes."

"Okay, then I will descend..."

"Not so fast. Junior Brother hasn’t become an Immortal yet and lacks experience. If he starts slacking during his Tribulation now, how will he fare in his future Cultivation? We should drop a heavier Thunder Tribulation."

"Fine, then I will descend..."

"I think Little Yang is doing quite well at the moment, energetic and vigorous, with a strong physique. He doesn’t lack experience, so a moderate Thunder Tribulation will suffice."

"As the Fairy Senior has said, Junior Brother is full of Essence, Qi, and Spirit, and strong of body, but there’s still room for improvement. Wouldn’t taking it up a notch be better?"

"Ying Tian, you give your opinion. What kind of Tribulation should Little Yang Pass?"

"Yingtian Immortal Senior should know the principle that the stronger the Thunder Tribulation, the better."

Both turned to look at Yingtian Immortal at the same time.

Yingtian Immortal broke out in a cold sweat, unsure of which side to choose.

Is this Lu Yang passing the Tribulation, or is it me?

"Since the dawn of time, the mighty have been revered. Why not have a duel between Immortal Fairy and Daoist Yun Zhi? The victor will decide the matter."

Fairy Eternity, who had appeared taut and serious just moments before, suddenly started coughing, "Immortal has serious injuries that require rest and cannot return to peak form for now. Miss Yun surely wouldn’t have the heart to compete with me in my current state."

"Once my injuries are healed, then I will compete with Miss Yun!"

Yun Zhi was having some regrets. Was taking The Controller as a bribe to stay quiet too cheap a price?

"Fairy Senior, why don’t we strike a compromise?" Yun Zhi suggested proactively.

"You see, the Thunder Tribulation has a total of eighty-one strikes. We could alternate, light strike following heavy, with eighty-one light and eighty-one heavy in total. This way, we could both have our requirements met."

Fairy Eternity thought about it seriously for a moment and felt it was a good idea.

Although she hadn’t lowered the power of all the Thunder Tribulations as she had wanted, halving them still seemed fair to Little Yang.

...

As the legendary Lu Yang’s breakthrough approached, the entire Seek Dao Sect turned up for the spectacle, even those running barbecue stands and butcheries came to join in.

Lu Yang’s previous Spirit Transformation Heavenly Tribulation was eye-opening, so his current Void Refinement Thunder Tribulation was expected to be extraordinary as well.

"Why hasn’t the Heavenly Tribulation descended yet?"

The crowd whispered among themselves, sensing something unusual.

"I’ve never heard of a Heavenly Tribulation being late."

The crowd was especially baffled, as it was an ironclad rule of the Cultivation World that Thunder Tribulation would come immediately upon a realm breakthrough—a rule that had held true for three hundred thousand years since Ancient Times, with no exceptions.

"Why is Senior Brother Lu standing with his arms open all this time? Is it some kind of ritual?"

"Maybe that’s why Senior Brother Lu is so strong?"

Boom—

The long-awaited Thunder Tribulation descended on Lu Yang like pillars, striking him with blinding brightness.

They were far from Sky Gate Mountain, but when the Thunder Tribulation descended, it was still deafening, resonating in their chests, vibrating as if in unison with the thunder. One could only imagine the immense pressure Lu Yang in the center of the Thunder Tribulation was facing.

"Here it comes, finally! What kind of Thunder Tribulation is this? It looks so powerful!"

"I don’t recognize it."

"Quick, go borrow the ’Thunder Tribulation Complete’ from the Scripture Pavilion!"

"I’ve memorized the ’Thunder Tribulation Complete’, but there isn’t this kind of Thunder Tribulation in it!"

"Who told you to flip through the ’Thunder Tribulation Complete?’ You were supposed to add a blank page at the back; the Thunder Tribulation needs an update!"

"Makes sense, makes sense!"

At first, Lu Yang was startled by the Thunder Tribulation. Was the Yingtian Immortal really this ruthless?

But soon, he noticed something was off; this strike of Thunder Tribulation, while looking fierce, actually felt tingly and numb on impact—quite comfortable, like a massage.

"It seems that the Yingtian Immortal still treats me alright... Ah—"

Before Lu Yang could finish his sentence, he was hit solidly by the second strike of Thunder Tribulation, which compared to the first, was as different as heaven and earth in terms of power.

Seeing the lack of power in the Thunder Tribulation, Lu Yang had let his guard down, only to be nearly knocked senseless by the second strike.

"First a mild Thunder Tribulation to get me to relax then suddenly a powerful one comes crashing down?"

"Yingtian Immortal, surely you jest. You’re using tactics against me?"

It was always the Cultivator facing the Thunder Tribulation with strategies; this was Lu Yang’s first time encountering a Thunder Tribulation that used tactics.

Just as Lu Yang braced himself for the third strike of Thunder Tribulation, it went back to the tingling sensation.

Not daring to let his guard down, Lu Yang was proven right as the fourth strike of Thunder Tribulation came with a frightening increase in power, far beyond what a Void Refinement Stage Thunder Tribulation should have.

"Hiss, it hurts so much."

With so many admirers watching from below, Lu Yang took the pain in stride, not making a sound, showing remarkable resilience.

In his mind, Lu Yang kept hypnotizing himself—eighty-one strikes of Thunder Tribulation, just bear with it until it’s over, eighty-one strikes of Thunder Tribulation, just bear with it until it’s over.

After the eighty-first strike of Thunder Tribulation, Lu Yang breathed a sigh of relief. Although the process was painful, he could barely hang on.

Mere Thunder Tribulation, that’s all it was.

Then the eighty-second strike of Thunder Tribulation was ready to unleash.

"Wait, why is there more Thunder Tribulation?!"

Chapter 1204: Chapter 123 Do You Not Want Me Anymore?

"Look, look, the eighty-second Thunder Tribulation has appeared!" Members of the Seek Dao Sect yelled excitedly.

"Hurry up and write it down in the ’Thunder Tribulation Complete,’ the eighty-first Thunder Tribulation isn’t the limit; there are more to come!"

This was indeed a breakthrough in previous Thunder Tribulation experience, posing a major test for all cultivators about to undergo their tribulation.

Previously, their consideration in tribulation was how to survive the eighty-one thunder tribulations, but now they wondered whether there were more thunder tribulations beyond the eighty-first.

Calls from the crowd surged one after another.

"Who would have thought Senior Brother Lu’s tribulation this time would not only feature a first-time type of thunder tribulation but also a different number!"

"Joining the Seek Dao Sect was indeed the right decision!"

Even the higher-ups of the Eternity Sect couldn’t help but remark, "Each tribulation creates history; truly, he is a man blessed by heaven!"

Yun Mengmeng felt pleased with the reactions of the people around her.

Gan Tian sensed the astonishing thunder tribulation at Sky Gate Mountain and thought back to her own tribulation when she ascended to the Body Integration Realm and couldn’t help but sigh, "Junior Brother Lu is truly beyond compare."

Gan Tian merely sighed twice, harboring no thoughts of defeat or dejection, for this was the Junior Brother chosen and nurtured by the Eldest Senior Sister, whose talents naturally stood out, making any comparison unnecessary.

"Eldest Senior Sister, is he the person you were looking for?" Gan Tian softly pondered, suddenly recalling a long-ago casual chat with the Eldest Senior Sister when she had mentioned happily,

"I need someone to help maintain my humanity, unfortunately, that person hasn’t appeared yet."

These were the original words of the Eldest Senior Sister, spoken only to Gan Tian.

The thunder tribulation continued, and Lu Yang, despite being struck until his skin split and flesh burst, did not utter a sound.

"One hundred sixty, one hundred sixty-one, one hundred sixty-two... my god, it’s finally over."

Lu Yang kept silent while the members of the Seek Dao Sect counted the thunder tribulations for him, growing more terrified as the count increased.

"Junior Brother Lu is truly defying heaven; he’s doubled it!"

The crowd erupted in excitement, while the disciples in the Void Refinement Stage witnessing the number of thunder tribulations felt a tingling pain in their bodies as they prematurely imagined what their own tribulation would be like.

Could they also be facing one hundred sixty-two thunder tribulations?

"Phew, he’s finally made it through." Lu Yang let out a breath; his appearance was a bit ragged, his robe tattered like a rag tied around his body, but now was not the time to worry about such things.

After the thunder tribulation, dew descended from heaven, silently and invisibly, nourishing Lu Yang’s battered body.

Lu Yang’s wounds healed at a visibly quick pace, his whole being transformed, as if reborn, with skin so fair and unblemished.

"Body Integration Realm." Lu Yang whispered softly to himself, revealing his current realm.

"Second-in-command, you did it!"

After the thunder tribulation, Yun Mengmeng was the first to rush up and congratulate him, smiling even more happily than Lu Yang himself.

"Good job, Martial Nephew Lu."

"You’re amazing, Senior Brother."

"Xuanyuan Sword Master, have you remembered your past life yet?"

"Still haven’t remembered? I hope you remember soon."

From the elders to the junior brothers and sisters, everyone came to Sky Gate Mountain to extend their blessings.

Lu Yang humbly accepted all, except the congratulations from Gu Junye.

Lu Yang was very popular within the Seek Dao Sect; he continued to receive congratulations from morning until evening, completing the process.

"It looks like even without this Immortal, Little Yang, you managed quite well." Immortal Fairy said gleefully, in a manner that practically screamed, "I’m the hero, praise me," leaving Lu Yang quite puzzled.

"If the Fairy had been here, my tribulation would surely have been even better." As a subject, there’s no need to worry about what His Majesty is thinking first, just agree.

Sure enough, as soon as he said this, Immortal Fairy laughed even more joyfully.

And the final congratulations came from Yun Zhi.

"Well done."

Eldest Senior Sister cherished her words like gold—a mere four words were enough to indicate her attitude.

"I am going to consolidate my realm first," Lu Yang said, knowing that stabilizing his realm was the most critical task after ascension.

"Go ahead."

Lu Yang returned to his abode. It was not his first time consolidating a realm; he was familiar with the process: burning incense, sitting in meditation, calming the mind, entering a meditative trance.

However, this time, no matter what, he could not enter the meditative trance. The words spoken by Gu Junye kept flashing in his mind.

"Xuanyuan Sword Master, have you remembered the memories of your past life?"

"You still haven’t remembered? I hope you remember them soon."

Why did these two sentences keep flashing by? Had I forgotten the memories of my previous life? No, I remembered my past life memories very clearly.

Was it because Gu Junye kept mentioning it, making me believe it myself?

That wasn’t right either.

Was I too excited about reaching the Body Integration Realm to enter the trance?

No, my mental state wasn’t that fragile.

What was it, then? Had I forgotten something?

...

"No, I haven’t completed the Heavenly Tribulation yet!"

Lu Yang suddenly realized, his eyes sparkled with understanding as he finally grasped the source of this unsettling strangeness!

"The Heavenly Tribulation for breaking through the Void Refinement Stage is divided into two phases; the first phase is the Thunder Tribulation, and the second phase is the Heart Tribulation."

He had only passed the first phase, and now he was in the second phase without realizing it!

"This is something everyone in the Cultivation World knows; I have known it for a long time. How could I have just thought of it now? Yes, when in the Heart Tribulation, some memories are shrouded in a veil, hard to unveil. It’s only by realizing that this is the Heart Tribulation that these memories will resurface!"

"I am currently undergoing the Heart Tribulation!"

"Little Yang, what’s wrong with you?" In the Spiritual Space, Immortal Fairy sprawled on Lu Yang’s chest, looking at him pitifully.

"Don’t you want me anymore?"

Immortal Fairy’s watery big eyes reflected Lu Yang’s expression of reluctant determination.

Lu Yang felt a tremendous reluctance in his heart, but he also knew that if he did not separate himself now, he would sink deeper and deeper into the illusion, unable to extricate himself.

For instance, now that he knew he was in an illusion, the Immortal Fairy before him was fake. Knowing it was fake meant that he could theoretically do whatever he wanted with the Immortal Fairy without any consequences, but he could not bring himself to do that; it was highly likely that he would not want to leave the illusion.

He could not hesitate any longer.

"Fairy...let’s meet in reality."

"Don’t!"

Lu Yang closed his eyes, stopped looking, and stopped thinking about the pitiful Immortal Fairy. He bit the tip of his tongue and fully activated the "Mind Seeing Method," his cultivation technique’s greatest feature was its ability to break through illusions!

A speck of light flashed across Lu Yang’s chest. As the "Mind Seeing Method" operated, the speck rapidly expanded, illuminating the entire abode and then enveloping the whole world.

Crack—

The illusion shattered, and the Heart Tribulation ended.

Lu Yang was still riddled with holes, just like before, but after the storm had passed, heavenly dew descended, nourishing his body.

Feeling his body gradually returning to its original state, Lu Yang revealed a relaxed smile.

"This now is reality."

Just like in the illusion, the heavenly dew restored Lu Yang’s body as tenderly as that of a newborn baby, with soft skin.

However, his realm was vastly different from that in the illusion.

"Is this...the Transcendance Tribulation Stage?"

Chapter 1205: Chapter 1204 Transcendance Tribulation Stage

Lu Yang was more than familiar with the power of the Transcendance Tribulation Stage; during his Void Refinement Stage, he often experienced fluctuations that reached the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, so he wouldn’t make a mistake in judging his own realm.

He felt his mana was profoundly thick, and his physical body was terrifyingly solid; a mere wave of his sleeve could slice off the top of a mountain. Put in the brilliant era of the Ancient Times, he could even shatter stars with a single finger.

"How did I directly become someone of the Transcendance Tribulation Stage when I am still in the midst of the Heart Tribulation?"

Lu Yang murmured, quickly discarding this doubt. His Clear Mind Technique was a top-tier Illusion Breaking Method in the world; there was no better way to break illusions while being in the same realm.

There was no illusionary realm that the Clear Mind Technique couldn’t dispel; thus, in the just-concluded Heart Tribulation, he only made himself forget about the existence of the Clear Mind Technique.

"Second-in-command, you’ve succeeded, huh... eh, you’ve reached the Transcendance Tribulation Stage?" After the tribulation, Yun Mengmeng was the first to arrive at Sky Gate Mountain and was surprised to find that the Second-in-command’s realm didn’t quite add up.

Isn’t it the Body Integration Realm after the Void Refinement Stage?

"He’s at the Transcendance Tribulation Stage?!"

Qinghe was greatly shocked; she had heard of fighting across levels, but never of cultivating across levels.

"It’s all just luck."

Regardless of the reason, Lu Yang first acknowledged it before anything else.

Everyone who came to congratulate him was collectively stunned; not only had he made history during the tribulation, but he continued to do so after it ended.

Has there ever been an example of skipping the Body Integration Stage in ancient and modern times?

Even when Yun Zhi was cultivating, she proceeded step by step and never skipped a realm.

"Congratulations, Martial Nephew Lu. With this, there aren’t many of us elders who have a higher cultivation level than you," the elders said with cheerful smiles. They had anticipated Lu Yang would surpass them one day, but they hadn’t expected it to come so soon.

Well, it was about time to retire.

"Little Lu, the position of the Second Elder will belong to you in the future."

"The position of the Third Elder..."

"The position of the Fourth Elder..."

"This position of the Grand Elder..."

"No, wait, the other elders are fine, but Grand Elder, aren’t we at the same realm? Can you retire?" Lu Yang became anxious. At this rate, he was about to hold all eight Great Elder positions!

If his master were here, he would probably hand over the position of Sect Leader to him as well.

"You are indeed extraordinary, Junior Brother Lu," his elder acknowledged with admiration.

"Senior Brother Lu, how can I skip realms like you?"

Gu Junye was particularly joyful, and the way he looked at Lu Yang was as if he had met an old friend from eons ago, personally solving the mystery for his old friend: "It seems, Xuanyuan Sword Master, that during your tribulation you channeled a part of your past life’s cultivation. The fusion of your past and present lives must have caused your realm to surge."

"If I am not mistaken, the Immortal Fairy would experience the same; after the Void Refinement Stage, she would go directly to the Transcendance Tribulation Stage!"

Lu Yang: "..."

No, I finally cultivated to the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, which was supposed to be a happy occasion, so why did I stop feeling happy after your congratulations?

Although the methods of congratulations were varied and strange, it was clear that these were genuine feelings. It showed how close the Seek Dao Sect was, and Lu Yang graciously accepted all the blessings, except those from the elders and Gu Junye.

From day to night, people from the Seek Dao Sect slowly departed one after another, and Lu Yang stood on the peak with his hands behind his back, personally seeing them off.

After stepping into the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, Lu Yang felt that his every move was effortlessly in harmony with the Dao Charm, signifying deep significance.

This was the confidence that his realm brought to him.

"You’ve made it to the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, Little Yang; not bad." Once everyone had gone, the Immortal Fairy hidden in the sky finally descended.

"The Transcendance Tribulation Stage, quite good." To Lu Yang’s surprise, the Eldest Senior Sister also appeared right after the Immortal Fairy.

So, before the tribulation when the Fairy said she had something to do, was it to find the Eldest Senior Sister?

"Eldest Senior Sister, Fairy, what’s really going on with me reaching the Transcendance Tribulation Stage?"

"Well, it’s probably because you were fluctuating to the Transcendance Tribulation Stage during the Void Refinement Stage." ƒrēewebnoѵёl.cσm

"You see, the principle of progressing to the Body Integration Realm from the Void Refinement Stage involves stabilizing the realm through various methods and ultimately comprehending the true essence of the Body Integration Realm, thereby achieving it."

"Since you often fluctuated to the Transcendance Tribulation Stage during your Void Refinement Stage, becoming most familiar with it, it’s quite normal to eventually stabilize in the Transcendance Tribulation Stage."

"I share the same opinion as the Fairy," the Eldest Senior Sister nodded.

"Mengmeng, Junior Brother is cultivating at an incredible speed, now that he has reached the Transcendance Tribulation Stage. You mustn’t let Junior Brother surpass you."

"I’m already working very hard in my cultivation, okay? When I just left our house, I was at the Early Tribulation Stage. Now, I’m already at the Middle Tribulation Stage!"

"Then tell me, how did you cultivate?"

"Eating, drinking, playing, and enjoying life—these are all methods taught to me by the Chief Housekeeper!"

"Yes, yes, all of us from the Immortal Lineage cultivate this way." The Immortal Fairy stood up to back up the Third Boss, together resisting the outside world.

"...Alright then."

Faced with the Immortal Fairy and Yun Mengmeng, Yun Zhi always felt powerless; both were untouchable.

She began to wonder if it was the right decision to let Yun Mengmeng join the Immortal Lineage?

"In reality, I probably can’t surpass Sister Mengmeng any time soon, since Sister Mengmeng has the Initial Form of Immortal Dao Fruit and is a Semi-Immortal," Lu Yang also spoke on behalf of Yun Mengmeng, telling the truth.

Being able to reach the Transcendance Tribulation Stage directly wasn’t something Lu Yang had anticipated. Originally, he planned to slowly seek the path to his own Dao Fruit after reaching the Body Integration Realm, allowing him to condense the Initial Form of Dao Fruit naturally and become a Semi-Immortal.

Now the pace of his cultivation was too fast, disrupting his plans.

"Indeed, now that you, Junior Brother, have cultivated to the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, you should start considering what kind of Initial Form of Dao Fruit to condense," Yun Zhi mentioned calmly. Ninety percent of those in the Transcendance Tribulation Stage worried about how to condense the Initial Form of Dao Fruit, but she believed in the talent of Junior Brother, knowing he wouldn’t be troubled by it.

What he needed to consider was which type of Initial Form of Dao Fruit to condense.

"Isn’t that obvious? It’ll be the Initial Form of Immortal Dao Fruit, of course!"

This time, Lu Yang didn’t immediately reject the Immortal Fairy’s statement; he was seriously considering another question, one that had troubled him for a long time.

"Eldest Senior Sister, do I really need to condense an Initial Form of Dao Fruit?"

Yun Zhi was taken aback: "What do you mean?"

"You don’t have a Dao Fruit, do you, Eldest Senior Sister?"

Lu Yang finally brought up the question. Although there was no direct evidence, somehow, he just felt it to be true.

The Eldest Senior Sister didn’t possess a Dao Fruit; she trod upon another path unknown to all.

Could he walk that same path?

This question, once asked, startled both Qinghe and Yun Mengmeng.

Yun Zhi was so powerful as to be unmatched; how could she not have a Dao Fruit?

"Ah? Xiao Zhi, aren’t you an Immortal?"

Only the Immortal Fairy showed no surprise; it was obvious to see that Miss Yun didn’t possess a Dao Fruit.

Yun Zhi didn’t expect Lu Yang to ask such a question, and was caught off guard.

After much hesitation and a silent sigh in her heart, she eventually spoke:

"Junior Brother, don’t follow in my footsteps; I have walked down the wrong path."

Chapter 1206: Chapter 1205 Yun Zhi’s Path

Lu Yang was utterly stupefied; even in the face of Heart Tribulation, he couldn’t utter such an outrageous statement.

"Eldest Senior Sister, do you mean that although you can scare away the Mid-heaven Emperor Lord, defeat Emperor Wu Yao of Yu, overcome the Four Ancient Immortals, and prevail over Ashy Bean and the Fairy, your path is wrong?"

Yun Zhi nodded, assuring Lu Yang he hadn’t misheard.

"Hey, hey, hey, Immortal like me is on par with Miss Yun!" Immortal Fairy, dissatisfied with Lu Yang’s last remark, pointed out the mistake, questioning what her affairs had to do with Miss Yun.

"Miss Yun, if your path is not the Dao Fruit path, then your ultimate realm isn’t ’Omniscience’ or ’Transcendence,’ right?"

Yun Zhi hadn’t expected Immortal Fairy to discern so much; should she say it was worthy coming from the founder of the Dao Fruit path?

"Xiao Zhi, is it so?"

Yun Zhi initially didn’t want to reveal so much. It was better to be aware of one’s mistaken paths privately—it wasn’t something to be proud of—but relentless questions from close ones compelled her to speak.

"Immortal Fairy Senior is correct, my realm cannot be measured by Dao Fruit. One step further, and it’s ’Harmonization.’"

"Harmonization?" Lu Yang heard this term for the first time.

"Harmonization is to replace Heaven with the heart," Yun Zhi said with a complex expression.

"To unify the body with the Dao, to replace Heaven with the heart, it sounds nice, but Heaven is heartless. After Harmonization, I would become the supreme Heaven, devoid of personal desires and distractions, and would also lose all desires."

"At that time, you all, to me, would be nothing more than the myriad beings under Heaven."

Lu Yang stared blankly, not expecting such an outcome: "Is this, is this still human?"

After finishing, Lu Yang wanted to slap himself twice; wasn’t this cursing?

Yun Zhi gave a bitter smile: "Of course not human. Haven’t I told you? After Harmonization, I become Heaven, how can Heaven be human?"

"Why did you choose this path?" Immortal Fairy curiously inquired, wasn’t the Dao Fruit path good? With Miss Yun’s talent, taking the Dao Fruit path, she could also become a being comparable to her.

Yun Zhi invited everyone to sit and poured each a cup of Enlightenment Tea before explaining the reasons.

"Originally, I also wanted to follow the Dao Fruit path."

"At that time, I had cultivated to the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, and the next step was to consolidate the Dao Fruit Outline. At that time, I didn’t know a single Semi-Immortal, and I only learned about Vast Sea Ancestral Master through Grandmaster."

"It so happened that during that period, Vast Sea Ancestral Master was in seclusion, and I had no one to consult."

"I thought, before the Ancestor comes out of seclusion, why not ponder over it myself, and then bring my questions to him when he emerges, which would also facilitate my learning."

"Unexpectedly, Vast Sea Ancestral Master’s seclusion lasted too long, and he did not emerge."

"How long did he seclude himself?" Immortal Fairy couldn’t help interrupting.

"...That’s not important. During the Ancestor’s seclusion, I deduced a completely new path, but at the time, I was unaware."

"After the Ancestor emerged, I requested to spar with him, and after defeating him cleanly, I then realized I was not on the path of Dao Fruit."

"..."

Lu Yang felt that the Vast Sea Ancestral Master was quite unfortunate; after all the hard work of his long seclusion, just as he emerged, Eldest Senior Sister came asking about the Dao Fruit path and then routed him completely.

What did the Ancestor achieve through his seclusion, after all?

No wonder Vast Sea Daoist Lord kept to his seclusion later, who wouldn’t be depressed?

"My path is incompatible with the Dao Fruit path. Initially, I didn’t think there was anything to it. The Dao Fruit path was created by predecessors; if predecessors could create a path, so could I. No matter what kind of path, as long as it makes me stronger, it’s fine."

"Later, I continued cultivating in this direction, until reaching the end of this path, which I named ’Harmonization.’"

"The end was right before my eyes, there was no reason not to approach it. Once the end was confirmed, I proceeded to attempt, and the stars as the Golden Cores you see today are the results of those attempts."

"It was precisely during that attempt that I realized the issues with Harmonization; it’s a path where one ultimately loses their humanity to become Heaven—this is an impassable road."

"Fortunately, that was my first attempt, and Harmonization was shallow. I hadn’t truly become Heaven and was able to break away, but it also deterred me from making a second attempt."

Yun Zhi earnestly said to Lu Yang: "That’s why I said, my path was wrong, Junior Brother, you shouldn’t follow my example."

Lu Yang nodded, indeed, if he were to mimic his Eldest Senior Sister, he, too, would end up with Harmonization, becoming the heartless Heaven—not at all the outcome he desired.

... Wait, thinking this, didn’t it imply that he could cultivate to Harmonization? Had he always been this confident?

Lu Yang suddenly recalled what Immortal Fairy had mentioned.

"After the Body Integration Realm, the Invincible Primordial Spirit will truly integrate with you, and then you will become extremely confident."

Lu Yang quickly inspected his own body secretly, searching for the Invincible Primordial Spirit, and saw no trace.

Damn, it indeed merged during the Pass Tribulation.

...

Lu Yang’s promotion to the Transcendance Tribulation Stage was such a significant event that the Cultivation Monthly printed at breakneck speed, with Guan Shanhai and The Controller working overtime.

Soon, Cultivation Monthly successfully spread the news throughout the entire Cultivation World, causing a worldwide stir.

The last time Lu Yang challenged a higher realm like Yang Kongdong, it seemed commonplace to those unacquainted with the matter. This time, even ordinary people were shocked.

In the streets, taverns, tea houses, flying boats, large ships... wherever there were people, there were discussions about Lu Yang.

"Gosh, unbelievable, one hundred and sixty-two heavenly thunders—who but Talent Lu could endure it?"

"That’s why he could directly advance to the Transcendance Tribulation Stage."

"I knew he was extraordinary when Talent Lu single-handedly defeated a Divinity Transformation Stage contender at the Foundation Establishment Stage. You all said it was fake news, but this is coming from the Seek Dao Sect, how could it be fake!"

Jiang Pingan, tilling in the Imperial Palace Forbidden Land, learned of Lu Yang’s promotion and slapped his thigh in regret. Such talent, he was destined to become an Immortal, and probably at an incredible pace too.

The contention for Lu Yang in the Great Era was indeed accurate, as he had guessed.

"If I had known, I wouldn’t have feared Daoist Yun Zhi back then; I should have forcefully dragged this lad to our Jiang Family to marry in!"

"At the very least, we should have sent a few princesses to the Seek Dao Sect to bond with the lad!"

Thinking of Meng Jingzhou, Jiang Pingan grew indignant: "How come the descendants of Meng Junzi are so promising!"

The more he thought, the more he felt his own descendants were disappointing, and he threw down his hoe and woke the sleeping Emperor Xia as if he were driving a donkey.

"You’re in the Divinity Transformation Stage, what are you sleeping for? Get up and cultivate, look at Lu Yang, how young he is, and he’s already at the Transcendance Tribulation Stage."

"Ah?"

Emperor Xia groggily woke up; was it too late for him to start striving now?

The happiest upon hearing this news had to be Lu Baqian, Master Ru of the Corpse Chasing Sect.

His loud, triumphant laughter could be heard throughout the entire Corpse Chasing Sect.

"Ha-ha, my title of the number one under the Pass Tribulation remains secure!"

Chapter 1207: Chapter 1206: The Apprentice Witch Meets the Master Witch

"Eldest Senior Sister’s path is unpassable, then I can only condense a Dao Fruit Outline," Lu Yang said.

Several days had passed since his promotion to the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, and after stabilizing his cultivation level, Lu Yang began to contemplate which path to take moving forward.

"I wonder if there’s a way for Eldest Senior Sister to maintain her humanity after Harmonization," he sighed. If Eldest Senior Sister could stay human after Harmonization, that would be the best possible outcome.

Unfortunately, he had asked Eldest Senior Sister this question, but she had not given him a straightforward answer.

"Fairy, how does one condense a Dao Fruit Outline?" Lu Yang directly asked the founder of the Dao Fruit path, Fairy Eternity, who was lying on the bed, hugging a pillow.

Hearing his words, Fairy Eternity sat up neatly from the bed and moved the pillow to lean against the wall, then leaned back on it herself.

"It’s quite simple, it depends on which Dao Fruit Outline you want. Depending on the type of Dao Fruit, they can be divided into ’Causality-Engaging’ Dao Fruits and ’Causality-Severing’ Dao Fruits."

"My Immortal Dao Fruit and Meng Junzi’s Borrowing Dao Fruit belong to the former, while other people’s Dao Fruits belong to the latter."

"The ultimate realm for the former is Omniscience, and the ultimate realm for the latter is Transcendence."

"Regardless of which type of Dao Fruit you wish to condense, the method is the same - understanding."

"The Time Immortal could condense the Time Dao Fruit Outline because he is born of the Innate Jianmu, the being with the longest lifespan, and is innately sensitive to time-related magic skills."

"Immortal Jiuchong loves Yin and Yang. Thus, in order to condense the Yin-Yang Dao Fruit, he went to great lengths to observe things related to Yin and Yang, from which he understood his own truths."

"The Demon Race, in general, believes in the survival of the fittest and natural selection, which is why Xiao Ling, Lianyi, and Qilin Immortal were able to condense this kind of Dao Fruit."

"Yingtian Immortal believes that Heavenly Tribulation highlights his status and is convinced he was born to face it. So he studied various tribulations and condensed the Tribulation Dao Fruit."

"I see that you have a high comprehension of the Immortal Dao Fruit, which is why I’ve been recommending that you condense an Initial Form of Immortal Dao Fruit."

"So, it really depends on what kind of Dao Fruit you want, or to be more precise, what you wish to achieve through the Dao Fruit. Any kind of Dao Fruit has the chance to be condensed if you find the right method."

"What if, for example, I had a friend... Oh right, suppose Old Meng wanted to condense a Harem Dao Fruit?"

"That’s also possible. A Dao Fruit is either about mastering a rule or adding a rule. The Harem Dao Fruit, once condensed, adds a rule that ’everyone likes him’."

"The likely outcome is that regardless of gender or species, all beings will go crazy over him, fighting over him, and wherever he goes, it would be like stirring up a hornet’s nest."

"Let’s not and say we did," Lu Yang quickly shook his head; the Harem Dao Fruit did not sound like a good idea.

As Lu Yang pondered what kind of Dao Fruit to condense, he heard a strange voice outside the abode.

"I hear Xiao Yang has cultivated to the Transcendance Tribulation Stage?"

After pondering for a while, Lu Yang remembered the voice belonged to Daoist Buyu.

Walking out of the abode, he saw Yun Mengmeng confronting Daoist Buyu, as well as Qinghe and Second Senior Brother Ye Zijin standing to one side. It seemed that Second Senior Brother had returned with their master.

"Bad Tao Zi, what are you doing here!" Yun Mengmeng watched Daoist Buyu with wariness; he was not someone to be trifled with, as he had once kidnapped Xiao Zhi from the Secret Realm.
