Ye Zijin deeply respected his master and knew the importance of decorum. Seeing his master in a standoff with Yun Mengmeng, he chose Qinghe to face, creating a two-on-two situation, to prevent his master from being at a disadvantage.

However, for some reason, whenever Ye Zijin and Qinghe locked eyes, he couldn’t help feeling a bit guilty.

"Who is this female cultivator?"

Daoist Buyu puffed out his whiskers and glared, "I am the Peak Master of Sky Gate Mountain; it’s you who’s the odd one here!"

In just a little over ten years that he hadn’t returned, all sorts of bizarre buildings had sprung up on Sky Gate Mountain. What on earth was this Soybean Temple?

"That’s right, you’re the Sect Leader," Yun Mengmeng then remembered Daoist Buyu’s identity. Subconsciously, she had always thought of Xiao Zhi as the Peak Master of Sky Gate Mountain.

"So, should I give you Spirit Stones then? I seem to have been living here for free all these years!" Yun Mengmeng started counting how many Spirit Stones she had on hand, and if it wasn’t enough, she might need to ask Xiao Zhi for an advance on her living expenses.

Once the debt of Spirit Stones was settled, she could continue berating him for being a rotten peach.

"Greetings, Master, Second Senior Brother."

"Truly at the Transcendance Tribulation Stage now, almost catching up to your master’s Cultivation Level!" Daoist Buyu saw Lu Yang and laughed heartily, repeatedly praising him as a good disciple.

"Having cultivated to this level, there’s not much more I can teach you, disciple. The path ahead is for you to tread on your own."

Ye Zijin smiled and slapped Lu Yang’s arm, also grinning broadly, "Junior Brother, you’ve really made a name for yourself. Just stepping out brings honor. On our way back, we encountered quite a few of Master’s acquaintances. Initially, they were all out to kill Master but, hearing that Master was returning to see you, they said they’d wait until after meeting you to resume their pursuit."

Lu Yang felt this didn’t seem like such an honorable matter.

"Master."

Upon hearing that Daoist Buyu had returned, Eldest Senior Sister and Third Senior Sister both came.

Daoist Buyu comforted them with a broad smile, "Very good. Our sect is finally all together. Today, we must celebrate properly!"

Lu Yang looked at Daoist Buyu in surprise. Our sect isn’t all together because it’s all because of you, Elder, always running around outside, isn’t it?

After all, a master is a master, and when it came to thick-skinned skills, he was just an amateur compared to his master.

With all of Daoist Buyu’s disciples gathered, Yun Mengmeng volunteered to be the Spirit Chef with Qinghe and Lu Yang assisting her, while Ye Zijin turned Talismans into fireworks to set the atmosphere. Gan Tian let the ancient zither spontaneously play tunes, and Yun Zhi contemplated whether or not to move the positions of stars in the sky to spell out a sentence, but in the end, deemed it too ostentatious and abandoned the idea. freewebnovel.com

"This young lady, your culinary skills are really something!" Daoist Buyu exclaimed after tasting the dish Yun Mengmeng made, amazed by its heavenly flavor.

"When I passed through Demon City, I was invited by the Demon Emperor to dine at the Imperial Palace. The Spirit Chef there was about your level!"

"It’s just that the Demon Emperor was so enthusiastic to see me that it made me feel a bit uneasy."

So Master had been invited by Little Zhu too, Lu Yang thought to himself. Little Zhu hadn’t mentioned it, though.

Zhu Tian was very tactful with his actions, not seeking credit actively, but the things he did would eventually reach the concerned parties’ ears.

As Lu Yang thought about this, he picked up another bite of the dish. Although it wasn’t his first time eating it, he was still amazed. Sister Mengmeng’s cooking was indeed delicious, far beyond what Immortal Fairy could compare to.

"Little Zhu’s enthusiasm towards you is, of course, because of Little Yang," Immortal Fairy got carried away by the atmosphere and emerged from Lu Yang’s body of her own accord.

"Whoa, who the hell are you?" Daoist Buyu got a huge scare when someone suddenly popped out, especially from his little disciple’s body.

Seeing this, Qinghe hastily swallowed her food, put down her chopsticks, formed a gesture, and with the descent of lotus petals and fireworks as a backdrop, formally introduced Immortal Fairy: "This honorable being is the first amongst the Five Ancient Immortals, also the preeminent beauty of the Ancient Ten Beauties, an enlightened being of great wisdom, sole esteemed one above all below the heavens, Immortal Fairy!"

Clatter—

Daoist Buyu’s chopsticks fell to the ground.

He remembered Lu Yang saying there was an Immortal in his body; it wasn’t just a fantasy after all.

Chapter 1208: Chapter 1207: Master and Disciple Duel

Yun Mengmeng, having been introduced to Qinghe at great length, suddenly remembered what she ought to be doing, and promptly knelt to kowtow.

"Your servant greets Your Majesty!"

His Majesty appeared in front of strangers, and as the Minister of Rites, she had to present her best front.

However, Historian Qinghe was too quick, having arranged the setting before her, leaving her only to call out a couple of times.

Everyone present was shocked at the appearance of Fairy Eternity, except for Yun Zhi, who as usual silently continued eating and enjoying her good sister’s cooking skills.

Daoist Buyu admitted that in his youth, he had fantasized about having an ancient evil beast sealed within him, so it was not unexpected for Little Yang to dream of having an immortal inside him.

After all, he was at that age.

He never imagined that Little Yang was not just fantasizing, but actually had an immortal living inside him.

Initially, I only dared to fantasize having a fierce beast within, but you straight up have a female immortal inside, what was introduced just now? The foremost of the Ancient Ten Beauties, just listening to this title tells you how beautiful she is.

Daoist Buyu pondered carefully, realizing this was his first encounter with an immortal and didn’t know how to properly greet: "Daoist Buyu has seen the immortal."

"You are Little Yang’s elder, there’s no need for you to be so formal with me," Fairy Eternity responded, as she effortlessly helped Daoist Buyu to rise.

Daoist Buyu tried hard to bend over but found he couldn’t, so he gave up on the formal greeting.

"So it turns out that the immortal has always resided within my young disciple, it seems his rapid progress in cultivation is also thanks to the immortal’s guidance."

"Oh it’s not just my guidance, Little Yang himself possesses outstanding talents."

Not the Fairy, since we’ve met, what guidance have you provided me? Ancient shameful pasts, then I got struck by the Yingtian Immortal, then I broke through the limits of the Void Refinement Stage...

The more Lu Yang recalled, the more he couldn’t continue, indeed it seemed his ability to advance to the Transcendance Tribulation Stage was because of Fairy Eternity.

If it hadn’t been for Fairy Eternity, he would just be progressing methodically to the Body Integration Realm.

"It turns out Little Yang is protected by an immortal, initially I was worried about Little Yang’s lack of worldly experience, now I can confidently hand over the position of Sect Leader to Little Yang."

"Don’t worry, giving the Sect Leader position to Little Yang, I assure you there won’t be any issues..."

"Hold on, you two, when did I ever agree to become the Sect Leader?" Lu Yang hastily pulled over the enthusiastic Fairy Eternity, who was all too happy to escalate the situation.

Daoist Buyu spoke earnestly, "Little Yang, your master knows the process of becoming a Sect Master, it involves declining three times and accepting on the fourth. Your master went through it too."

"However, your excellence is apparent to everyone in the Seek Dao Sect, no one would object to you becoming the Sect Leader directly."

"Your master is getting old, some things are beyond my abilities now, my greatest wish in life is to see you younger generations grow strong and take over the responsibilities we shoulder."

"No, Master, you’re only two thousand years old, you still have eight thousand years of lifespan left!" Lu Yang was dumbfounded, he could hardly utter such an absurd statement.

"So, the position of Sect Leader is yours!" Daoist Buyu made the decision without further discussion, he had planned to do so upon his return to the Seek Dao Sect, now seeing that Lu Yang had the support of an immortal praised as the foremost among the Ancient Five Immortals, there was no doubt he could handle being the Sect Leader.

"No, I refuse."

"I am the Sect Leader; you must obey me!"

"I have an Acting Sect Leader experience voucher, you can’t control me!"

Both master and disciple saw in each other’s eyes a steadfast belief.

"If that’s the case, then we must battle!" both said simultaneously.

Being from the Sword Cultivators of the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, known for their offensive capabilities, the premises of Sky Gate Mountain was too small to contain their might,

Both simultaneously flew towards the inner regions of the Seek Dao Sect, settling in a desolate mountainous area where no one resided.

The others followed suit, picking a nearby spot to watch the battle. Yun Mengmeng didn’t forget to carry the platter and table while Qinghe, Gan Tian, and Ye Zijin helped with carrying. Yun Zhi set up a protective barrier to prevent any harm from the swirling sword qi of the two fighters.

Daoist Buyu and Lu Yang each stood atop the mountain, silent without a word.

No one announced the start, but the two drew their swords and unleashed their Swordsmanship Domains simultaneously.

Boom—

The moment their Swordsmanship Domains collided, a massive sphere of sword qi formed. Countless sword energies whirled within the sphere, and in the blink of an eye, the mountains and earth caught between them vanished, leaving only a crescent-shaped deep pit.

Daoist Buyu’s eyes shone with a fighting spirit, for it was the first time since he had grasped his Swordsmanship Domain that he encountered someone who could match him in swordsmanship.

Similarly, Lu Yang found his equal for the first time during the Sword Inquiry Ceremony. Facing all sword cultivators across the world, he had never met an opponent who matched him until now.

"Very well, I was worried you had jumped straight to the Transcendance Tribulation Stage and your combat sense and swordsmanship comprehension couldn’t keep up. It seems I was overly concerned!"

Daoist Buyu laughed heartily, unleashing his sword qi carelessly and sweeping forward. The sword qi surged like waves, a white gleam everywhere—this was a killing sword technique hardly ever used.

Among those of the same realm, all would avoid the sharpness of this move.

Lu Yang’s right arm vibrated as he too executed boundless sword qi, like a torrent pouring downhill, sweeping the desolate frontier. Then, his sword qi transformed into the shapes of a black dragon, a golden phoenix, and a white qiongqi, rushing towards Daoist Buyu.

Countless halos burst in the air and then exploded, shattering space and steaming up spiritual energy, boiling over the heavens!

In moments, the two exchanged hundreds of moves, their speed so fast that even other practitioners in the Transcendance Tribulation Stage could barely keep up, let alone manage to block and attack every strike.

"Buddha Land in Palm!"

A hand appeared, vast and boundless, covering the entire mountain range, thunderously descending as if the sky were collapsing.

Daoist Buyu felt a suction force at the palm, unable to resist, pulling him in. freēwēbnovel.com

He tried to slash out a wave of sword qi, all absorbed by the palm.

"Spatial Divine Ability, huh? Heaven and Earth in an Inch!"

Daoist Buyu smiled faintly, countering spatial divine ability with spatial divine ability, stepping through space in one move to reach the back of the hand—an attacker’s blind spot.

However, before he could rejoice, he saw above him a darker mass—a second palm!

Lu Yang had executed Buddha Land in Palm twice simultaneously, specifically to prevent Daoist Buyu from being at the back of the hand!

Daoist Buyu’s expression changed, wanting to use Heaven and Earth in an Inch to escape again, but it was too late.

The second palm struck the back of the first palm, with Daoist Buyu caught in between, as if two small worlds had collided.

After the palms vanished, Daoist Buyu emerged, gasping for breath, his clothes tattered and his vitality greatly damaged.

"Master, you should concede. I still haven’t used the Immortal Sword Technique or the Imitation Fist."

Despite being temporarily at a disadvantage, Daoist Buyu, unwilling to concede, wiped the blood from the corner of his mouth and flatly rejected Lu Yang’s suggestion, "Concede? I’ve never conceded in my life! You think this is all I have? Have you forgotten my Sword Opens Heaven’s Gate!"

"Go, Second-in-command! I believe you can win!" One side was the second-in-command, one side was Daoist Buyu; Yun Mengmeng naturally supported the second-in-command without hesitation.

"Hey, why aren’t you guys cheering?" Yun Mengmeng noticed she was the only one shouting; Gan Tian and Ye Zijin remained silent, as if they weren’t concerned about the outcome of the battle.

Gan Tian shook her head helplessly and explained, "Does it make a difference who becomes Sect Leader between them? In the end, won’t Eldest Senior Sister still be the one doing all the work?"

Yun Mengmeng thought about it and realized the truth; the second-in-command was also busy expanding the territory for the Great Bean Dynasty and wouldn’t have time to be Sect Leader.

Gan Tian turned to Eldest Senior Sister and asked, "By the way, Eldest Senior Sister, they said they wanted to fight, but did they specify how to decide the position of Sect Leader?"

Eldest Senior Sister spoke lightly, "Naturally, whoever wins becomes the Sect Leader."

Chapter 1209: Chapter 1208: The Death of Lu Yang

High above in the sky, master and disciple stood sword to sword, their breaths held, the powerful aura rendering the world silent.

The duel between two of the strongest sword cultivators of the age was unfolding – in the blink of an eye, hundreds of moves were exchanged, and a moment of distraction could determine the winner.

As Eldest Senior Sister’s voice fell, Daoist Buyu watched Lu Yang with gratification, realizing that his little disciple had grown so much without his knowledge.

Perhaps, it was time to let go.

"After some careful consideration, seeing as your master has never admitted defeat in his life, it might be interesting to try the taste of defeat. Your master has decided, your master admits..."

Whoosh— fɾeeweɓnѳveɭ.com

Sharp Sword Qi came rushing towards him, forcing Daoist Buyu to muster his energy to deflect it.

Before he could speak again, he saw Lu Yang instantly move to stand before him.

Clang—

Eye to eye, their swords collided, shaking the heavens and the earth!

"Master, what were you saying just now, I didn’t hear clearly. Were you going to say you think you will surely win? I think so too, Master, you win..."

"Good disciple, your master is getting old and can’t beat you anymore!"

The originally one-handed Daoist Buyu suddenly gripped the sword hilt with both hands and, with a burst of strength, pushed Lu Yang into an inferior position, cutting him off mid-sentence.

Then, with another burst of force, Lu Yang felt as if he was no longer facing a person, but continuous towering mountains, so heavy they were almost unthinkable. Each time he tried to speak, he felt his master’s strength increase, interrupting him!

The Inheriting Shadow Sword and the Seven Star Sword Set flew out from the Green Blade Sword Small World, forming the Extinguish Immortal Sword Array above Lu Yang’s head.

Daoist Buyu was on alert. He had heard that this was Xiao Zhi’s war trophy from Emperor Wu Yao of Yu. Xiao Zhi also said that this Extinguish Immortal Sword Array could be traced back to the Kirin Immortal!

Which indicated the immense power of this Sword Array!

Underneath the Extinguish Immortal Sword Array, Lu Yang felt his body beyond control, and with a thump, he knelt to the ground, his posture exceedingly proper.

"Disciple is indeed not as good as his master..."

"Sword Opens Heaven’s Gate!"

Daoist Buyu bellowed, his sword’s edge blazed brilliantly like a rainbow, piercing and cold as ice, pointing straight to the sky. The Extinguish Immortal Sword Array collapsed, and Lu Yang plummeted to the ground like a meteor shower, creating an abyss as deep as could be.

Daoist Buyu spat out a mouthful of fresh blood, propped himself up with one hand on the ground, and clutched his chest with the other, trembling like chaff in the wind.

"Although ’Sword Opens Heaven’s Gate’ is your master’s ultimate move, it comes with a great cost. Your master no longer has the strength to..."

Along with a dragon’s roar, the ground trembled. Utilizing Earth Shrinking, Lu Yang appeared beneath Daoist Buyu’s feet. Sword Qi transformed into a dragon, taking Daoist Buyu soaring into the sky.

Daoist Buyu’s body shook, shattering the dragon-shaped Sword Qi, and he returned to the ground.

Both understood that admitting defeat directly was impossible, always interrupted by the other. Only by defeating the opponent and rendering them speechless could they concede defeat.

If that’s the case, then there was a straightforward solution.

"Let us settle it with one move!"

"That is exactly my intention!"

"Sword Opens Heaven’s Gate!"

"Immortal Sword Technique!"

The two gathered their strength, their auras peaking simultaneously, unleashing their strongest sword skills!

The way of the sword was resplendent, turning the dark night as bright as day. The entire Seek Dao Sect could feel the clash of the two Sword Qis!

The space vibrated, and dust filled the air.

Lu Yang was overpowered by Daoist Buyu, sent flying backward, as if he had lost all his strength, crashing through two mountains and embedding into the cliffside of a third.

Seeing Lu Yang motionless, Daoist Buyu flew over with smug assurance to show off.

"Good disciple, in the end, you are not quite..."

Daoist Buyu was about to admit defeat when his expression suddenly changed dramatically. The aura of Lu Yang, stuck on the cliff face, was rapidly fading!

"What’s happened to you?"

Lu Yang, with his last dying breath, raised his hand, trying to reach for Daoist Buyu, but he was too weak to muster any strength.

"Master will always be Master... Disciple’s skills are inferior... dying without regrets..."

Speechless Daoist frantically infused spiritual essence into Lu Yang’s body, but it flowed away just as quickly, like air leaking from a balloon.

Those who were watching the battle while eating hurried over to check the situation, and upon seeing this scene, they all fell silent.

"Xiao Zhi, save him quickly!" Speechless Daoist urged anxiously.

Yun Zhi could only shake her head helplessly; even she was powerless to reverse such a situation.

Fairy Eternity flew out from Lu Yang’s body, lying on his chest and wailing bitterly.

"Little Yang, why did you just die like this—"

"It’s all because I failed to protect you!"

"How can I live without you!"

Her crying was like raindrops on pear blossoms, her tearful eyes misty, touching the hearts of those who heard.

The place fell deathly silent, save for Fairy Eternity’s sobbing.

Master and disciple fought over the position of Sect Leader, resulting in Speechless Daoist striking down his own disciple; power struggles, infighting among comrades, a tragedy of the mortal world—nothing could be more sorrowful.

"Right, I can give you the Initial Form of Immortal Dao Fruit!"

"...no need for that."

Lu Yang used his last bit of energy to prevent Fairy Eternity from reviving him, his words intermittent, "Master... before your disciple dies... I have no other wishes... just hoping you will be a good Sect Leader... leading our Sect to glory..."

"Eldest Senior Sister is very tired... Don’t let her continue as Acting Sect Leader..."

"Okay, okay, I promise, Master promises you everything!" Speechless Daoist, holding Lu Yang’s gradually cooling hand, said hastily.

Hearing this, Lu Yang seemed to have settled a weighty matter in his mind; his body was cold, his wrist limp and drooping, and he passed away with a smile.

His breath had ceased, clearly, he was dead.

Speechless Daoist remained silent.

"Wait, that’s not right, if Master has agreed then there’s no need for me to feign death." Lu Yang, following the mood of the moment, pretended to be dead, but halfway through, he realized something was amiss.

If Master already won, what was there to pretend about?

"He’s playing possum?!" Speechless Daoist quickly pressed Lu Yang back down.

"Your last wish, as your Master, I will fulfill it all, so rest in peace, my good disciple."

Lu Yang resisted Speechless Daoist’s hand and sat up; Speechless Daoist could not keep him down: "I really am still alive."

The two looked at each other, Speechless Daoist asked uncertainly, "Pretending to be dead?"

"Pretending to be dead."

They were silent once more, then they heard Speechless Daoist draw his sword to strike: "Clever boy, you dare to deceive me!"

Lu Yang rolled over, dodging the lethal sword: "Master, it was you who taught me to use wit and bravery in battle!"

"I certainly did not teach you to use them against me! I’ll chop you, you unfilial disciple!"

"Law of Heaven!"

Lu Yang turned into a being of spiritual energy, causing Speechless Daoist’s sword to miss its mark.

"Stop dodging!"

"Stop chopping!"

The two chased each other around the crowd, both of them exhausted after a long scuffle. Finally, they calmed down.

Speechless Daoist stopped and pointed at Lu Yang, laughing heartily: "Good, you’re something, boy, even more unprincipled than me!"

"I’m saying you don’t need my teaching! Even if I tried, I couldn’t have turned you into this."

"Well then, as we agreed before, I will remain the Sect Leader!"

Seeing Master laughing, Lu Yang also couldn’t help but burst out laughing; the laughter of master and disciple echoed through the mountains.

"Then I’ll leave the Sect affairs all to you, Master," Yun Zhi said, standing to the side.

Speechless Daoist suddenly couldn’t laugh anymore.

Chapter 1210: Chapter 1209: The Status of the Master Through the Pupil’s Prestige

Lu Yang was resurrected, Yun Zhi retired, and Daoist Buyu once again took control of Seek Dao Sect with great power, much to everyone’s joy.

Under the moonlight, everyone continued to dine, toasting and laughing together, yet only Daoist Buyu remained downcast.

Among the four disciples, only Ye Zijin, who had spent days and nights with Daoist Buyu, was the most filial and comfortingly said,

"Master, today is a day of reunion for our Sky Gate Mountain, please smile a bit more. Tomorrow, when you become Sect Leader, you might not be able to smile at all."

Daoist Buyu: "..."

You have already surpassed me.

"I originally intended to impart Sword Opens Heaven’s Gate to Xiao Yang as a congratulatory gift for his ascending to Sect Leader, but it seems now that it won’t be necessary."

Just now, Lu Yang’s feigned death had given Daoist Buyu quite a scare, and upon recalling the exchange of moves during their clash, as well as the power of the Immortal Sword Technique,

Daoist Buyu faintly felt that the Immortal Sword Technique was a sword skill even more formidable than Sword Opens Heaven’s Gate.

Since Xiao Yang already had his unique sword technique, there was no need to learn his moves.

For sword cultivators, focus is of utmost importance; biting off more than one can chew is unwise. Sword Opens Heaven’s Gate is not easy to master and Xiao Yang shouldn’t waste a year and a half to learn it.

...

The news of Daoist Buyu regaining great power spread throughout the entire Seek Dao Sect, leaving everyone immensely shocked.

"Who is Daoist Buyu?"

Of course, this was a rarity, comparable to those like the initial Lu Yang, who knew little about the Cultivation World and had never heard of the famous Daoist Buyu.

"What, you mean our Seek Dao Sect actually has a Sect Leader?"

"What, isn’t the Sect Leader called Eldest Senior Sister?"

"Are you dumb? If she’s called Eldest Senior Sister, could she be the Sect Leader?"

"I always thought calling Yun Zhi Eldest Senior Sister meant that she was the eldest amongst the elders’ generation, and it just became a habit passed down to our generation. So, she’s actually from ours?"

"Quiet! You shouldn’t speak carelessly, making it sound like Eldest Senior Sister is over two thousand years old!"

Occasionally descending the mountain, Lu Yang heard the discussions of the junior brothers and sisters and sighed at how young they were. He remembered the times when he was just as ignorant of danger until Eldest Senior Sister threw him to the border, where he quickly learned to behave.

"Speaking of which, there was never an official statement regarding the relationship between Eldest Senior Sister and the position of Sect Leader."

Lu Yang recalled his experiences since joining Seek Dao Sect. The matter of Eldest Senior Sister acting as the Sect Leader was always passed down by word of mouth, so it was no wonder the new disciples were unaware of the facts.

Daoist Buyu looked at the congratulatory letters fluttering in like snowflakes, feeling quite angry.

"Did you all have Zijin write these congratulatory letters? They all sound so sarcastic!"

What consoled Daoist Buyu was that there were also a few letters that were sincerely meant.

Such as those from Demon City, from Western Paradise Temple, from the East Sea Dragon Clan.

The only problem was that they began their messages differently from others, all uniformly starting with: Lu Yang, his master, and so on...

"This must be what people mean by ’the disciple’s honor reflects upon the master.’"

Outside Seek Dao Sect, several Transcendance Tribulation Stage cultivators gathered to discuss heatedly, their indignation causing them to slap their thighs in frustration.

"Didn’t Old Buyu just tell us he was going to visit Lu Yang? How has he become the Sect Leader now?"

"Damn it, we’ve been tricked by that old sly fox!"

"Always so treacherous and cunning!"

"I knew we couldn’t believe a word that old thief said!"

After much discussion, they reluctantly came to a conclusion that there was nothing they could do, they couldn’t very well squat at the gates of Seek Dao Sect waiting for Old Buyu, who might not come out for a whole year and a half.

At the top floor of Scripture Pavilion, the minimum requirement to access this level was to be in the Body Integration Realm.

Now that Lu Yang had surpassed this requirement, he easily entered the highest floor.

As Lu Yang walked on the top floor, any scripture he casually picked from the shelves was at least of the Body Integration Realm, even the Transcendance Tribulation Stage techniques were not in short supply.

In order to compose the "Mind Seeing Method", Tribulation Crossing Chapter, these references were indispensable.

"But why do these techniques look so ancient?"

Lu Yang noticed that some techniques were noticeably different in color from the rest, extremely old, it was unclear how long they had been there.

"Ah, I see, these techniques were provided by the prisoners of Captive Peak."

Lu Yang realized, with each capture of a prisoner from Captive Peak, a treasure location was obtained, where these prisoners had collected these techniques.

Considering there were more than a hundred prisoners from the Body Integration Realm, it was clear that these old techniques had been acquired from them.

Presumably, Elder Brother Dai had led people to scour these treasure locations, keeping the valuable Heaven and Earth Treasures in the treasury of Sky Gate Mountain and placing the techniques on the top floor of Scripture Pavilion.

Previously, Lu Yang did not have the privilege to access the top floor, unaware of these matters; now seeing them, he figured it out quite simply.

"Mountain and Sea Immortal Technique", "Sealing God Technique"?

Two techniques were particularly conspicuous, their names indicating they were anything but ordinary.

With Lu Yang’s level of insight, he wasn’t fully capable of comprehending the mysteries of Immortal Level Techniques, but he could grasp the general idea. freewёbnoνel.com

"Are these Guan Shanhai and The Controller’s techniques?"

"The two of them sure gave a thorough account," Lu Yang chuckled. These two’s techniques, if released into the world, would cause untold chaos, for they directly pointed towards becoming an Immortal, and with careful study, one could find the opportunity to form an outline of Dao Fruit.

Of course, whether one could condense an outline of Dao Fruit depended on one’s comprehension.

"One embodies the universe within the heart, evolving the world and the other uses the Power of Faith to seal the gods and become the source of belief, both quite imaginative." Fairy Eternity marveled, finding the approaches of these two techniques unique, never having appeared even in Ancient Times.

Although Guan Shanhai and The Controller were prisoners, they were also Immortals, protagonists who had dominated their respective eras for a hundred thousand years.

Those who cultivated to Immortal status were without exception geniuses, each with their own unique skills.

Their luck was just poor, having encountered Yun Zhi.

Hearing Little Yang mutter as he scrutinized the techniques, Fairy Eternity was quite astonished, "Isn’t it because their fates weren’t as strong as yours, and you imprisoned them in Captive Peak?"

Lu Yang could only roughly understand Immortal Level techniques, but he could leisurely read Tribulation-Passing Level techniques and comprehend them with ease.

Something other Transcendance Stage cultivators could not accomplish, not even Daoist Buyu.

Lu Yang’s level of insight had already surpassed that of the Transcendance Stage.

If insight had a level, Lu Yang’s would be of the Half-Immortal level.

Half-Immortal techniques were also available; if Lu Yang wished, Ao Ling, Jiang Lianyi, and others would also be willing to share their respective techniques with him.

But intuition told Lu Yang that none of these were what he needed.

He had a vague sense that he had grasped a shred of inspiration regarding the outline of Dao Fruit, yet couldn’t quite articulate what it was.

"Does it have something to do with my cultivation technique?"

"What’s this... ’Sword Opens Heaven’s Gate’?"

Lu Yang set aside his concerns about cultivation techniques and eagerly began to learn.

Five days later, Lu Yang returned Sword Opens Heaven’s Gate to its original place.

"I’ve learned it."

Chapter 1211: Chapter 1210 Qilin’er

After relaxing from mastering the Sword Opens Heaven’s Gate, Lu Yang continued to study cultivation techniques.

The matter of cultivation techniques was related to his future path in cultivating, so, even though Eldest Senior Sister helped him revise the techniques to guarantee a base level, Lu Yang dared not slack off.

Months passed by, during which Lu Yang had stayed in the Scripture Pavilion and had never left the top floor.

He had memorized all the techniques on the top floor and had analyzed the strengths and weaknesses of others’ techniques.

"Guan Shanhai’s ’Mountain and Sea Immortal Technique’ can evolve the heaven and earth, The Controller’s ’Sealing God Technique’ can become the source of faith; whether it’s an immortal level technique or a tribulation crossing level technique, each inherently possesses a significant effect."

"The sole effect of the ’Mind Seeing Method’ is to persist on one’s true self, to see one’s nature clearly... Fairy, could the condition to condense the Eternity Dao Fruit be to persist in true self and to see one’s nature clearly?"

Recalling Sister Mengmeng and the Fairy’s behavior, Lu Yang could easily identify a common trait between them.

"Have you always said I could condense the Eternity Dao Fruit because of this reason?"

Floating around Lu Yang, Immortal Fairy chuckled upon hearing his words: "Indeed, it’s one of the reasons."

"The most fundamental condition for the Eternity Dao Fruit is that the heart must remain immortal, unaffected by the passage of years, without major personality changes or deviating from one’s original intention."

"Are there many such people?" Lu Yang could not recall seeing anyone like that.

Yawning, Immortal Fairy continued: "There are many, it’s just that you have cultivated too quickly and never had the chance to meet such people. In ancient times, Immortal here had seen countless such people, living longer and pursuing power, becoming less and less human."

"You don’t have to worry about this when cultivating the Clear Mind Technique."

Lu Yang suddenly understood; Eldest Senior Sister initially made him cultivate the Clear Mind Technique likely for this purpose.

Understanding the true meaning of the Clear Mind Technique, Lu Yang had new ideas for continuing the Tribulation Crossing Chapter.

...

"Eldest Senior Sister, this is the new technique I’ve written."

Lu Yang took out the recently written technique, his months of accumulation and enlightenment all focused within this text.

Remembering the times when he had shown his techniques to Eldest Senior Sister, Lu Yang felt nervous, neither able to sit nor stand, fearing Eldest Senior Sister might say it was insufficient.

It was not until he noticed Eldest Senior Sister’s slight smile that his heart trembled.

"Well written."

"Eldest Senior Sister, has my technique passed?"

Yun Zhi did not directly answer his question but returned the technique to Lu Yang: "Since you reached the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, each thing you do may become an opportunity to form an outline of your Dao Fruit; and your technique is particularly significant for the Dao Fruit Outline."

"If I intervene too much, it might actually harm you; after the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, you must ultimately rely on yourself"

Hearing Eldest Senior Sister say this, Lu Yang did not feel overjoyed but felt a melancholic sense of loss.

The path Eldest Senior Sister had laid out for him ended here; he could grow without her protection, which also meant that she would no longer provide help in his future cultivation.

Boom—

A sudden clap of thunder interrupted Lu Yang’s sadness.

"Is someone going to Pass Tribulation?"

Following the sound of the thunder, Lu Yang saw it originated from Old Meng’s location.

"That’s right, it’s time for Old Meng to break through."

With the lifting of the Sun seal and the restoration of the Sun and Lunar Power to the standards of the Ancient Times, Meng Jingzhou’s opportunities came one after another, surpassing the hardships of living.

Before Lu Yang had entered the Scripture Pavilion, he heard Old Meng had gone somewhere to experience the mortal trials.

Since it drew the thunder, it seemed the trials were highly successful.

Thunder, manifesting the might of heaven, repeatedly struck, and Meng Jingzhou’s figure appeared as tiny as an insect before the thunder, his body lacerated yet resiliently persevering.

"It’s strange, why does Old Meng have only eighty-one thunders?"

Lu Yang thought about himself facing one hundred sixty-two thunders; Old Meng should also have drawn at least one hundred sixty thunders.

"Could it really be that Senior Yingtian Immortal is targeting me?"

Like Meng Jingzhou’s tribulation, the Seek Dao Sect’s disciples also kept their eyes on Meng Jingzhou on the mountaintop.

Thunder Tribulation and Heart Tribulation had ended, and heavenly nectar descended to nourish Meng Jingzhou’s body.

Meng Jingzhou clenched his fist slightly, feeling the explosive power within his body, and he let out an excited long howl.

He had reached the Transcendance Tribulation Stage as well.

Once he condensed the Dao Fruit Outline and then the complete Dao Fruit to become an immortal, he would be liberated!

Becoming an immortal was within reach, how could he not be excited!

"Hahaha, excellent, excellent, the Meng Family has a successor!" Before anyone could celebrate, Meng Junzi unexpectedly showed up at Seek Dao Sect.

As the most outstanding talent of the Meng Family, Meng Jingzhou’s crucial event of Transcendance could not be missed by Meng Junzi.

Lu Yang noticed that Eldest Senior Sister’s expression was calm, not surprised by Meng Junzi’s arrival; he thought that Meng Junzi’s visit to Seek Dao Sect must have been informed to Eldest Senior Sister in advance.

"Great Ancestor." Meng Jingzhou got dressed before paying his respects. Eighty-one bolts of Thunder Tribulation would reduce any material to ashes.

"Truly worthy of being our Meng Family’s Qilin’er!" Meng Junzi had never been as happy as he was today.

No, defeating Jiang Pingan before the founding of the nation was equally thrilling.

"Great Ancestor, calling me Qilin’er, isn’t it a bit..." Meng Jingzhou carefully said, although Qilin’er sounded complimentary, it seemed that in the heavens and earth there was only one Qilin, the Qilin Immortal.

Wouldn’t that make him the son of the Qilin Immortal?

"That’s also true, never mind, it’s not important. Let me take you to meet a few old friends."

Meng Junzi, without further ado, dragged Meng Jingzhou along and headed straight for the Imperial City.

Recently, the Great Xia Royal Family had received invigorating news; the reclusive great ancestor Jiang Pingan had once again emerged to teach the princes and princesses cultivation.

Wild State was rich in minerals. Cultivators adapted to local conditions to refine these minerals, and over time, Wild State became a gathering place for blacksmiths. There were over a hundred large and small blacksmith shops in Quyi County.

Amongst the many blacksmith shops, the Wang Family Blacksmith Shop was the most unimpressive one. Their main customers were neighbors needing repairs for their shovels, hoes, kitchen knives, and iron pots.

Small Third Grade power?

The two constables appeared in the room at some point, smiling and watching County Magistrate Lu.

Upon hearing this, County Magistrate Lu’s face changed, and then he angrily pushed Meng Jingzhou, "Get lost! Two little constables also dare to arrest me, ruining my mood for the evening!"

Meng Jingzhou remained immovable.

Lu Yang kicked County Magistrate Lu to the ground and swiftly tied him up.

County Magistrate Lu was at the Divinity Transformation Stage, but facing Lu Yang was like facing a great mountain, utterly suppressed and without a shred of resistance.

It was only then that he realized these two constables were no ordinary men.

"Who exactly are you, and who sent you! Remember, I am an official appointed by the Dynasty, you lack the grade to arrest me!"

Lu Yang was taken aback and turned to ask Meng Jingzhou, "Is there such a rule?"

Meng Jingzhou thought for a moment: "The County Magistrate is a fourth-grade official, and usually to arrest an official of this rank, one would need an official of at least the fourth grade or higher. However, that’s an unspoken rule; there’s no explicit regulation."

Lu Yang shrugged, "So it’s just an unspoken rule, then we’ll ignore it."

Lu Yang always abided by the law, acting in accordance with explicit regulations. Since they had jurisdiction over the Hundred Sword Alliance case, they could arrest anyone related to it.

"Besides, I am a Pillar State Minister myself, of higher grade than him. What’s wrong with arresting him?"

Dawn arrived, and Man Gu woke up from a deep sleep, or rather, was woken up by Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou.

"Junior Brother Man, good news, we have a big case."

"What big case?"

"We’ve arrested your superior, County Magistrate Lu."

"Ah?"

Am I still asleep?

Chapter 1219: Chapter 1218: Honest People Are Reasonable

Man Gu sat up bewildered, pondering seriously for a moment, and confirmed that this was not a dream.

The reason was simple, he couldn’t have such a dream.

"Senior Brothers, initially, I didn’t understand the norms of officialdom and offended County Magistrate Lu, which led to him always disliking me, but that’s not a reason to arrest him, is it?"

Meng Jingzhou gave a thumbs up, signaling Man Gu to be at ease, "We are all acting according to the rules and regulations, the County Magistrate has problems of his own."

Man Gu breathed a sigh of relief; indeed, both Senior Brothers were sticklers for rules and would not arrest someone for personal gain.

He remembered asking the two Senior Brothers for help, which was to capture a ghost, and spending a night to end up capturing a superior, the answer was quite obvious.

"So, was it County Magistrate Lu who was causing the trouble?"

No doubt it was the two Senior Brothers, who solved the problem that had troubled him for three months in a single day.

"That’s not quite it, we two were on the night shift when we stumbled upon an illegal organization and followed the clues to discover that County Magistrate Lu had been protecting this group all along," said Lu Yang.

"I see," Man Gu nodded.

He had confronted the County Magistrate before and didn’t have any psychological burden about it; he and Lu Yang had killed the Yanjiang County Magistrate.

Moreover, it was not a big deal now, as they were only arresting and not killing the County Magistrate.

The arrest of County Magistrate Lu was a big deal and couldn’t be kept secret, and since Lu Yang and his companion acted uprightly, there was no need to hide anything. The news of County Magistrate Lu’s arrest quickly spread throughout the entire Government Office.

"What the hell, County Magistrate Lu was arrested by the newcomers?"

Everyone in the Government Office who heard the news would freeze for a couple of seconds, their brains needing time to digest the information.

"They just started yesterday, didn’t they? And they arrested the County Magistrate the very same night?"

Having worked in the government system for so many years, they hadn’t seen or even heard of such outrageous events.

"Secretary, what do you think... Oh, you’re taking your medicine, I won’t disturb you then."

The officials had wanted to ask the secretary for his opinion, but seeing that he was shivering while taking his herbal medicine, they discreetly left.

How could the secretary not tremble? For years he had been warning Man Gu about what not to do, knowing full well that County Magistrate Lu harbored dislike for Man Gu. If it weren’t for Man Gu’s status as the Top Scorer, Lu would have caused him trouble long ago.

Man Gu’s annual performance evaluation depended on the County Magistrate’s assessment, so he had tried his best to maintain a good relationship between Man Gu and the County Magistrate.

Now, there was no need to maintain that relationship.

...

"Open court!" Man Gu, dressed in his official robes, rolled up his sleeves and smacked the table with a palm louder than the warning wood.

"Bring up the prisoner!"

"Authority—Justice—"

Two meritorious constables escorted County Magistrate Lu to the stand.

Hearing that there was another session, the citizens came to watch the excitement, and only after arriving did they believe that this time the new officials had made a real mark by capturing a high-ranking official.

Old Wang and his son, the blacksmith Wang, were shocked to see the two constables from the previous night escorting County Magistrate Lu; they were speechless with surprise.

Wasn’t it said that they were going to capture the Hundred Sword Alliance? How did they even arrest the County Magistrate?

"Man Gu, how dare you let them arrest me!" bellowed County Magistrate Lu, unable to contain his anger. These two constables were clearly directed by Man Gu!

"Why wouldn’t I dare to arrest... oh, at this time I should say, you are corrupt and have abused your power for personal gain; it is my duty to arrest you!"

"Is it true that the Hundred Sword Alliance has been regularly providing you with Spirit Stones?"

"No."

"Was it you who ordered Hundred Sword Alliance to use all means to seize swords from all over Wild State?"

"No."

"One hundred and eight swords, grades ranging from Spirit Transformation Level to Golden Core Level, were found in your room. Are these swords yours?"

"No."

"Did you violate the Dynasty’s regulations by going to the brothel after work hours? Did that happen?"

"No."

Man Gu turned his head to the secretary, who was writing feverishly, and said, "Write this down, the evidence is conclusive, but he refuses to admit guilt. He does not qualify for a lighter sentence due to confession."

Before the court session, Lu Yang and his companion had efficiently returned to gather all the evidence, including the ninety-nine people from Hundred Sword Alliance.

With so many people from Hundred Sword Alliance, the testimonies were not yet complete, so they had only questioned the main and deputy heads and the four individuals from Xuan Hei Overlord.

It wasn’t a big problem, they would complete the testimonies later and hold another court session.

"I am an official appointed by the Dynasty; no one below a fourth-grade official has the authority to deal with me!" County Magistrate Lu grew increasingly angry, regarding this as a tremendous disgrace.

"Just wait a moment."

Man Gu left these words behind as he leafed through various regulations on the spot, first checking the criminal law to confirm the charges and then the criminal procedures to determine the jurisdiction. Only then did he close the books with satisfaction.

"See, the law clearly states that I have authority over anyone in my jurisdiction. It doesn’t say lower-grade officials can’t arrest higher-grade ones."

Man Gu displayed his Identity Jade. "Besides, I am a disciple of the Seek Dao Sect. We, disciples of the Seek Dao Sect, have the right to enforce the law."

Man Gu had always seen Lu Yang and his companion as role models to learn from. If they were honest people, so was he. And honest people always act rationally.

"Alright, take him away."

Since County Magistrate Lu said nothing, Man Gu saw that there was no need for further questioning.

...

The news of Man Gu arresting his superior quickly reached the ears of the upper echelons in Wild State. Their reaction was not much better than those in the Government Office; they all hesitated for a moment, questioning if they had heard wrong.

History is often said to reflect reality, but in the combined thirty thousand years of Great Yu, Great Qian, and Great Xia, such an incident had never occurred.

"Look on the bright side, at least future generations will have a reference when studying history," joked one of the high-ranking officials, who had encountered Man Gu a few times and knew this seemed like something Man Gu would do.

"In fact, there are precedents. At the end of every dynasty, this is what the rebels did."

"Mr. Song, that is going too far. Are you implying that Man Gu is rebelling?"

"You said that, not me."

"That’s what you are implying!"

Seeing the conversation heading in an undesirable direction, Governor Lv tapped on the table: "Enough with the jokes. Although this incident is unprecedented, Man Gu’s actions are not against the rules. Based on the evidence submitted, County Magistrate Lu has indeed violated the law and should be removed from his position."

"Who should be appointed as the County Magistrate then? Man Gu? Since he became a County Magistrate, he has managed Quyi County efficiently, and there has been significant economic development."

"Of course, the economy has developed significantly. He took advantage of his fluctuation to the Body Integration Realm to go down the mines himself. He nearly excavated an entire vein. How is that different from cheating? He cannot be allowed to become a County Magistrate."

"As long as he can develop the economy, why demand so much? Why shouldn’t he use his cultivation level?"

"If not Man Gu, then who? Zhongshan County scarcely has anyone impressive; who could take on such a responsibility?"

Governor Lv shook his head and made his decision: "Indeed, Man Gu is not suitable. Although he is the Top Scorer, his experience is still insufficient. A promotion of such a nature would require an order from the Dynasty. In my opinion, the County Magistrate of Guyuan County in Zhongshan County is prudent and experienced and commands respect. He could be appointed as the County Magistrate."

Chapter 1220: Chapter 1219: The Drought Demon Appears, Catastrophe of World Annihilation!

Quyi County outskirts cemetery.

A sneaky figure danced a bizarre dance, and a great door appeared beneath his feet.

He followed the door down into an underground tomb.

The figure excitedly rubbed his hands together, the method indeed worked, and it opened the tomb.

However, the tomb chamber was empty, lacking the imagined rare treasures and valuable antiques, holding only a pitch-black coffin with its four corners nailed down by blood-stained nails, and atop the coffin lay a palm-sized seal.

He stealthily took the seal, with the words "Mountain Seal" inscribed at its base.

After taking the seal, the figure hurriedly left, not noticing that the coffin was shaking.

...

Corpse Chasing Sect.

"Typically, there are two methods of cultivation for those at the Void Refinement Stage, Red Dust Mortality or War Feeds War..."

As Zhao Po was promoted to the Void Refinement Stage, Lu Baqian personally instructed him, imparting various techniques of the stage.

Zhao Po was listening intently when suddenly a crisp sound came from within Lu Baqian’s embrace, as if something had shattered!

Lu Baqian pulled out an object from within, a broken piece of Jade.

"Damn, the seal has been broken!" exclaimed Lu Baqian, his expression drastically changing.

"Sect Leader, what happened?" Zhao Po asked hurriedly.

"The seal is gone!"

"Seal? What seal?" Zhao Po still didn’t understand.

"Six thousand years ago, one of our forebears in the Corpse Chasing Sect, for some unknown reason, let a zombie he had created slip beyond his control. That zombie had already cultivated to ’Unformable Bone,’ just half a step away from becoming a Drought Demon!"

"The forebear and his zombie waged a fierce battle, and he desperately sealed the zombie but perished in the process, only fragmented messages returned to the Sect."

"But the most critical location of the seal wasn’t communicated back, leaving our sect unable to deal with that zombie."

"Now, six thousand years have passed, and although that zombie was sealed, now that it has broken free, it must have reached the ’Drought Demon’ Realm!"

Upon hearing this, Zhao Po’s expression also severely changed, a Drought Demon appearing meant scorched lands for thousands of miles, a catastrophe capable of ending the world!

"Our Sect’s Elders have all vested their cultivation in their zombies, and the Drought Demon has absolute control over other zombies; they can’t join the battle, so I’m the only one who can act!"

"We could ask the Dynasty for help!"

"It’s too late, once a Drought Demon appears, it will undoubtedly flee. Once it gains strength, even those at the Tribulation Crossing Stage will be unable to contend with it; we must go quickly!"

Lu Baqian pulled out a compass, rotated the ’compass’ on the compass, and the direction finally stopped at the east! ƒreewebɳovel.com

"It seems that the Drought Demon is in the east!"

Oddly, Zhao Po’s heart panicked; he always felt that something bad was about to happen.

The Sect Leader facing this might be more dangerous than lucky.

"Sect Leader, isn’t there another way to deal with that Drought Demon?"

"There is one possibility; our forebear possessed a Mountain Suppressing Seal, which is highly effective against Drought Demons, but this seal was crafted by the hermit family, the Divine Craftsman Wang Family!"

Lu Baqian sighed, "The Divine Craftsman Wang Family has been lost for a hundred years, nowhere to be found."

"Battling the Drought Demon is perhaps my destined fate!"

...

"Am I finally rid of this damned seal?" the coffin rattled as the female Drought Demon murmured to herself, how long had she waited for this day, three thousand or five thousand years?

Zombies, as long as their Spiritual Wisdom is not destroyed, and their bodies are not demolished, will grow stronger over time; a seal can only slow this process.

Over these six thousand years, she had slowly grown stronger, finally advancing from Unformable Bone to Drought Demon.

But becoming a true Drought Demon wasn’t so simple; rejected by heaven and earth, only by undergoing the Heavenly Tribulation, Earth Tribulation, and Human Tribulation could one truly become a Drought Demon.

Five hundred years ago, tribulation clouds appeared in the tomb chamber, striking her to near death; fortunately, she survived, this was the Heavenly Tribulation.

The Earth Tribulation was the Mountain Suppressing Seal pressing on the coffin; only by removing it could she pass through the Earth Tribulation.

With the Mountain Suppressing Seal stolen by a grave robber, she was left with only the Human Tribulation.

"My current Realm is at the Half-step Tribulation Crossing Stage, once I emerge, I should encounter a Cultivator of similar strength; only by defeating this Cultivator can I transcend the Human Tribulation!"

The female Drought Demon chuckled, this was her domain, no one below the Tribulation Crossing Stage could defeat her unless they used the Mountain Suppressing Seal!

...

"If you ask me, our approach was all wrong; if looking for ghosts, then of course we should search in the cemetery," Constable Lu analyzed earnestly.

"Your words are sensible," Constable Meng nodded, agreeing with his colleague’s opinion.

Wandering around the town in the dead of night and not even encountering a ghost’s shadow, it was better to take proactive action rather than passively wait.

Two new constables, eager to prove themselves, resolved to handle the unexplained haunting incident no matter what.

"I heard there’s a deserted area on the outskirts of Quyi County that’s often used for burials; perhaps there are some aggrieved spirits there."

The two immediately agreed and headed to the cemetery on the outskirts.

Normally, a cemetery was a place of intense Yin Energy, and any mortal who was physically weak could be possessed upon visiting.

Meng Jingzhou arrived and yawned, his breath slightly escaping him, instantly dispersing the Yin Energy.

"Hey, focus on the job," Lu Yang reminded, "We’re in uniform, representing the Dynasty; we don’t want any ghosts thinking we are slacking off."

Meng Jingzhou snorted, "Mind your own business."

As the two bickered, the ground suddenly shifted and a burst of Qi soared into the sky, terrifyingly intense!

A stunningly beautiful woman appeared before them; although her complexion was pale, her beauty remained undeniable.

Bathed in the moonlight, the Drought Demon delightfully discovered that the Yin Energy was stronger than before the seal, which could help her grow even stronger.

She immediately set her sights on the two on-duty constables.

"Two little constables, huh? It’s been a while since I’ve fed, I’ll start with you!"

The Drought Demon released a terrifying aura, making the two constables tremble in fear.

A Drought Demon appears, wreaking havoc over thousands of miles!

Death Qi spread from her feet, leaving nothing alive in its wake.

This Death Qi extended a full two fathoms before stopping near Lu Yang’s feet.

However, the Drought Demon was so focused on Meng Jingzhou that she didn’t notice this anomaly.

Opening her mouth, she bit down on Meng Jingzhou’s neck, only to scream in agony and roll on the ground in pain.

"Who are you, how can you possess such terrifying Yang Qi!"

The Drought Demon’s pain was heart-wrenching; normally, Yang Qi would nourish her, but this individual’s Yang Qi was too abundant and intense.

"It seems that I’ve heard the Grand Elder mention that this creature is a Drought Demon," Meng Jingzhou jabbed at the Drought Demon, causing sizzling smoke wherever the touch, the Pure Yang Qi corroding her.

Such intense Yang Qi, truly her nemesis; indeed, crossing the Human Tribulation wasn’t easy, was it?

Determined, the Drought Demon knew that becoming a true Drought Demon wouldn’t be easy.

If that was the case, she’d go all out!

Unreservedly, the Drought Demon released the aura of a Half-step Tribulation Crossing Stage, an aura so terrifying that even zombies must bow before her, making her the true queen of zombies!

She was the embodiment of disaster!

"Come then, let’s see what capabilities you have!"

"Stop shouting, behave yourself," Meng Jingzhou impatiently pinned her down, thinking they had found the source of the ghosts only to discover it was a Drought Demon.

"Transcendence Tribulation Stage?" The Drought Demon panicked, easily subdued by someone of only a Great Power level!

"What do you think, shall we kill her?" Lu Yang drew the Green Peak Sword, his first time facing a real Drought Demon; it seemed respectful to use the sword.

"Another Transcendence Tribulation period? And a Sword Cultivator?"

This must be a joke, one with Yang Qi enough to suppress her and another whose attacking methods are unmatched among Sword Cultivators. She thought the Human Tribulation was difficult, but she didn’t expect it to be this challenging.

How long had she slept? Were Transcendence Stage beings now working as constables?

"Don’t kill me, I surrender!" The Drought Demon hurriedly kowtowed and admitted her faults, realizing she couldn’t win against these two.

"Do you see that? Isn’t she wearing clothes from the Corpse Chasing Sect? She must be a lost zombie from their flock," Meng Jingzhou queried, noting the tattered clothes that barely revealed their origin.

"Really? Should we send her back to the Corpse Chasing Sect and let them deal with her?"

Just as the Drought Demon felt relieved about surviving, she heard Lu Yang throw a damper.

"Not so simple, her Cultivation Level is such that the Corpse Chasing Sect might not be able to hold her, and if she escapes from their custody, that’d be problematic."

"I won’t run, I promise I won’t run!" The Drought Demon quickly said, seeing Lu Yang hadn’t sheathed the Green Peak Sword yet and revealed her vulnerability outright.

"There’s a magic artifact called the Mountain Suppressing Seal; with it, I can’t escape!"

"Is that true? Where is the Mountain Suppressing Seal then?" Lu Yang was skeptical.

"I can sense that the Mountain Suppressing Seal that originally sealed me has been taken away; it went in that direction!" the Drought Demon pointed.

Following her direction, Lu Yang and his companion checked the surroundings and recalled the map, "That direction, isn’t that Guyuan County?"

Chapter 1221: Chapter 1220: Valued by Ineffable Officials

Lu Baqian held a Peach Wood Sword, surrounded by numerous magic artifacts enshrouded in a thick fog, all designed to combat zombies.

Magic artifacts floated nearby for easy activation, and the thick fog helped conceal their forms from the Drought Demon.

During his flight here, Lu Baqian thought through many strategies, determined to restrain the Drought Demon here and prevent it from slaughtering the innocent!

Using his compass, he arrived at the cemetery on the outskirts of Quyi County, only to find empty coffins before him.

"Damn, I’m too late, it has escaped!" Lu Baqian’s face looked particularly unpleasant; with the Drought Demon free, endless troubles would follow.

After a careful observation, Lu Baqian was puzzled, "But the emergence of a Drought Demon scorches the earth for thousands of miles, so why does this place still have vitality?"

Logically, after a Drought Demon emerges, it would unconsciously release its domain, strip vitality, and turn the area into a dead land.

"And isn’t this Chaotic Tomb Ridge, why is there no Yin Energy at all? Was it absorbed by the Drought Demon?"

...

"Control the domain a bit, release just a hint of Death Qi and see," Constable Meng said unapologetically.

A person has to bow under the eaves, if she dared release Death Qi, these two Tribulation Crossing Great Powers would respond with Yang Qi and Sword Qi.

"Is it this direction?"

"Yes, we are very close to the Mountain Seal now."

...

"Lord Zhang, congratulations are in order, soon you’ll be promoted to the County Magistrate of Zhongshan County."

Lord Zhang blew away the steam from his teacup casually and asked indifferently, "Wangzhi, seeking me out so late, it must be about more than just this, right?"

"Nothing much else, just that I happened upon a treasure, quite delighted, and thought to share the appreciation with Lord Zhang."

"What kind of treasure?"

Wangzhi took out a Big Seal wrapped in red cloth from his bosom and pushed it in front of Lord Zhang.

Lord Zhang picked up the Big Seal and read the two big characters on the bottom: "Mountain Suppressing?"

"This seal is truly remarkable, look at this craftsmanship, these patterns, surely made using the long-lost Ninety-nine Stages of Refining Technique!"

"Absolutely, the pattern even hides the words ’Wang An’, a Divine Craftsman’s signature, absolutely genuine, definitely a work of the Divine Craftsman Wang Family!"

"However, for nearly a thousand years, the Divine Craftsman Wang Family hasn’t produced any notable figures, heavily declined, the artifacts passed down are decent but far from their peak works."

"Your Lordship has insight, according to my research, this Mountain Seal is indeed the peak work of the Divine Craftsman Wang Family."

Hearing ’Mountain Seal’, Lord Zhang became even more enamored with the Big Seal: "Indeed, this is the Mountain Seal, known for its power to suppress mountains and evil."

Seeing Lord Zhang’s reaction, Wangzhi knew the matter was settled.

Lord Zhang did not care for Spirit Stones or magic artifacts, only showing interest in Feng Shui, evident from the arrangement of his house.

This had been specially arranged by the people from the Heavenly Strategy Sect, facing south with its back against the mountain rocks, harnessing the Spiritual Energy of the mountains and rivers, and capturing the essence of the sun and the moon. The front of the house was open, and from a distance, one could see the water in the courtyard pond, signifying the gathering and retaining of wind and Qi.

Not to mention the relationships the Heavenly Strategy Sect’s people had used, or how many Spirit Stones they had spent, just take these mountain rocks and pond water—though seemingly ordinary, the mountain rocks were actually brought back from the mountains of the Demon Territory, and the water of the pond was melted from the Extreme Northern Lands.

He had discovered that the people from the Heavenly Strategy Sect had said that to achieve the best Feng Shui layout, it was ideal to use a Mountain Suppressing Seal with the power to suppress evil as a magic artifact.

Ordinary magic artifacts couldn’t catch the eye of Lord Zhang, only the best would be used.

He happened to find a record in ancient tomes, dating back five hundred years, where tomb raiders found a hidden tomb beneath the cemetery in the neighboring county. On the coffin, there was a Mountain Seal left; just as he thought to retrieve the Seal, dark clouds formed above the coffin and lightning struck out of nowhere, hitting the coffin and scaring away the tomb raiders.

Lord Zhang laughed heartily, "The people from the Heavenly Strategy Sect really are as prescient as gods, they said it would surely catch the attention of an incredibly prestigious official, eliminating any worries about my career from then on!"

Having thought that it would take ten or twenty years to be promoted to County Magistrate, now being able to advance ahead of time, he probably had already caught the eye of that incredibly prestigious official.

"Originally, I was hesitating whether to recommend you or Dinghai for the position of County Magistrate after I leave, but now it seems Dinghai, though capable, is straightforward and lacks adaptability. Promoting him might hurt him. Wangzhi, you are cunning and perceptive, so you should climb higher."

"Wangzhi thanks Lord Zhang for his recognition of my merits!"

Just as Wangzhi prepared to take his leave, suddenly three figures appeared in the room, two men and one woman.

Lu Yang drew his sword and aimed it at the two people, "Put your hands on the table and don’t move. We are constables from Quyi County, we’ve been watching you for a long time. The bribery you’re involved in has already been recorded by the Recording Orb; you’re under arrest!"

Initially, hearing that these two were just constables, Lord Zhang was unconcerned, but when he heard Lu Yang mentioning the Recording Orb, his expression drastically changed, for it could be used as leverage against him!

"You dare!"

Lord Zhang’s shadow split into two shadow wolves, which bit at the constables’ shadows—an extremely rare Shadow Divine Ability, unpreventable.

"Don’t think about harming anyone!"

The female Dry Corpse immediately stepped in front of the two men, stomping on one of the shadow wolves, and since Lord Zhang was connected to the shadow wolf, he felt as if his chest was being crushed, making it hard for him to breathe.

The female Dry Corpse excitedly turned to Lu Yang, "Sirs, does this count as a merit for me?"

"Who are you people to dare arrest me!"

Meng Jingzhou rolled his eyes, annoyed, and slapped Lord Zhang’s old face, "If you’re deaf, how can you still be a County Magistrate? Didn’t we just say, we are constables from Quyi County."

"I’ll have you know, I’ve already been noticed by that prestigious official, and no longer worry about my career path. My promotion to County Magistrate this time was that official’s doing, if you provoke me, you are opposing that official!"

"What a mess."

...

Early in the morning, Lu Yang and his companion originally wanted to wake Man Gu, but hearing the snoring sound coming from the room—Man Gu was sleeping soundly—it seemed inhumane to wake him, so they left a note overturned at the room’s doorway.

After a while, the secretary, carrying an official decree, also placed it at the doorstep of Man Gu’s room.

Rubbing his eyes, Man Gu opened the room door and saw two papers on the chair by the door, yawning as he picked them up to read.

"The decree states that the position of County Magistrate has been finalized and is assigned to Zhang Tongheng of Guyuan County."

"From Senior Brother, let me see, they caught a tomb raider last night, also stumbled upon the disposing process, the matter was urgent, they’ve already arrested the person, asking me to issue an arrest warrant now. The arrest warrant’s content is all prepared, just missing my signature?"

Man Gu unfolded the arrest warrant left by Lu Yang and his companion.

"Strange, how is this person also named Zhang Tongheng?"

Chapter 1222: Chapter 1221: The County Magistrate Position is Vacant Again

"How is this Mountain Suppressing Seal used?" Lu Yang weighed the Seal in his hand and asked the Dry Corpse.

"There’s a corresponding mantra; as long as you know the mantra, you can control me..." The Dry Corpse didn’t dare to play tricks and truthfully recited the mantra.

Lu Yang read it once, and when he had recited half of it, he saw the Dry Corpse painfully clutching her head.

"Can you two believe me now?" After finishing the incantation, the Dry Corpse asked cautiously. She still couldn’t understand why her Human Tribulation was so powerful.

Worried that the Dry Corpse was acting, Lu Yang silently recited the mantra in his mind again. The Dry Corpse reacted just the same, and only then did Lu Yang believe her words.

"So, you’re saying anyone who knows the mantra and holds the Mountain Suppressing Seal can control you?"

"Holding the Mountain Suppressing Seal and reciting the mantra can only give me a headache and cannot truly control me. To really control me, you need to drop blood to recognize the master and make a contract with the Seal."

Lu Yang and his companion nodded; it didn’t sound like a lie.

"Let’s go, let’s take her to the Corpse Chasing Sect."

"Why hasn’t the Sect Leader returned?" Zhao Po anxiously waited at the entrance of the Corpse Chasing Sect.

Three specks rapidly moved across the sky, catching Zhao Po’s attention.

Back then, Old Meng and he were both at the Golden Core Stage. So many years had flashed by.

He hasn’t come back all night. Please, Senior Brothers, go help!" Zhao Po hastily spoke. Now was not the time for reminiscing.

The Dry Corpse panicked upon hearing this: "Don’t spout nonsense, the Drought Demon is perfectly safe!"

She had to rush; to save her life, she had given up all the means to control herself. If this youngster blabbed more, causing the two esteemed ones to form a bad impression of her, how could she survive?

"How could I talk nonsense about such a serious matter? I stayed up all night looking through ancient texts and sought advice from every person I could find!"

Zhao Po finally noticed that although the Dry Corpse’s clothes were tattered, they were indeed the garments of their Corpse Chasing Sect.

"You, you are that Drought Demon?!"

Zhao Po’s eyes widened as he looked at Lu Yang and the other man, seeking a reasonable explanation.

Lu Yang scratched his head, somewhat vexed. This matter seemed pretty straightforward; there wasn’t much to explain: "Uh, it’s just that we happened to encounter her. Seeing that she was wearing the clothes of the Corpse Chasing Sect, we thought we should bring her to you for handling."

"We can’t handle her at all," Zhao Po said quickly. Even the Sect Leader, the first under the Transcendance Tribulation Stage, had less than a thirty percent chance of victory against the Dry Corpse. If it caused chaos in their custody, what could they do?

"No need to worry about that; we have the Mountain Suppressing Seal." Lu Yang explained how to use the Seal, and Zhao Po finally breathed a sigh of relief.

"Then when the Sect Leader returns, shall we have the Sect Leader hold the Seal?"

"We both have business to attend to, so why don’t you take the Seal and drop blood to recognize mastery? After all, you’re at the Void Refinement Stage and lacking life-saving methods."

Zhao Po could not win against Lu Yang and reluctantly accepted the Dry Corpse, taking the Seal and performing the blood rituals to recognize mastery.

To make Lu Yang and his companion feel at ease, the Dry Corpse even sweetly called out "Master."

In high-level cultivator combat, a single oversight could lead to total defeat!

The female Dry Corpse was even more excited than Lu Baqian. Right, this is the Human Tribulation I should be facing.

Chapter 1223: Chapter 1222: The Consequences of Eavesdropping

"Lord Governor Zhou Hai has taken up his post and requires all county magistrates in Zhongshan County to attend a meeting tomorrow?" Man Gu, who had been busy all day and had just gotten off work, received the notice.

He was currently dealing with the affairs of both the previous and the one before that governor and had been very busy the past few days.

Fortunately, with the help of two senior brothers here, he was able to leave work on time.

"Finally, a new governor has arrived," Man Gu sighed. It hadn’t been easy with two changes of governors in just a few days.

After thinking it through, Man Gu informed Lu Yang and the other about the meeting and hoped they could join him.

Typically, whenever a county magistrate stepped out, they would bring along attendants or government officials to take care of and protect the magistrate.

"Joining the meeting as well? Indeed, Junior Brother Man, you’re currently in the Void Refinement Stage. It’s alright within our local area, but outside the county town, you might encounter dangers."

This meant that Lu Yang and the other would be busy hunting for female ghosts on their night shifts and wouldn’t rest even after the night shift ended, as they would accompany Man Gu to the meeting the following day.

Although those in the Transcendance Tribulation Stage wouldn’t feel tired even without rest for a hundred and eighty days, Man Gu was still very touched.

...

In Quyi County, where governance flowed smoothly, the two newly appointed constables encountered nothing throughout their night shift and afterwards, accompanied Man Gu to Zhongshan County.

A few days ago, Lu Yang and his companion had come to Zhongshan County to resolve issues with the Hundred Sword Alliance, but it had been night then, and the streets were empty and silent.

Arriving in Zhongshan County during the day, it was bustling, and although Quyi County had thrived under Man Gu’s governance over the past years, it still couldn’t compare to Zhongshan County.

At the entrance of the Governor Mansion, they encountered several county magistrates who were arriving for the meeting. Some were in sedans, others in horse carriages, all looking quite spectacular. Only Man Gu and his companions were walking.

Despite Man Gu having walked here, no county magistrate dared to underestimate him. As they descended from their sedans or carriages, they all greeted Man Gu with smiling faces.

Capturing two governors within three days, with the second governor being imprisoned on the day he assumed office—such a feat was indeed terrifying.

"Lord Man, it’s been a while and you still look as distinguished as ever."

Upon hearing this, the other county magistrates hurriedly entered the Governor Mansion, hoping not to ’exchange ideas’ further, lest trouble arises from nowhere.

Man Gu scratched his head, puzzled—he had delivered the responses just as the secretary had instructed, so why were their reactions different from what the secretary said?

"Never mind, let’s go in." Man Gu was always broad-minded; not understanding something wasn’t worth overthinking and straining his brain.

Upon entering the Governor’s Mansion, Man Gu went into the council hall, while Lu Yang and the other, as attendants, could only stand guard outside.

Along with Lu Yang and his companion outside, there were other attendants and government officials brought by the other county magistrates, so they were not lonely.

"That’s quite supportive of you two senior brothers. Who knows how long this new governor’s meeting will last. Perhaps you two seniors can take a stroll around the county."

Lu Yang waved his hand and laughed, "No need, no need. We came specifically to protect you; we can’t leave."

"Lord Man, thank you."

"I am Yang Dinghai, the newly appointed county magistrate of Guyuan County."

Both I and Liu Wangzhi had a chance to become the county magistrate. However, Liu Wangzhi was adept at ingratiating himself with Zhang Tongheng, and the likelihood of him becoming the county magistrate was higher. The two senior brothers were waiting outside, and he was eager to wrap up the meeting early.

...

A man stood outside the council hall, from his attire, he was clearly the County Magistrate.

County Magistrate Zhou, hearing the murmurs inside the hall, cracked a smile.

While in Wild State, he held the position of Gong Cao, responsible for personnel movement, wielding immense power, and even the County Magistrates were always courteous around him.

His assignment in Zhongshan State as the County Magistrate was merely a formality, a gilding of his resume, until he was eligible for a natural promotion to a higher grade.

His achievements today were inseparable from his cultivation technique.

His cultivation technique was a bit special, akin to the Buddhist telepathy, but not as powerful; it only allowed him to eavesdrop on conversations. Astute by nature, he could decipher relationships from these conversations, sowing discord or thriving on both sides, thus profiting from the situation.

The reason he was late was that he wanted to listen to the county officials’ conversation inside the council hall, as well as the exchanges among the government officials outside, seeking useful intelligence.

"It’s about time to go in," said County Magistrate Zhou with a smile, regretting not having heard the conversation between the two people brought by Man Gu.

County Magistrate Zhou was momentarily puzzled; what had just happened? He felt like he was missing a piece of his memory.

"It’s about time to go in," County Magistrate Zhou said with a smile, regretting not having heard the conversation of the two people brought by Man Gu.

The conversation content brought by Man Gu entered his ears.

On his first day in office, County Magistrate Zhou was meant to show his authority, but instead, he ended up standing outside the council hall, punished for nearly three hours.

Chapter 1224: Chapter 123 Barely Retained the Title of Number One Below the Transcendance Tribulation Stage

The constables outside the meeting hall all witnessed County Magistrate Zhou being made to stand at the door for over two hours, and they transmitted messages to their respective County Magistrates, who began to look at Zhou with increasingly bemused eyes.

Is this some strange kind of hobby?

But even if he liked standing at the door, he couldn’t expect them to wait from noon until now.

Even Zhou, who had exceptional interpersonal skills and a top-notch mental resilience, felt embarrassed in this situation.

Zhou’s face changed color repeatedly. Although he was at fault, being persuaded by Man Gu in just a few words not to hold the meeting was a blow to his dignity.

Man Gu was puzzled, "But wasn’t it you who wasted our time by standing at the door and not coming in?"

Faced with the truth, Zhou had no defense against Man Gu and ordered, "We must have the meeting today!"

"Oh," Man Gu sat down obediently.

Seeing Man Gu’s indifferent attitude, Zhou’s blood pressure rose; he had never encountered such a person in his official career!

He made an effort to adjust his mentality and chaired the meeting.

In reality, it was just a simple introductory meeting. After all, he was new to the job and unfamiliar with the place; he couldn’t rashly decide the development direction of Zhongshan County.

At the end of the meeting, Zhou asked, "Does anyone else have something to say?"

No one responded.

Zhou scanned the room and fixed his gaze on Man Gu, who seemed eager to leave, "Lord Man, do you have anything to say?"

Man Gu shook his head, remembering the notes the secretary had written, "No."

Seeing that Man Gu was somewhat sensible and understood the rules of bureaucracy, Zhou’s tone softened a bit, "Lord Man, don’t be constrained. Here, you can speak freely."

This was the explanation the secretary had given Man Gu about when a superior says to speak but not really to speak—all direct quotes.

Zhou stared at Man Gu intently, wishing he could swallow him whole.

It seemed that Man Gu had his eye on the position of County Magistrate, having captured the Governor twice already, but he didn’t expect himself to become the Magistrate, harboring resentment and repeatedly embarrassing him during the meeting.

Through clenched teeth, Zhou managed to utter, "...Meeting adjourned."
